電影專刊

明星們的秋波 284

— 仲琴

一個人的性格行爲在兩隻眼睛裏可以猜到心窩裏去，如果和藹的性格，眼中終帶些慈祥氣昧，如果惡毒的性格眼中就現出兇光來了，同時女子的明眸能表現充分的美，所謂秋波一轉，足以消魂，我們如果拿電影明星的眼睛揣摩一下，那麽明星們某一種作風都可以在她的明眸中尋出來，也是怪有趣的事。瓊克勞馥是出名的大眼姐，她的眼睛的大，當然無用說得了，瓊克勞馥的大眼，平心而論起來，實在稍微妨礙她面部的美，但是她的大眼十足的神氣，她就因爲這對大眼睛而達到神氣活現的作風。在大飯店和雨二片中她的精彩就在兩隻大眼睛上，是無可諱言的。

和瓊克勞馥相反的是瑙瑪希拉，瑙瑪希拉的眼睛特别小，她的眸大並且常揷在上面眼脣下，所以一望，就知道是個細心而拘謹的閨女派調，令人起威敬之感，她的作風都在中間顯露無遺了。

葛萊泰嘉寶的眼睛很深刻悲切，她演到慘淡頑艶處都能給人表不少的同情，她的婉轉的秋波，像一池春水，能使人陶醉而沈溺其中。

熱女郎克萊拉寳的眼中現出充分的熱，而帶有剛强不覊的氣味，她的眼睛上眼脣和眉毛相距極近，這是剛强不覊的特徵。

珍　蓋諒的眼波中現着十分的温柔和悅，她的作風嬌小玲瓏，無限的可愛，盡在温柔之中。

瑪琳黛德麗的眼波尖銳透明，所以她的作風趨向於神妙莫測，須背後推測，尋弦外之音的。

妲露拉朋克海的眼波風騷動人，她的作風能眩目奪魂，令人心醉。

康絲登裴納的眼波現着拙强的態度，所以她處處描寫不能屈辱的剛毅作風。

已說了不少，還有許多可以自已揣摩，在眼睛上可以猜測内心，决不會猜測錯了的。

影片談評

評﹁偷情記﹂LoveOnTheSpot 285

— 燕南

昨天看了卡爾登所映的﹁偷情記﹂，忽然想到兩個月以前看的﹁性愛的俘虜﹂。眞的，這張﹁偷情記﹂雖然是根據小說改編的，但和﹁性愛的俘虜﹂却有異曲同工之妙而且在故事，技藝各方面，也有些相同。

本事是這樣的：在一個旅館裏，住了一位少年，他是個妙手空空的穿窬者。在三次失竊以後，偵探雖然猜疑到他，但是一些拿不着憑據。那時另一個女郎和她的父親，也住在這旅館裏。父女們都是戴了紳士假面具的騙子。但是女郎愛上了這少年，她坦白的說明她以後要改過了。少年也受了感動，盡還贓物，兩人一同走向正當之路。

演員是我們很生疏的。飾竊賊的少年是瑞却杜門RickadDolman，他表現出英國靑年們所有的態度。面部自然的表情，載歌載舞，煞是討人喜歡。也許可以認爲他有看佛萊的動人吧？他的活潑詼諧，使人極端滿意。尤其是他極切合於劇中人。飾女郎的是柔絲瑪瑞愛姆RosemaryAmes大致還好。她很美麗，只是表情差了些。唱的曲子很不錯。她的父親是由阿伯瑞馬特Ａnbreymather飾的，專以說白討俏，可以呌人發笑。

被竊的老嫗海綸　和HelenFerrers，在配角中佔了極重要的地位。她所表演的，刻骨形容着一般自傲的貴族式夫人，很爲中肯。至於那小孩子約翰莘格JohnSinger是很可造就的，在這片子裏，已現出了極大的表演天才。

對白並不太多，如果你能每一句都

大鼻嘲 286

— 炳

在好萊塢甚之小孩子你對他說大鼻子先生時，没有不知道是指點傑美社倫的傑美的名聲，全靠他的鼻子生出來的，他旣有這樣一隻令人稱羡的大鼻子，於是有許多人造了一隻歌謠來嘲笑他，大意是：

落杉磯姐兒們面上的香粉，在皮佛萊的山頂上可以聞得到；到了夏天，眞可當作一把遮陽傘，使三個小孩子可以躱在底下乘凉；但是裏面的風太熱了，不如到海濱去乘凉吧！

呀丨可氣我爲什麽不也生這麽一個東西，好在好萊塢賺大錢呢？

明白，那末你可以找到無數的幽默材料，使你發笑。

至於導演，只能算中等以上。攝影上，角度地位不錯。光線也可以看。衣飾和佈景，一望而知牠是英國片子，美麗之中，很帶了高貴的大陸色彩。當然，每一個演員的態度，也都有關係的。剪接一切還不錯。至於藉以號召的大游泳，在水池裏的女郎們，和鏡頭的攝下，雖然抄舞台團體舞的故技，但仍不失其新穎，只可惜太短而變化太少。四隻曲子，都是﹁爵士歌﹂ＴazzSongs，可以說一個﹁好﹂字。

在一切歌舞片中，配樂常常是應當很好的。但是道一張片子的音樂很平常，鼓不起人的興奮。

劇義方面，很是淺薄的，但還有些諷剌和調笑意味。（例如在六十歲老翁的老袋中，搜出乂史）

總之，這張片子，可以使你有快感，可以使你發笑。雖然，牠不能呌你永久記着牠。

這是好萊塢一生長在中國的女明星，名字呌霞麗馬立薩，在本刊三月六日思瀛君的﹁一位無國籍的女子﹂中已介紹過。

快訊一束 287

— 介

天一公司新片﹁生機﹂現已攝製過半，由陳玉梅袁美雲主演。前傳内有胡姗，但早已改去矣。

南方公司所製﹁白金龍﹂一片。因係粤劇改編，故其中三分之二爲粤語對白。餘則上海語及國語兼有之。該片中除三位演員爲南方公司之人外，餘則爲天一公司之全數班底云。

蓋呌天在齊天舞臺停鑼後，積極從事影業，如平劇名人苑月樓等均被邀參加。前定名稱﹁呌天影片公司﹂，現用股東制，改爲﹁乾坤影片公司﹂。唯秘密進行，故知之者絶少。

最近聯華公司各片廠，積極開攝各種短片，内以新聞滑稽二種居多。已攝成者，有五套，不久將公映。此殆爲國片前途之好現象云。

以化裝著名之馬徐維邦，五年前曾被推爲﹁東方千面人﹂，聞有加入天一公司之訊，但尚未接洽妥協云。

影戲院的怪現狀 288

— 趙鵬

影戲院是高尚娱樂的塲所，到影戲院去是鑒賞銀幕上表演的優劣，可是有一般顧客們，他們的目的，並不是在銀幕上的表演，却是在鑒賞，戲院裏的漂亮女子的臉兒，和服裝。

有許多的女性往往穿得花枝招展，灑得香噴噴，在影戲院故意地的賣弄風騷，博得異性的埀靑，向男子眉來目去的，表演銀幕上的戀愛工作起來，高尚的影戲院，竟作了公開戀愛的介紹所？有許多影戲院裏的音樂亦是花樣百出，奏的音樂和片裏的意思没全不同，一般粗心的顧客們，只要奏的繼續不斷就算了，要是稍爲停止片刻，就要吵閙起來，一面奏的時候常常把脚蹬個不定，吵的人頭痛。

﹁武松﹂將在蘇州拍外景 289

— 松夫

呌天影片公司的第一部影片武松﹂，已經籌備了好久。蓋呌天想所這許的外景在杭州拍攝。可是他近來因爲在蘇州另有事務，不能脫身，所以决定在蘇州拍攝。大約在一個月可以拍完云。

零零碎碎 290

— 周敬之

張慧冲赴東北冒險攝來的﹁熱河血涙﹂，業已全部修剪竣事，一度在北京試映，成績尚佳，擬不日公映於北京大戲院云。明星公司改變作風的﹁脂粉市塲，連日正趕拍完竣，不日將在卡爾登公映。

﹁航空救國﹂迷漫聲裏，電影界自不願從人，聯華當局正着手游藝會募捐的進行。這次演出的劇本人員，有金燄，阮玲玉，鄭君里，陳燕燕諸大明星，同時聯華基木人員均可見面。并聞劇名暫定﹁抗爭﹂，爲金燄所寫。

電影小說賽珍會StateFair（四） 291

— 蕙君

﹁很抱歉我以爲你嚇，暈了才抱你的﹂！他說着瑪姬已漲紅了臉﹁我從没有嚇暈過，她辨别。

少年似乎漸漸對她發生好感。﹁婦女誰都膽小，我料你見着老鼠也怕吧﹂！他調侃她。

﹁我什麽也不怕！惱恨的燄芒在她眼中放射。

﹁再坐一次﹂？少年提議，當飛車到站頭停下。

﹁死也不坐了﹂！她喘息說，可是見他譏　的神情，她躊躇，忘懷了車子已將開行。

迅雷地，飛車又依軌疾馳，他的手臂又擁住她，而她，無從抵拒地，閉住眼睛，把粉類依偎在他的肩。

﹁開心嗎﹂！他問。瑪姬含羞地點頭，當他扶着她下車走過隧道到地面時，

﹁你呌什麽名字？他告訴她自己的名字不！不要說讓我猜。海倫······不是丨裴蒂······不是！瑪姬······是了！瑪姬﹂。她認可的心緒呌做潘脫，以及職業是新聞記者之後。他們淡着，笑着，一起去喝汽水，一起去坐飛船，瑪姬眞快活極了。啊，賽珍會是多麽有意趣　她幸虧得來了！她覺得今夜才是生平最眞實最可愛的夜······但如今又過去了丨怪快的過度了！可是，瞧潘脫懇切，愛慕的態度，她知道還有丨明天！

今夜，惠恩，也感到神秘的新鮮。他站近那大看裏，守着，等着他知道這兒是天空表演的塲合。鼓聲突然咚咚他震響，塲主人在宣佈說；﹁請看霍根女士表演丨她是世界第一爲三上吊藝員﹂！在惠恩的懷疑的眼前，一個纖細前身段，穿着門　的緊身衣的少女奔出來鞠了躬，爬上繩子。啊，這竟是愛蜜蘭！

他的嘴半張着，簡直不敢喘息，守到表演終了。她下了繩，似乎在園聚着的觀衆招中尋他，於是，向着他的方向，擲了一個空吻。一聲長長的嘆息從他的嘴唇發出，終究，他决意走向寫着﹁閑人莫入﹂的後臺門。在那兒，他潤乾濕他的乾的嘴唇，守候着，直至愛蜜蘭，穿了便裝，欣愉地走出來歡迎他。（未完）

1933.04.03

The Battle of Shimen Village Slightly Abates Yesterday 1

The Shuizhaiyu Position Has Been Abandoned

The Shihe Position is Isolated

Enemy Disguised Units Plan to Disrupt Qindao

Enemy Aircraft Bomb Haiyang and Other Places

(Luanzhou) There were no major battles in the Shimen Village area on the morning of the 2nd. The enemy still seemed to be advancing. Cavalry Wang Shibu's troops crossed the Great Wall coal mine railway line and contacted the enemy. (2nd Dispatch) (Luanzhou) The main force of our army's front line defended the northeast area of □□□ on the 2nd. Cavalry was between □□□□, confronting the enemy. After 10 o'clock, sandstorms raged, and the battlefield was shrouded in sand. The weather turned cold. There were no fierce battles on the front line all day, only occasional cavalry engagements. No enemy aircraft were spotted in the afternoon. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) The enemy Iwata Detachment invaded our Shimen Village position last night. There were no fierce battles there this morning. Five Japanese planes flew over our second line of defense and dropped more than ten bombs. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) After the Japanese army at Jiukou issued a general attack order early on the 31st, the Japanese army, in a joint land and air operation, fiercely attacked Shimen Village. The Japanese army and most of the puppet troops, after reaching Shahe Village, used all their strength to advance towards Shimen, with the cover of aircraft and heavy artillery. A certain regiment of our army guarded Liangjia Mountain, exchanging fire with the enemy. At 2 p.m. on the 1st, the enemy used eighteen aircraft to bomb Shimen Village. Our army remained in the trenches, unmoved. On the evening of the 1st, under orders from the forward headquarters, they gathered forces at Houzhuang and Haiyang Town, southwest of Shimen, to implement an ambush plan. On the evening of the 1st, the Japanese army sneaked into Shimen, and was fiercely attacked by our left and right flanks. The Japanese army did not dare to advance rashly. After 8 a.m. this morning, a large number of Japanese planes reconnoitered and bombed various places in Haiyang Town, including the Nan Dasi of the garrison camp. There were fierce clashes at the front. The Japanese army planned to directly approach Changli from Shimen Village. We have taken strict precautions. This morning, Japanese armored vehicles on the Shihe front drove to the Shihe Railway Bridge, repaired the bridge, and fired artillery at both sides of the railway. (2nd Dispatch at Noon)

(Beiping) There are no major battles in the Shimen Village area today. Only a certain cavalry division of our army had slight contact with the enemy in the Great Wall area, and was then repelled by our forces. Five enemy aircraft flew to our army's second line of defense this afternoon, dropped more than ten bombs, and fled. We suffered no major losses. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Since yesterday, the enemy has launched fierce attacks on our Shimen Village position with a combined force of infantry, cavalry, and artillery. The fighting was fierce last night. It is reported that our army's position in that area has been newly deployed. Details are unknown. (2nd Dispatch)

Tianjin military telephone still connected to Haiyang Town at noon on the 2nd. There was a change in our Shimen Village position on the evening of the 1st. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) The battle of Shimen Village is extremely fierce. Enemy aircraft dropped countless bombs on the 1st. Our army engaged in hand-to-hand combat with the enemy four or five times. Casualties are countless. The situation is extremely tragic. This morning, fourteen enemy aircraft flew to Shimen again, circling and bombing, which is rare in previous battles. The First Detachment of puppet troops, about a thousand strong, was also discovered on the left flank □□□, launching a fierce attack on us. The situation is very critical. Our army's reserve team has gone to meet them. Until the morning of the 2nd, fighting was still fierce. The Beining train still sold tickets to Qindao on the morning of the 2nd, but there were few passengers. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) The artillery battle at Shimen Village intensified on the evening of the 1st. The enemy's attack became more fierce at midnight, and they seemed to be continuing to advance. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) After Shuizhaiyu was broken through by the enemy, the Shihe position was isolated. The enemy protruding from Yucheng also dispatched armored troops, firing artillery near the Shihe Bridge to threaten us. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) The enemy's armored train on the Shihe front line is unusually active on the east bank, firing artillery at the west bank from time to time, seemingly attempting to charge our defense line. Our army is also on strict alert. The situation on the Shihe line is tense. (2nd Dispatch)

(Luanzhou) According to a telegram from the front, fierce fighting continued in the Shimen Village area all day. After dusk, it entered a state of confrontation. Commander Yao Dongfan, due to heavy casualties in his troops, is personally actively gathering and replenishing ammunition in a certain area, waiting for a decisive battle with the enemy. The Shihe line has been moved to a certain major defense line in □□ due to changes in the situation. The enemy is also reorganizing and reinforcing troops, and there will continue to be major battles. (2nd Dispatch)

(Luanzhou) He Zhuguo and He Jinghua took a special train to the front line in the evening to inspect and provide guidance. (2nd Dispatch)

(Luanzhou) The enemy plans to first disrupt Qinhuangdao with disguised units. The enemy's marines will take the opportunity to coordinate with the Kwantung Army or puppet troops to drive out the Chinese army, occupy Qinbu, and block the island. According to reports from the front, the enemy has sent more than a hundred puppet soldiers led by Ding Qiang, disguised in civilian clothes, to sneak into Qinbu and carry out secret activities, creating incidents within days. More than thirty people were captured by our forces on the 2nd. We have notified the British and American garrisons and the Kailuan authorities to pay attention. The Liu camp in Qinbu is under strict guard. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) There is one Japanese aircraft carrier, one cruiser, two destroyers, and three torpedo boats anchored off the coast of Qindao. There are a total of four or five cruisers, destroyers, torpedo boats, and other ships off the coast of Shanhaiguan and Beidaihe, patrolling the sea from time to time. (2nd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Luanzhou reports that at around 6 a.m. on the 1st, more than a dozen enemy planes fiercely bombed the Shimen Village area. Our army was hidden and unmoved. At the same time, three enemy planes over Haiyang Town dropped bombs on our forward headquarters, causing the public to flee west, resulting in a chaotic market. The telephone lines connecting the village to Huangdao were destroyed by the bombing, and repaired on the evening of the 1st. At 10 a.m. on the 1st, more than a thousand enemy soldiers on the Shimen Village front launched a combined infantry, artillery, and air attack on our troops. Our troops calmly responded. At the same time, more than a thousand enemy soldiers on the right flank of Shimen attacked our Shuizhaiyu via Pan Taoyu and Yashui River, attempting to attack our Haiyang Town. Our Nanlinzi reserve team rushed to meet them. The battle continued until noon, when our line at Shuizhaiyu was broken through by the enemy. We immediately mobilized reinforcements for a counterattack, charging and engaging in hand-to-hand combat, gaining and losing ground repeatedly. The enemy was unable to succeed. At 2 p.m., the enemy increased their force by more than two thousand infantry and cavalry, advancing towards us. At the same time, the enemy aircraft carrier in Qinhuangdao dispatched more than twenty planes, concentrating their bombing on our positions, as dense as falling hail, for as long as two hours. Our army was surrounded by land and air. The villages along Shuizhaiyu and the Gaobeishang position to the south were almost completely destroyed. Our casualties were more than half, leading to the loss of the Shuizhaiyu position. The Shihe position was prominent and isolated. On the south bank, two hundred enemy sailors landed at Xielingkou at noon on the 1st and began operations. The enemy in Shanhaiguan also dispatched armored vehicles, firing artillery at the Shihe Bridge to threaten us. Our □□□ commander has arrived at the front line to supervise the battle. On the morning of the 2nd, more than a dozen enemy planes bombed Haiyang Town and Shimen Village. Shimen Village is under extreme enemy pressure. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) The main force of the enemy fiercely attacking our Shahe Shimen Village is the Matsumoto unit of the 14th Division, newly transferred by the Japanese from Shenyang and Tongliao to Shanhaiguan. The infantry, cavalry, and artillery units number more than seven thousand, accompanied by more than thirty tanks and more than twenty aircraft, launching a large-scale attack. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Linyu reports by telephone that the enemy continued to fiercely attack our Shimen Village position last night and this morning, dividing their forces into three routes. One unit, a combined infantry and cavalry force of about a thousand, attacked the left flank of Liangjia Mountain and Shimen Village from Pantouyu and Shangdiaobuluo and other places. Another route, consisting of various infantry and cavalry units and rebel troops, numbering over two thousand, attacked the front of Shimen Village and Shuizhaiyu. Another route, mostly cavalry, attacked Yangzhuang on the right flank of Shimen Village from Dingjiayu. The enemy used heavy artillery and large squadrons of aircraft to cover their troops, attacking our army. Fighting raged all day, with heavy casualties on both sides. The fighting at Shuiyu Village on the front of Shimen Village was the fiercest. Our army is mobilizing reserve teams to launch a counterattack against the enemy. As of this morning, fighting was still raging near Wanmen Village. (2nd Dispatch)

(Luanzhou) After the breakthrough at Shuizhaiyu caused our reinforcement Jia camp to fail in achieving a miraculous victory, the □ regiments and □□ battalions guarding Yashuiyu, Chenzhuang, and Liangjia Mountain were surrounded by the superior enemy by morning. The battle was tragic, with many casualties, especially in the Jiang camp. However, they still gathered their remaining courage, broke out of the encirclement, waved their swords and slashed, killing many enemies. The fighting was also fierce on the right flank □ camp. The □ company of the □ regiment of the cavalry □ division in the Yashui River Shuizhaiyu area is still engaged in fierce fighting with the enemy. Until after 5 o'clock, the fierce sound of gunfire at Shimen Village shook the mountains and valleys. The telephone line to Shimen Village was cut off after 3 o'clock. Our army is engaged in hand-to-hand combat. At 4 o'clock in Haiyang Town, three enemy aircraft came again to bomb and destroy heavily. An enemy plane also flew to Shenhepu, west of Haiyang, for reconnaissance. (1st Dispatch)

After our army's counterattack at Linyu failed yesterday, by about 10 a.m. today, the enemy launched a fierce attack on our Shimen Village position near the Yashui River with more than three thousand new-style troops via Pantao Yu, and used fourteen aircraft to take turns bombing repeatedly, bombing our □ regiment's □ battalion, which rushed to aid, and was again surrounded by the enemy. At this time, multiple aircraft from the enemy's aircraft carrier also came to bomb. By about 2 p.m., the entire position had been almost leveled and destroyed. As of the time of the telegram, fighting was still raging. According to captured enemy wounded, the Shimen Village area is defended by the puppet 2nd Garrison Army, consisting of three brigades and six regiments, about six thousand people, dressed the same as the Japanese army, with many Japanese people. The Qiuziyu area is defended by the puppet garrison army's 1st Cavalry Detachment, Ding Qiang's unit and Zhao Lei's 1st Brigade, Miao Zibin's unit, totaling four thousand people, along with four or five hundred Japanese soldiers. (1st Dispatch)

Enemy Ship on Fire off the Coast of Qindao 2

(Beiping) A certain enemy ship anchored near the coast of Qindao caught fire due to an explosion in the ammunition depot. Details are unknown. (2nd Dispatch)

Two Japanese Ships Anchored Outside Dagukou 3

(Beiping) Of the five Japanese ships outside Dagukou, two have sailed away, leaving two still anchored outside the port. (2nd Dispatch)

Seven Japanese Ships Arrive at Xielingkou 4

(Beiping) Seven Japanese ships arrived at Xielingkou today. The Japanese aircraft carrier also sailed from Lushun. A part of our garrison in Qinhuangdao is implementing emergency alert measures from the 1st, and has notified Chilton, the General Manager of the Kailuan Mining Bureau, that if the Japanese army provokes the Chinese army and lands via the Kailuan International Wharf, the Japanese army should bear full responsibility for compensation. He Zhuguo has transferred a certain unit to reinforce the defenses west of the Luan River, which are extremely tight. (2nd Dispatch)

Battle Situation Near Tiemenguan 5

(Beiping) On the 31st, more than a hundred enemy soldiers disrupted the area near Tiemenguan and were repelled by our forces. This morning, the enemy launched a fierce attack on us with mountain and field guns, and it seemed that reinforcements had arrived, preparing to continue attacking us. (2nd Dispatch)

He Zhuguo Cables Ping to Report Military Situation 6

(Beiping) He Zhuguo cabled Ping at noon on the 1st, stating that the enemy attacked our Shahezhai position yesterday, advancing repeatedly despite setbacks. Until 1 p.m., they engaged in hand-to-hand combat with the enemy as many as four or five times. The enemy fired more than five hundred rounds of artillery, and aircraft dropped countless bombs. Both sides suffered heavy casualties. On the Shimen Village □ wing □□□, north of the □□□□□□□□ line, a mixed force of Japanese and puppet troops of about one regiment was also discovered, making contact with the □□□ unit. The Fourth Company of our Shahezhai garrison was almost completely wiped out, etc. (2nd Dispatch)

Enemy Attacks Sun's Army's Defense Area Near Fengning 7

Was Repelled by Sun's Army

The Feng Unit is in Heavy Fighting with the Enemy East of Duolun

Two-Thirds of the Enemy Withdraw from the Gubeikou Area 8

(Beiping) The enemy's Motegi Cavalry Brigade launched a sudden attack on the defense area of Sun Dianying's army in the areas of Guotun, Zhangsanying, and Chuizishan near Fengning at dawn on the 31st. After our Xing Brigade fought bravely and resisted fiercely, the enemy failed to succeed and retreated after 1 p.m. Our soldiers suffered more than a hundred casualties, and the enemy suffered even more deaths and injuries. Currently, there are approximately twenty thousand Japanese and puppet troops concentrated in the Weichang area, including the Motegi Cavalry Brigade, a part of the Matsuda and Takada Infantry Brigades, and approximately seven to eight thousand puppet troops led separately by Mongol Commanders Chai and Li. The enemy dispatches planes to reconnoiter the rear of our positions every day, seemingly planning to force our army to withdraw from Rehe with heavy troops. Our side's morale is high, and we are determined to fight to the death. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Duolun reports that several dozen enemy soldiers and more than seven hundred puppet troops appeared in the Honghuashan area, eighty li east of Duolun, this morning, and were met with a counterattack by Feng Zhanhai's army. As of the time of the telegram, fighting was still raging. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) According to a telephone call from Shixiazhen, as of the 31st to the 1st, artillery fire was still heard fiercely at Gubeikou. It is heard that Tang's unit and Sun's unit in Fengning have jointly launched an attack towards Chahar East, and the battle situation remains unclear. Approximately two-thirds of the Japanese and puppet troops in the Gubeikou area have withdrawn. Approximately five thousand enemy troops stationed in Gubeikou were reinforced from Luanping Plains, and now there are only one thousand and several hundred remaining. When the Japanese troops withdrew, they also fired more than thirty rounds of artillery at our army to prevent our army from counterattacking. The residents of Gubeikou, suffering from excessive oppression by the enemy, eagerly hope that the National Army will take advantage of the enemy's weakness and launch a counterattack on Gubeikou. Several enemy planes arrived in Miyun County on the 31st and dropped four bombs, causing no losses. It has been very peaceful for days. (2nd Dispatch)

Liu Yifei Advances Towards Guyuan 9

(Beiping) Liu Yifei left Zhangjiakou on the morning of the 31st and advanced towards Guyuan. Yesterday, he telegraphed a certain organization in Zhangbei County, reporting his whereabouts and stating that he would lead his troops to resist Japan and maneuver between Duolun and Beiping. Telegraph communications have been disrupted since noon on the 2nd. Telegraph communications have now been restored. (2nd Dispatch)

Sun's Troops' Wounded Soldiers Arrive at Kangzhuang 10

(Beiping) Wounded soldiers from Sun Dianying's unit are currently at the Kangzhuang rear hospital, numbering over a hundred. Another hundred arrived at Kangzhuang today from Zhangjiakou. Another four hundred wounded soldiers will arrive at Zhangjiakou tonight and will be transferred to Kangzhuang tomorrow. (2nd Dispatch)

Japanese Aircraft Bomb Shixiazhen 11

(Beiping) According to a telephone call from Miyun, several Japanese aircraft flew to Shixiazhen at 2 p.m. this afternoon and dropped three bombs. Losses are unknown. The situation in Gubeikou remains calm. (2nd Dispatch)

Deserters North of Xiyuan Have Been Dealt With 12

(Beiping) The Military Affairs Committee received a report that a certain unit of the Northeast Army had fled to a certain village more than ten li north of Xiyuan the day before yesterday. It immediately ordered the Pingjin Garrison Headquarters to dispatch a team to encircle and suppress them last night. The deserters were carrying weapons such as machine guns and grenades. After being surrounded, they immediately resisted arrest and a fierce battle broke out. The situation was thoroughly resolved this morning. As a result, in addition to those who were killed, all the remaining deserters were disarmed and captured, totaling nineteen people. They were sent to Ping this morning. Several soldiers from the garrison unit were also killed or wounded. (2nd Dispatch)

Current Commentary

The Sino-Russian Commercial Treaty and the National Consumer Cooperative 13

Since the economic panic among capitalist countries is becoming more and more profound, the state of capitalism moving from shaking to extinction is becoming more and more obvious. Although academic economists still use superficial theories of prosperity, decline, and perpetual cycles as a means of self-deception, the declining trend of the river flowing downwards cannot be reversed by wishful thinking. All attempts to restore prosperity will only be a flash in the pan and will inevitably become the final struggle. MacDonald failed in the former, how can Hitler be effective in the latter? Hoover's repeated declarations have all become unfulfilled promissory notes, so how can Roosevelt have the ability to reverse the situation and save the dying to fulfill his promises during the election?

At a time when the entire society is gradually moving away from the realm of capitalism and entering a new path of socialism, China, which is only a corner of the world, cannot go against the trend. In this country where national capital is extremely immature, it may be easier to change course because the accumulated difficulties have not yet become overwhelming. For many years, domestic sages have had differing opinions on the steps of social transformation, but have reached a consensus on the direction of the socialist path. Regardless of what method or steps China takes to achieve the goal of socialism, it may be mutually beneficial to establish close ties with the Soviet Union in the economy and create a unified front. The current national crisis has made us realize the extreme mistake of severing relations with the Soviet Union, so reviving Mr. Sun Yat-sen's strategy of alliance with the Soviet Union is in line with the philosophy of "when things are exhausted, there will be change; change will lead to progress."

At a time when the two countries are mutually dispatching envoys and consuls and national exchanges are gradually increasing, the signing of a Sino-Soviet commercial treaty is an important task at hand. Regarding the issue of the commercial treaty, before the most-favored-nation clause is abolished, the contents of commercial treaties signed by our country with various countries may be largely the same, but in essence, they are almost uniform due to the inclusion of the most-favored-nation clause. We cannot hope to find any special significance in the Sino-Soviet commercial treaty. However, the establishment of the so-called Trade Bureau with the Soviet Union, which is associated with the Sino-Soviet commercial treaty, is worth studying.

The general significance of the Trade Bureau with the Soviet Union is that the Soviet Union's foreign trade is entirely state-owned, with unified authority and consistent policies. If we conduct transactions with them separately through private individuals, the resulting competition may prevent us from obtaining favorable terms, and it would be overwhelming for them to deal with us separately. Therefore, a bureau must be established to achieve a one-on-one position in order to achieve direct and fair transactions. However, we believe that the duties of the bureau should go far beyond this. We must further organize the national consumer market in order to build a strong economic united front.

At a time when there is a surplus of all commodities in the world, what capitalist powers covet in our country is this vast consumer market that can absorb their surplus commodities. Therefore, controlling the consumer market is the most effective way to deal with the powers. In recent years, our struggle against Japan has also used economic severance as a weapon, but the shortcoming is that the focus has only been on passive resistance and there has been little active organization. Even the so-called promotion of domestic goods movement, its methods and steps are still too empty and scattered. If we can further pool huge capital to organize a national consumer cooperative, with domestic products as the center and Soviet products to supplement the deficiencies, order a large number of necessities from the Soviet Union under the guidance of the Trade Bureau with the Soviet Union, and distribute them to general consumers at low prices together with domestic products, and purchase what is still insufficient from other powers that are friendly to us, then not only will the struggle against Japan achieve extremely high economic results, but also the purchase issue can be used as an effective tactic in negotiating between the powers.

However, all the above is premised on the ability to incite an anti-imperialist national revolution against Japan. If the people's determination to resist Japan is still subject to suppression due to the threat of Japanese gunboats, and the policy of seeking temporary peace through compromise has not changed drastically, then organization and policies will all become empty talk on paper.

Enemy Attacks Qingshankou and Retreats 14

Enemy Aircraft Bomb Jianchangying

Zheng Guilin's Troops Still Defend Yangzhuang

(Luanzhou) Taotouying reports that on the 1st, more than two hundred enemy infantry and artillery attacked the position of the □ battalion of our Qiu regiment in the Qingshankou area. The defending soldiers resisted valiantly, and repelled the enemy at approximately 5 o'clock. The enemy and our side each suffered more than ten casualties. At the end of the day, the enemy continued to attack our right flank position at Heilongtou with four mountain guns, firing more than forty rounds, destroying one gun emplacement. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) After withdrawing from Yiyuankou, the volunteer army of Zheng Guilin is still currently defending the □□ position. Li Chao, a counselor of Zheng's unit, came to Ping earlier and is now returning to defense. His deputy commander, Wu Jinduo, has come to Ping again today to discuss military affairs. (2nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Qian'an reports that enemy aircraft bombed Jianchangying on the 1st. Our buildings were all destroyed by the bombing. Our army captured many traitors. (2nd Dispatch)

Enemy Disrupts Area Near Panjiakou 15

(Beiping) A certain party received a telegram from Zhang Letian, the Brigade Commander of the 29th Army, stating that at noon on the 1st, two enemy aircraft came to reconnoiter the area near the Sahe Bridge and dropped several bombs, fortunately not injuring anyone. At 4 p.m., the enemy gathered dozens of soldiers again, disrupting the area near Panjiakou, and were discovered and repelled by the defending soldiers of our position. (2nd Dispatch)

Dare-to-Die Squad Ambush Japanese Tanks 16

(Beiping) Zhang Guowei, an adjutant of a certain army unit, returned to Luanzhou from the front line, talking about a certain acting company commander of our Li Jialin regiment leading five soldiers to ambush a Japanese tank convoy from a certain place forty li from Lengkou on the 31st. Our five dare-to-die soldiers broke through the enemy's position, wildly firing large knives and box cannons left and right. The enemy, caught unprepared, panicked and scurried about. In about an hour, the enemy suffered more than twenty deaths and injuries, and the remainder fled. When the five returned to their unit, they were covered in blood. The company commander, holding a grenade, climbed onto a Japanese tank and bombed it, sacrificing his life. Five enemy tanks were destroyed. Our Lin Zuozhen regiment followed up with infantry and artillery. More than two hundred Japanese soldiers suffered heavy casualties and retreated north, moving towards Lingyuan. The front line is forty li from Lengkou. The enemy dispatches four or five planes every day to bomb our front line positions. (2nd Dispatch)

He Yingqin Will Be Officially Appointed Chairman of the Military Affairs Committee 17

Vacancy for Minister of Military Administration

Proposed that Zhu Peide Succeed

(Nanjing) It is rumored that the Central Government plans to officially appoint He Yingqin as the Chairman of the Ping Military Affairs Committee to be stationed in North China for a long time, controlling northern military affairs. For the vacant position of Minister of Military Administration, it is proposed to appoint Zhu Peide. As for the position of Director-General of Training, which Zhu is currently acting, it is still hoped that Li Jishen will return to Beijing to preside over it. (2nd Dispatch)

Chairman of the U.S. Naval Committee Proposes Building Thirty Ships in Three Years 18

Requires an Expenditure of 230 Million U.S. Dollars

To Avoid the Scorn of a "Paper Fleet"

(Washington) Vincent, Chairman of the U.S. House Naval Affairs Committee, proposed a ship construction program today, advocating the construction of thirty new ships within three years to end the era of the American "paper fleet." He hopes that President Roosevelt will support this proposal. According to Vincent's plan, the United States must immediately begin building the new ships permitted by the London Treaty. It is planned to build twenty destroyers, five light cruisers, four submarines, and one aircraft carrier within three years, requiring a total expenditure of 230 million gold dollars. It is estimated that the expenditure in the first year will not exceed 46 million gold dollars. This sum can be indirectly raised as long as the various departments of national defense make every effort to economize on political expenses. He firmly advocates strict economy in naval spending, but the time has come for shipbuilding and we cannot abandon eating for fear of choking. Moreover, this plan not only provides jobs for the unemployed and increases the effectiveness of the navy, but also allows the United States to have other physical objects besides a few drawings when discussing arms reduction with other countries. As for the reduction of naval administration, he believes that other than merging the Naval Purchasing Department with the Army Purchasing Department, there is little room for savings. Vincent has met with President Roosevelt several times regarding shipbuilding. He once told the President that it is estimated that it will cost 600 million gold dollars over five years to build all the warships permitted by the London Treaty. The new program proposed by Vincent today has not yet exceeded this estimated amount. However, it has exceeded half the amount of his first proposal to the President to spend 30 million gold dollars annually for shipbuilding expenses, probably because Vincent anticipated that disarmament would be difficult to agree to in the near future, so he advocated slightly increasing the shipbuilding budget in order to see it completed sooner. (1st National Telegram)

Saionji Supports Saitō 19

Incentivizing the Temporary Maintenance of the Status Quo

Coping with Extraordinary Times

Cabinet Decides to Convene Emergency Meeting Tomorrow

Prime Minister of Japan's Future to be Clearly Indicated

Seiyūkai Attempts to Regain Power

But Party Rule Will Not Be Easily Revived for the Time Being

Shizuoka, today, 9:30 AM, Prime Minister Saitō visited Saionji in Okitsu, reported in detail the events of withdrawing from the League of Nations, as well as future diplomatic policies and the results of the Diet, and recent political situations. Furthermore, regarding the current situation, the Prime Minister disclosed his political views. Saionji then strongly encouraged the Prime Minister, saying that the current extraordinary situation is becoming increasingly serious. The Emperor has also issued an edict, urging the nation to awaken. Therefore, if the political situation becomes unstable at this time, it would be extremely frightening. One should uphold the Emperor's will, shoulder the responsibility of the current situation, and not lightly advance or retreat, deeply hoping for full self-respect, and so on. Therefore, Prime Minister Saitō will temporarily endeavor to take on the difficult task. After a meeting of more than one hour, he departed at 10:40 AM, and at 1:40 PM took the express train from Shizuoka Station to return to Kyoto. According to the Prime Minister, he reported in detail to Prince Saionji today the events of withdrawing from the League of Nations. As for future diplomatic policies, a concrete decision has not yet been made, but Japan must proceed in cooperation with the great powers. Therefore, withdrawal is a separate issue, and efforts must be made in this regard in the future. Prince Saionji fully understands the government's current policy and has told me to devote myself to the country until death. Therefore, I myself will naturally proceed with this determination. As for the May 15 Incident, it is planned to be completed within May. Although Minister of Justice Oyama personally intends to resign, I hope that he will remain in office, as does Minister of Finance Takahashi. As for the development of the current situation, although there are various rumors, the Diet has just concluded, and there are still many things that need to be done. Therefore, now is not the time to resign, and future matters are still under consideration. (2nd, Dentsu News Agency)

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Saitō, after returning to Kyoto from Okitsu this afternoon, made an informal statement to reporters, and it is scheduled to convene a temporary emergency cabinet meeting on the morning of the 4th to report to each cabinet member the important strategies of the current political situation after meeting with the elder statesman and Prince Saionji. However, the fate of the Saitō Cabinet was not mentioned. It is generally speculated that the issue of the Saitō Cabinet's future will be clearly indicated after the emergency cabinet meeting (2nd, Chinese United News)

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Saitō's meeting with Prince Saionji has a significant relationship with the future political situation, and all aspects of the political world are paying close attention. The observations of the Seiyūkai and the Minseitō are each beneficial to their respective parties, so it is feared that a considerably complex vortex will be unavoidable depending on the Prime Minister's attitude in the future.

Seiyūkai's Perspective on the Prime Minister 20

Regarding the Meeting with Prince Saionji

The Prime Minister's conversation only considered others and spoke of the present, but there was no expression of new future plans or ambitions. If there is a true determination to shoulder the major current situation, then it is not just a matter of handling the aftermath of the Diet. This point actually exposes the powerlessness of the current cabinet and hints at the direction of the political situation. In short, the current cabinet's ability to achieve extraordinary results in this Diet is all due to the background of the Seiyūkai. The government has already done its best and has nothing else to do. Therefore, from a fair point of view, the reason for the existence of the current cabinet has now disappeared, and it has already achieved success and fame. Even the Prime Minister's meeting with Prince Saionji implicitly indicates this atmosphere. This is not a selfish view of our party but a very fair and appropriate observation. The current government is intent on organizing the post-Diet duties, seemingly in anticipation of a satisfactory resolution of the political situation.

Minseitō's Perspective 21

Prime Minister's Meeting with Prince Saionji

Regarding reporting on the withdrawal from the League of Nations and the conclusion of the Diet, as for political issues, it is feared that the responsibility in the future will become increasingly important, and it has been decided to exert all efforts to do so. It is believed that Prince Saionji understands this, and Prince Saionji also deeply understands this and hopes for the Prime Minister's self-respect. As a result, the rumors of political unrest should be swept away. Furthermore, the Prime Minister believes that the next Diet can be passed without incident. If it is not easy to pass, whether or not there is a determination to dissolve the Diet and discuss ways to open up the political situation will become a problem. In any case, the Minseitō is vigilant against all maneuvers at this time, and will consistently maintain the current cabinet in a just and upright manner. Regarding these matters, the Minseitō will informally report the party's actions in the Diet, and to gain understanding, it will soon send Secretary-General Matsuda to visit Prince Saionji. (2nd, Dentsu News Agency)

(Reuters, Tokyo, March 28) The Japanese Diet has adjourned on March 25. During the session of this Diet, the friendly attitude between the government and the Seiyūkai was clearly visible. Now, however, rumors of a cabinet change are rampant. According to reports, some time ago, it was widely rumored that Prime Minister Saitō and Seiyūkai President Suzuki had reached an understanding that if the Seiyūkai supported the passage of the 1933-34 budget, the current national unity cabinet would resign after the Diet adjourned and recommend the organization of a purely Seiyūkai cabinet to replace it. This is why the Seiyūkai adopted a friendly attitude during the Diet session, partly in the hope of regaining power. Although this specific understanding is highly questionable, if the current cabinet resigns, the power to select a successor will largely be in the hands of the elder statesman Saionji. It is said that the Seiyūkai's recent opposition to Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations and its insistence to the end is due to this reason, as the Seiyūkai members are well aware that Saionji is also opposed to withdrawal. It is easy to see that the Seiyūkai is making every effort to prepare for its return to power. It should be noted that on May 15, when Seiyūkai Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi was assassinated, the Seiyūkai held an absolute majority in the House of Representatives. After this act of violence occurred, it was necessary to organize a strong national unity government to cope with the serious domestic and foreign situation. The Seiyūkai now says that the current crisis has passed and a national unity government is no longer needed, so it believes that there is reason to take back power from Saitō now. If the Seiyūkai's words are credible and the national crisis has indeed disappeared, then the change of cabinet will naturally be easy. However, outside observers believe that the current restoration of party rule is extremely dangerous and may be even worse than the infighting a year ago that led to the establishment of a national unity government. There are many reasons why the Japanese people were united last year, but the two largest were the pressure from Geneva and the excitement over the Manchurian Incident. Now that Japan has withdrawn from the League of Nations, external condemnation is gradually diminishing, and the development of Manchuria is largely settled and no longer as active and dynamic as before. Therefore, Japan's unity is likely to weaken. Moreover, taxes are surprisingly high, and the people bear unprecedented burdens and sacrifices. Therefore, the general opinion is that Japan still urgently needs a national unity government today.

Japan to Issue Statement on Mandated Rule of Islands 22

(Tokyo) After the Japanese government formally notified its withdrawal from the League of Nations, the issue of the mandated rule of the South Pacific Islands became the center of international disputes. In addition, since Hitler came to power, the German government has expressed a clear attitude on this issue. Although Japan has repeatedly tried to escape this difficult situation with appeasement and double-edged political maneuvers, it has become clear in recent days that this issue cannot be resolved by simple means. Therefore, after several secret discussions between the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of the Navy, it has been decided that the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs will issue a formal and important statement on the South Pacific rule issue on the 4th, expressing the Japanese government's clear attitude on this issue. According to sources, once this statement is issued, it will cause a major wave in the international community. (2nd, Chinese United News)

Matsuoka's Activities in the United States 23

Meeting with Key Political Figures

(Washington) Former Japanese Chief Delegate to the League of Nations, Matsuoka Yōsuke, met with Senator Pittman, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, yesterday for two hours. The conversation concerned economic issues, especially the issue of raising silver prices. Matsuoka then met with former Senate Foreign Relations Committee Chairman Borah and House Foreign Affairs Committee Chairman McReynolds. He then visited the French Ambassador to the United States, Claudel, and U.S. Under Secretary of State Moley. In the evening, he attended a banquet at the Japanese Embassy, which was also attended by many key figures in the American political world. This afternoon, Matsuoka will give a lecture in Chicago on the Manchurian situation, and within a few days he will also visit the Troy Motor Factory and other factories. (2nd, Havas News Agency)

Using New York Newspaper Space to Sow Discord Between China and the United States 24

(New York) The New York Times published an article by former Japanese Chief Delegate to the League of Nations, Matsuoka Yōsuke, explaining Japan's position on the Manchurian issue and the process of withdrawing from the League of Nations. The main idea is that he admits that the United States and Japan are mutually suspicious, and that American newspapers in general, as well as the attitude adopted by the League of Nations, have not given Japan fair treatment. Japan has no grievances against the League of Nations, but Japan has no choice but to declare its withdrawal, which it deeply regrets. There are fundamental differences between the opinions of the League of Nations and Japan. The Lytton Commission's intention is to create temporary international cooperation through various specialized committees to achieve internal transformation of China. This is due to an insufficient understanding of the situation in China. China is the largest country in the world, and the task of restoring order from chaos is extremely arduous, which cannot be accomplished by the League of Nations' original methods. Only force can solve it. To eliminate Chinese warlords, it is necessary to take this major measure, but no country or several countries are willing to do so. Matsuoka recalled the old case of the humiliation of the American Consul in Nanjing, saying that at that time, the United States had to station troops in China and park warships in commercial ports to protect diplomatic representatives. This fact is unprecedented for other countries, and two soldiers must be sent to protect each foreign businessman. What benefits can be said to exist in trade with China under such circumstances? He also said that the United States' trade with Japan, apart from the United Kingdom, is more than with any other country. The United States' exports to the Far East, including the Philippines, are not as much as its exports to Japan. Japan does not want to close the door of American trade in China, and even less does it want to close the door of American trade with Japan. Matsuoka also criticized the United States' pro-China policy, saying that the United States' position on China is contradictory to its general policy. Although the American government has asked the Senate to ratify the Nine-Power Treaty to guarantee the territorial integrity of China, it has at the same time refused to join the League of Nations and the Permanent Court of International Justice, unwilling to provide the same guarantee to European countries. How is this not a contradiction? He also said that many Japanese people are concerned about the American sentiment towards Japan, but he does not care. Although the American people sympathize with China, after the final analysis, the American intellect will overcome its emotions. Matsuoka concluded by saying that Japan's actions in Manchuria are logical and effective, enough to save humanity and peace in the Far East. (2nd, Havas News Agency)

Atrocities Committed by the Enemy at Gubeikou 25

A Refugee Account from Gubeikou

(Beiping) According to refugees from Gubeikou, on the morning of the 11th of last month, a Japanese tank drove into Gubeikou and patrolled the main street of Hedong for a week. At the same time, a Japanese plane flew in and scattered leaflets everywhere, stating "Welcome the army of the Great Japanese Empire to enter the country, quickly bring flags to greet them outside the pass, otherwise Gubeikou will be bombed into scorched earth." That afternoon, the main enemy force of one thousand men marched in formation, mostly Korean bandits, with only a few Japanese soldiers among them. After the enemy arrived, they looted everything on the first night. Slightly better wooden furniture was moved outside the pass for fuel, and broken objects were thrown all over the streets. After occupying the area, the enemy troops conducted extensive searches, and any intellectuals or former soldiers were immediately put to death. On the 19th night, a platoon of our troops sneaked up to the high building on the eastern wall of Gubeikou. There were nine Japanese sentries in the building, eight of whom were killed by our troops with hand grenades, and the remaining one was wounded and escaped. After a while, a large force of enemy reinforcements arrived and engaged our troops in a long battle. They eventually retreated due to lack of support. After suffering this major blow, the Japanese cut off all traffic on the streets of Gubeikou. The Japanese military suffered heavy casualties. The wounded were transported back for medical treatment, and the dead were collected from all the residents of Gubeikou and placed in coffins, two or three Japanese soldiers per coffin, and transported to Xijiaochang to be burned. Of the more than one thousand households in Gubeikou, two-thirds had fled. (2nd, Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Zhu Chuanjing went to Baoding to visit He Chengjun, and has now returned to Beiping after completing his mission. He is scheduled to return to Wuhan within a few days. (2nd, Special Dispatch)

Liang Zuoyou Active Again 56

Yesterday Visited Han Fuju

Proposed National Salvation Plan Through Thrift

(Jinan) Today, Liang Zuoyou visited Han Fuju and Zhang Shaotang, the secretary-general of the provincial government, and presented his self-authored National Salvation Through Thrift plan, which is over 8,000 words long. The main points include establishing a National Salvation Through Thrift Committee, electing committee members by the people, and establishing a National Salvation Through Thrift Bank. The committee would manage the issuance of 200 million yuan in National Salvation Through Thrift circulating notes, to be used as follows: 10% for suppressing communists, defending against foreign aggression, and disaster relief; 60% for developing industries; and the rest for bank funds. The fundraising method would involve each of the 400 million people in the country contributing one "pu man" (simple man), paying one copper coin per day, with two years as one term, and a term payment of two yuan. In this way, 200 million yuan could be raised in ten years, and the national salvation plan could be completed. The original text is quite logical. (2nd Special Dispatch)

Tragic Incident of Gangsters Feuding and Killing Each Other 80

Liu Mazi Covered in Knife Wounds

Wang Youcai's Abdomen Pierced and Intestines Protruding

(Changshu) Wang Youcai from Huaiyin and Liu Mazi had a feud over the uneven distribution of money from gambling dens, leading to a deadly fight. At 10 AM on the 2nd, Wang and his brother Youkui secretly carried daggers and iron rulers to Liu's house at No. 14 Zhongxiang Lane in the city, dragged Liu out, and began hacking and stabbing him. Liu was slashed dozens of times, covered in wounds, and blood flowed all over the street. Liu's wife, Bao, knelt and begged for mercy, but was also stabbed in the back of the head. The patrol police, only armed with short sticks, did not dare to intervene until the security team arrived and stopped them. Liu was unable to move. Both were sent to the Yuhe Hospital. Wang Youcai was also stabbed in the abdomen, and about an inch of his intestines protruded. Liu's life is in danger. Youkui was unharmed and has been taken into custody by the Public Security Bureau. At the time, Qiancai, naked and roaring angrily, was like a madman, stabbing and slashing for half an hour. More than a thousand onlookers were stunned. (2nd Special Dispatch)

Diverse Forms of Anti-Semitic Movements in Germany 81

Jewish Shops: Some Closed, Some Operating Normally

No Riots Reported Anywhere Except Kiel

Schleicher Announces End to Boycott Is Unnecessary

Einstein's Property Confiscated by German Authorities

Reuters, Berlin, 1st: The organization of the anti-Jewish movement in Berlin is disorganized. Despite the nationwide announcement of a boycott against Jewish shops, many still remained open for business, even with anti-Jewish signs displayed in their windows. Most Jewish shops in Berlin proper were closed, but not all large Jewish shops in the suburbs followed suit, and their owners were not disturbed. Many non-Jewish shop employees in these closed large Jewish shops were left with nothing to do, and these employees did not entirely support the anti-Jewish boycott. Groups of people gathered in front of the closed Jewish shops, discussing the matter in heated tones, while brown-shirted comrades walked among them, placing signs on the windows to indicate that they were Jewish shops. Today is the day of the National Socialist Party's major demonstration; swastika flags and imperial flags were flying on all trams and streetcars in Berlin, and military bands paraded through the streets, playing military songs and patriotic songs. The streets of Kurfürstendamm were crowded, many shops were closed, and the number of idlers increased. The anti-Jewish movement on Kurfürstendamm was very strict; not only were leaflets posted outside Jewish shops, but also Jewish doctors' offices and other offices were boycotted. What was particularly discouraging was the placement of cameras in front of Jewish shops; anyone seen leaving a Jewish shop was photographed, and as a result, people did not dare to enter. Today is Saturday, the Jewish Sabbath, so many Jews took the opportunity to close their shops. There have been no instances of violence against people in the Kurfürstendamm area. The train to Denmark today was full of passengers, all of whom were Jews leaving the country. Several hundred disembarked in Copenhagen, but many others continued on to other parts of Denmark.

Reuters, Munich, 1st: General Schleicher, leader of the anti-Jewish movement, declared here tonight that, according to telegrams from overseas, it is not necessary to continue the boycott after Wednesday, April 5th. Therefore, the boycott will be limited to one day, and will end nationwide tonight, approximately.

National, Berlin, 1st: Today, Germany held a nationwide one-day boycott of Jewish shops to express the German people's indignation at the Jews' anti-German propaganda. However, the day passed peacefully and without incident. All shops not owned by Jews posted large characters on their windows reading "German Shop" to avoid being mistaken for Jewish shops and attacked by the crowd. Austrian Jews operating shops in Berlin also wrote "Austrian Shop" on their windows. There were no unexpected events in the provinces, except in Kiel, where a Jewish lawyer shot a National Socialist Stormtrooper in the midst of the anti-Jewish turmoil, seriously wounding him. The lawyer, named Scheim, was arrested and imprisoned, but the public was so outraged that they broke into the prison and killed Scheim. They then swarmed to the shop owned by Scheim's father and destroyed all the goods.

National, Berlin, 1st: Professor Einstein's bank deposits have been frozen today by the Berlin political police. In addition, mortgages and cash worth about 30,000 marks have also been confiscated by the authorities. According to newspaper reports, the reason for these harsh measures is that this money was apparently used for treasonous purposes. Furthermore, the Prussian Academy of Sciences issued a statement today stating that it was outraged by newspaper reports of Professor Einstein's participation in anti-German propaganda in France and the United States. Einstein was originally a Swiss citizen, but obtained Prussian citizenship in 1913 after being elected as a member of the Academy of Sciences. Now, he is openly engaged in anti-German propaganda abroad, which is contrary to the Academy's principles and ideology. Therefore, the Academy considers itself fortunate that Einstein has left the organization.

French Female Aviator Flies to the Far East 82

Via Shanghai to Tokyo

Havas, Le Bourget, France, 1st: French female aviator Ms. Hélène Boucher departed from here at 6 a.m. this morning in a 300-horsepower aircraft, intending to fly swiftly to Hanoi, Vietnam, and then leisurely to Tokyo. The planned route is Brindisi, Athens, Aleppo, Basra, Jask, Calcutta, Rangoon, Hanoi, Shanghai, Seoul, and Tokyo.

Britain, Germany, and the Soviet Union 83

British Ambassador to Moscow Recalled to London

To Attend Cabinet Meeting and Report on British Citizens' Arrests

Soviet Russia Will Prosecute on Four Charges Under Domestic Law

U.S. Resumption of Relations with Russia Not Affected by British Case

Prussian Police Suddenly Search Russian Oil Company

Thirteen Employees Detained, Reasons Unannounced

Havas, London, 2nd: British Ambassador to Russia, Sir Esmond Ovey, has been recalled and arrived here this morning. A special committee of the Cabinet will be formed on Monday to discuss the situation caused by the arrest of British engineers in Russia. Ovey will attend and present his views.

Reuters, London, 1st: It is reported that the Soviet authorities will prosecute the British Vickers Company engineers arrested in Russia under sections 6-11 of Article 58 of the Russian Criminal Code, including charges of espionage, sabotage, bribery, and conspiracy.

TASS, London, 1st: Local newspapers are disappointed that the U.S. has not paid much attention to the Moscow British engineer case. They had hoped that this case would hinder the progress of establishing diplomatic relations between the U.S. and the Soviet Union. The "Morning Post" stated in an editorial that the case had not aroused the interest of the United States as they had hoped. U.S. newspapers published the news in a very brief manner and placed it on the back pages, while featuring news about the establishment of diplomatic relations between the U.S. and the Soviet Union on the front page.

Reuters, Berlin, 1st: The Prussian police today searched the offices of the Russian Coal and Oil Company and detained all thirteen employees inside. The reasons for the detention have not been announced, but it is widely believed to be the latest in a series of searches of the company's branches in Cologne, Leipzig, and Mülheim. It is reported that the Russian Oil Company supplies 30% of Germany's oil.

British-French Contact

Four-Power Agreement Plan 84

French Ambassador to Italy Returns to Paris

Reports on Rome Negotiations

Havas, Paris, 1st: This afternoon at 4:00, the British ambassador to France, Lord Tyrrell, visited Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour, with the aim of informing Paul-Boncour of the opinions of the British Prime Minister and Foreign Secretary after consulting with the French authorities in Paris. After Tyrrell left, the Foreign Minister immediately reported the results of his conversation with Tyrrell to Prime Minister Daladier. The French ambassador to Rome, Suvard, has returned to Paris to report all news related to the current situation to the authorities. Since the government has clearly understood the British and Italian proposals, it can fully express its views. It is expected that a cabinet meeting will be held next week to discuss the matter. This afternoon, Suvard and Paul-Boncour talked for two hours. Suvard reported to Paul-Boncour all the details of the recent negotiations between the British and Italian authorities in Rome. The two then exchanged views on the negotiations in Rome and elsewhere.

Havas, Paris, 1st: The French Ambassador to Rome, Suvard, arrived in Paris at 9:50 AM this morning. At 3:00 PM, he visited Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour. They talked until 4:00 PM, when the British Ambassador, Tyrrell, arrived, and the conversation was temporarily suspended for half an hour. Afterwards, they resumed the conversation until 5:00 PM. Suvard then went to the Ministry of War and met with Prime Minister Daladier.

Havas, Paris, 2nd: The French Ambassador to Italy, Suvard, has returned to the country and recently received a representative from this agency. He issued an important statement regarding the plan proposed by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. Suvard strongly advocated that an accurate report must be made to public opinion, so that false news does not confuse listeners. Suvard stated that the plan circulated externally is not what was discussed in Rome. The wording of the plan drafted in Rome has not yet been finalized. Mussolini's intention is that the draft agreement should be included within the scope of the League of Nations. Its main points are that the four major powers participate in the work of the League of Nations, and that the disarmament conference achieves results, as it has the same benefits. There is a need to reach an understanding. If the disarmament conference fails, then organize a true "insurance company" to avoid the danger after the failure and all attempts to modify the peace treaty by force. However, no country among the four major powers should evade this contract, as it is in the common interest of all countries. Suvard concluded that Mussolini believed that France, being loyal to the League of Nations, would certainly understand the purpose of this agreement, which would strengthen the League of Nations.

U.S. President Signs New Order

Reducing Veterans' Pensions 85

Effective July 1st

Affects 400,000 People

Havas, Washington, 2nd: President Roosevelt's order regarding the reduction of veterans' pensions will take effect on July 1st of this year. The terms of this order stipulate that all pensions will be reduced by 20% and the method of payment will be modified. The following conditions must be met in order to receive a pension: (1) must have enlisted for at least three months; (2) the enlistment period must be before the cessation of hostilities; (3) must have a certificate of good conduct for the enlistment period; (4) long-term disability must not be due to misconduct. This order will apply to veterans of the Spanish-American War, the Boxer Rebellion in China, the Philippine Insurrection, and the European War of 1914. For widows of veterans of the three wars before the Great War, the pensions they should receive will be reduced by 50%. It is estimated that according to this order, 400,600 people will no longer receive pensions.

Havas, Washington, 2nd: The Disabled Veterans of the European War Association strongly opposes President Roosevelt's order to reduce the pensions of veterans, which amounts to 400 million gold yuan. The chairman of the association, Conley, declared that we have those who lost their sight and those with crippled limbs fighting in Europe. The fact that the pensions enjoyed by these people are being reduced so much will arouse resentment among the people. Public opinion throughout the country will demand that the government keep the promises made in 1918.

I. Description of Future Wars and Total Mobilization 88

What will future wars be like? Needless to say, we all know that everything is evolving, and war has also evolved greatly from ancient times to the present. In the wars of primitive times, the main subject of war was roughly one person as the center, or one clan as the center. However, as society gradually evolved, the main subject of war gradually expanded to include nations, tribes, cities, or countries. Also, ancient wars were limited to a portion of the population, especially a small number of people advocating the use of force to wage war. Therefore, the end of the war was always attributed to the downfall of the central figure, the decline of one clan, or the defeat of the armed group of a tribe, city, or country. However, since the Franco-Prussian War of 1870-1873, the state of evolution has been particularly apparent. That is, the French army was almost completely destroyed by the German army. Although the field army was a false message and did not cause confusion. Suvard declared that the plan circulated externally is not what was discussed in Rome. However, no country among the four major powers should evade this contract, as it is in the common interest of all countries. Japan's Preparations for Total War (Japanese Correspondence) 91

Recently, the Science Pictorial Publishing House in this area held a symposium on national mobilization. The attendees were all figures from the Army Department, such as Kamitsuki Yoshio, Head of the Control Section of the Maintenance Bureau; Yari Tomoshiru, a member of the section; Yamada Seiichi of the Mobilization Section of the Maintenance Bureau; and Tani Hagi Kah雄 of the Press Corps. Their discussions were extremely important. I will translate and summarize them below. Reading it should clarify a glimpse of Japan's recent preparations for war.

I. Description of Future Wars and Total Mobilization 92

What kind of form will future wars take? Needless to say, we all know that everything evolves, and war has also evolved greatly from ancient times to the present. In the wars of the primitive era, the main subject of the war was roughly centered on one person, or one clan. However, as society gradually evolved, the main subject of war gradually expanded to ethnic groups, tribes, cities, or countries. Furthermore, ancient wars were limited to a part of the population, especially a small number of people who advocated the use of force to fight. Therefore, the end of the war was always attributed to the downfall of the central figure, or the demise of a clan, or the defeat of armed groups of tribes, cities, or countries. However, since the Franco-Prussian War from 1870 to 1873, an evolutionary state has been particularly manifested, that is, the French army was almost completely destroyed by the German army. Although the field army was completely defeated, it is said that the strength of the volunteer army assembled by Gambetta afterwards was 2.5 million. This shows that in this era, even if the field army is destroyed, if the people still have a strong will to continue the war, they can still fight for the country. After that, although the Sino-Japanese War and the Russo-Japanese War also occurred, these were not considered thorough wars, and can be said to have ended midway. Therefore, the so-called national war form was not manifested. If Japan had been defeated at that time, it would have gathered volunteer soldiers again to continue the national decisive battle. As for the World War, needless to say, almost all of Europe participated in the war. There is history that can testify to the footprint of its evolution. That is, in the primitive era, war was a state of one person against one person. However, due to the evolution of society, war has gradually become various forms, such as the Franco-Prussian War, which can be said to be a war of the whole people, and the World War, which can be said to be a war of national power. If there is another war in the future, I think that this future war has a very close relationship with the entire world's politics, economy, transportation, and transportation. Therefore, the occurrence of war is less like a military war state of one country against one country like the Sino-Japanese War and the Russo-Japanese War, and more like a complex war state of several countries against several countries or one country against several countries. From this point of view, in the future war, the number of soldiers used by the two armies should increase compared to past battles. Therefore, more military supplies should also be needed. Moreover, as mentioned earlier, the methods of engagement have also changed greatly, and finally become the so-called war of national power. Therefore, when two countries are at war, eliminating the enemy country's will to continue the war is also counted as a tactic. So, what methods should be used to eliminate the enemy country's will to continue the war? There are many methods. To give one or two examples, one method is to use propaganda to dispel the army's or the people's belief in victory. Furthermore, airplanes are very developed now. Transporting a ton of bombs by plane from a distance and dropping them on political centers such as Tokyo or economic and industrial centers such as Nagoya or Kitakyushu is another method. Or, airplanes can still be used to drop bombs on industrial cities to plan to destroy their resources. This kind of planned destruction of resources is also a method of engagement. Other measures, such as the starvation policy or economic blockade adopted by Germany against Britain, should also be regarded as an important means of engagement. Recently, a certain country (referring to the Soviet Union) even issued a statement that there will be no front lines in future wars. In fact, when fighting a war, bullets must be used to confront each other. Therefore, there is no such thing as a war without a front line. However, a certain country's means of engagement are like this: on the one hand, fighting on the front line, while expanding the front line, from the rear of the front line, to the colonies and the enemy country, using various methods to eliminate its military force, or guide its revolution. Indeed, it may be possible for a certain country to adopt such means of engagement. From this point of view, future wars are no longer linear or planar, but three-dimensional. In terms of region, the war has expanded from the battlefield to the country. Regarding the equipment of the army, during the World War, Germany used poison gas to attack secretly, causing the British army to be defeated. Conversely, Britain used tanks to break into the German army, putting the German territory in danger. As such, weapons have made tremendous progress due to war. In the future, new weapons will inevitably be produced in response to the times. Moreover, these weapons will use a large amount of iron. Recently, the tendency to use a large amount of poison gas materials has also been clearly manifested. When we look at the weapons that various countries are striving for, we can understand that what they value is the enrichment of aircraft, the development of chemical warfare equipment, and the increase in the power of guns and cannons. In order to remedy these, they are doing their best to research optical, electrical, and precision mechanical knowledge weapons, and various cars are used to replace horses. Mechanized corps have been discovered in various countries since several years ago. If we observe the situation of future wars in this way, it is very clear that a large amount of iron and a large amount of military supplies are needed from any aspect. During the Russo-Japanese War, the Japanese army fired 1.05 million shells in two years. In the Battle of Shenyang, the Japanese army fired 330,000 shells in two weeks. However, in the Battle of the Marne during the World War, the French army fired 1 million shells in one week. That is to say, the number of shells used by Japan in two years during the Russo-Japanese War was fired by the French army in one week. Furthermore, in the Battle of Sulm, the French army alone used 20 million shells in two weeks, while the British army used 14 million shells. As such, with so much iron falling on the enemy's position, just imagining these shells, where should these industries manufacture them during wartime? This question will inevitably arise immediately. In the Japanese army, there is only the arsenal. Of course, not many things can be made here. Therefore, it is impossible not to rely on private factories. This is just for bullets. However, clothing, rations, etc. also require a great amount. Other things, such as hygiene materials and veterinary materials, also require a considerable amount. It is ultimately impossible to manufacture these things in government-owned factories. Expanding capacity temporarily cannot be done in a short period of time. Therefore, it is necessary to use private factories. Other questions such as how to obtain raw materials, and if the products are manufactured, how should they be stored and where should they be transported? If you think about it, there will definitely be various other questions. These questions should be resolved in peacetime. It is impossible to prepare when the war breaks out. Therefore, we must prepare in peacetime. We call the plan for this kind of preparation military-industrial mobilization.

(To be continued)

You Guocai's Troops Return to Guizhou 93

There is No Confirmation of Contact Between You and Wang's Troops

Sichuan's Liu Xiang and Yunnan's Long Yun Ask You and Jiang for Residence

Beijing News: It was reported in Chongqing's telegram a few days ago that You Guocai's troops, with the support of Long Yun, were advancing towards Guizhou and had opened fire with Wang Jialie's troops. According to reliable sources, as of the second day before yesterday, there had been no fighting. After You Guocai arrived in Shanghai, he stayed for several days because someone was detecting his whereabouts, and then took a boat south, going to Yunnan via Hong Kong. He arrived in Yunnan on the 16th of last month and met with Long Yun, the chairman of Yunnan. Long immediately replenished him with ammunition and firearms. You's troops, totaling more than 5,000 people, are now stationed in various counties in eastern Yunnan, such as Luoping, Shizong, Yiliang, and Pingyi, which are very close to the Guizhou border. You left Kunming on the 20th and went to Luoping to reorganize his troops. There is no report that the army has been mobilized. The Guizhou army Jiang Zaizhen's troops, which retreated into southern Sichuan, originally cooperated with You's troops and are still stationed in Nanchuan. However, Liu Xiang of Sichuan and Long Yun of Yunnan believe that the Guizhou army should not be stationed in neighboring provinces for a long time, and have respectively telegraphed Wang Jialie, the chairman of Guizhou, to ask You and Jiang's troops for residence so that they can return to their province. Zhongding Pan Yi Discovered in Teng County 95

It is Said to be Relics of the Shang and Zhou Dynasties

Jinan Correspondence: Teng County is located in southern Shandong and was the State of Teng in the Spring and Autumn Period. Last year, nine Han Dynasty stone paintings were discovered in the county. They are antique and extremely precious. They have now been moved to the Provincial Library on the shore of Daming Lake in Jinan for preservation. Yesterday, the Education Department also received a telegram from Wei Xihong, an inspector in Teng County, reporting that fourteen Zhongding Pan Yi antiques were discovered in Dongan Shang Village in the county, and merchants are competing to buy them. The Education Department believes that the discovery of Zhongding Pan Yi and other antiques is very important, and Wei Xihong's report is brief and not detailed. Therefore, the county magistrate was ordered to report in detail that if the antiques were discovered by private individuals and have not been sold, they should be purchased at a price and returned to the public. If they have already been purchased by merchants, efforts should also be made to purchase them back for preservation to avoid loss. It is said that these antiques are relics of the Shang and Zhou Dynasties.

Since then, the county has been completely under the iron hooves of the bandits and has been used by the bandits as a Soviet area for a full six years. When Chairman Chiang personally came to Jiangxi to plan the fourth major encirclement and suppression campaign, he regarded the area as the source of the Red bandits in the country. The people of the three counties had been immersed in the Red Sea for a long time. Therefore, Wang Maode's division on the west bank of the Gan River, Li Zhenqiu and Ye Zhao's troops from Chongyi and Shangyou in southern Jiangxi, and Tao Guang's troops from Pingxiang were ordered to advance towards the three counties. At that time, the Red bandits entrenched in the area were Li Tianzhu's troops. Li appointed himself as the commander of the Xiang-Gan Military Region and commander of the pseudo-Eighth Army, commanding the pseudo-Twenty-first, Twenty-second, and Twenty-third Divisions, with about 3,000 to 4,000 guns. Their pseudo-organ was located in Yongxin City, and the bandits were distributed in Suichuan, Lianhua, Anfu, Wan'an, and various borders, appearing and disappearing on the west bank of the Gan River, looting on a large scale. After the general attack by the Gan, Yue, and Xiang armies, Wang's troops had recovered Ninggang, and Li's troops had captured the bandit nests in Wudoujiang and Huang'ao south of Suichuan, and joined Wang's troops to attack Yaqian. The bandits in the area bordering Suichuan, Wan'an, Shangyou, and Chongyi, because Li's bandits were under pressure, abandoned their old nest on the Gan-Xiang border and fled north. When Kong Hechong's pseudo-Sixteenth Army invaded Xinyu and Fenyi in February, Li's bandits attempted to cross the Yuan River and join Kong's troops, but Zhu Yaohua and Tao Guang cut them off, so they turned and fled southeast, invading Xiajiang and Xingan, and attempted to cooperate with the bandits in Yongfeng on the east bank of the Gan River. The police team of the county, which had fled to Pingxiang, had also returned to the county with the army. At this moment, the Gan, Yue, and Xiang armies have joined forces to attack Yongxin. Once Yongxin is recovered, there will be no counties in western Jiangxi that are completely occupied by bandits. However, two-thirds of the people in these counties have died. The fields and gardens have long been covered with weeds, and the houses are full of weeds. The broken and miserable scene cannot be described in words. At this moment, Xiong Shihui has appointed Li Zhengyi as the administrative inspector of the Tenth District, taking a detour through Hunan to clean up the ruins, save the dying, and heal the wounded.
