Songjiang 96

A False Alarm of Robbery at the Li Family in the City 97

The Li family's residence east of Aijia Bridge in the northern gate of the city was once robbed in the past. Unexpectedly, last night (the 1st) at about 9:00 p.m., the residence suddenly heard a very loud knocking sound on the back door. Because it was late at night and the location was remote, the family recalled the past and were like frightened birds. They knew it was not a good person and quickly tried to report to the police station by telephone. However, after shaking the phone for a long time, there was no response. They realized something was wrong and a family member climbed over the front wall and reported to the Public Security Bureau. The police rushed to the scene, but the person knocking on the door was nowhere to be found. However, it was observed that the telephone line had been cut. It can be seen that the bandits attempted to rob but failed.

Crackdown on Ferryboats in Conflicting Routes 98

Last year, the Construction Department issued a license for inland steamships and ferryboats to ensure the safety of travelers. Those who obtained licenses complied with the regulations, but those who tried to be clever often used old-fashioned rowing boats modified with diesel engines and propellers, without a fixed route, competing with various boats for business, resulting in frequent capsizing and burning incidents. With the approval of the former Construction Bureau, it was decided to crack down on them. Now that the Construction Bureau has been abolished, the county government has found that the Xin Aili, Tianli, and Xinfeng boats traveling from Shanyang to Song, the Xingfei and two unnamed boats traveling from Tinglin to Song, and the Aili boat traveling from Jinshanwei to Song all conflict with the routes of the Bianli Company's boats and should be stopped immediately. The remaining existing motorized rowing boats should be reported for inspection within two weeks. Only after they are legal will they be allowed to travel.

Jinshan 99

An Official on Duty Assaults and Humiliates the Principal of the People's Education Center 100

The Ping Opera Research Association of the Zhu Jing People's Education Center in this county is rehearsing Ping Opera from March 30th to raise funds for the aviation patriotic donation. At about 7:00 p.m. on April 1st, an official on duty from the Shi Cheng District in this county, accompanied by four friends, entered the venue to watch the play without buying tickets. Shen Shixiong, the principal of the People's Education Center, advised them to buy tickets to enter the venue. The official on duty refused and slapped Principal Shen in the face. Principal Shen believed that the official on duty was so fierce and immediately asked the police officers of the County Public Security Bureau who were maintaining order on the scene to report to the County Bureau. At that time, the District Official was also watching the play at the scene and reported to the District Official. Unexpectedly, the District Official not only did not blame the official on duty, but instead questioned Principal Shen, which aroused public outrage among the audience. The scene became chaotic for a while. The staff in the venue reported to the County Government by telephone. Secretary Zhang of the County Government instructed the County Government to take them away, but the police officers of the County Public Security Bureau who were maintaining order on the scene did not dare to take them away because they saw that the District Official was on the scene. At that time, the crowd was excited. Seeing that the situation was not good, the District Official agreed to the County Public Security Bureau sending police to take them away, and Principal Shen also went to the County Public Security Bureau to report. It is now heard that all circles in the local area believe that the official on duty assaulted and humiliated public officials and destroyed the aviation patriotic movement, and unanimously advocate strict handling.

City News

Song Zheyuan's Representative

Xiao Zhenying Talks About the Bloody Battle 105

Six Thousand Enemies Killed with Broadswords at Xifengkou

Soldiers Stand in the Wind and Snow Without Weariness

People Flock to the Battlefield to Rescue the Wounded

Urgently Needs Trucks, Requests Assistance with Purchase

In the Future, We Must Unanimously Embrace the Determination to Sacrifice

Xiao Zhenying (Xiange), a member of the Beiping Military Sub-Committee, represents Song Zheyuan, the commander of the Twenty-ninth Army and commander-in-chief of the Third Army Corps.

He arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning after coming south from the front line to seek assistance. He issued a written statement yesterday, which is recorded below.

Song Zheyuan's Painful Words 106

Zhenying has come south this time because since the Battle of Xifengkou, our army has received support and condolences from all walks of life. Our commander-in-chief, Song Gongmingxuan, specially sent Zhenying to various places in Beijing and Shanghai to report everything and to express his gratitude on his behalf. Since the fall of Rehe, many say that the disparity in military preparedness between the enemy and us is too great to fight. Commander-in-Chief Song set out under orders, saying painfully that any country must first have those who sacrifice before there can be a day of success. In the Russo-Japanese War, the Japanese army was also inferior to Russia, but it was able to sacrifice 20,000 brave men to fight for a fortress and thus defeat a strong enemy and leap to become a hero. Now that the disaster of the invaders is deep, it is a great opportunity for our soldiers to become martyrs. If our 40,000 comrades are all sacrificed for the survival of the country and the nation, then it can be considered a worthy death, and only in this way can it be worthy of the country's intention to cultivate soldiers.

Bloody Battle at Xifeng Kill the Enemy 107

When we set off, the enemy's Thirteenth and Fourteenth Brigades, attached with puppet Mongolian troops, had advanced rapidly and occupied the advantageous positions of the Great Wall at Xifengkou. Our army rushed 160 miles in eight hours to block the enemy head-on. The enemy occupied high ground and unleashed the power of cannons, airplanes, tanks, armored vehicles, and various new-style weapons, which could not be approached. Our army was caught off guard and had no fortifications to cover them. They charged repeatedly, but no one survived. Commander-in-Chief Song personally led Division Commander Feng Zhi'an, Division Commander Zhang Zizhong, Brigade Commander Zhao Dengyu, etc., to command on the battlefield, and fought a bloody battle for three days and nights. Both sides suffered heavy casualties. Brigade Commander Zhao was wounded but did not retreat. On the fourth night, it was decided to divide the troops and use a detour strategy. Brigade Commander Zhao, with his wounds wrapped, led his team around 50 miles to attack the enemy's rear. Brigade Commander Tong Zeguang also joined the attack with his troops, and surrounded the enemy. It was late at night, and our army waved broadswords and slashed wildly. They wiped out the enemy's infantry and cavalry battalions and charged into the artillery positions, seizing 18 enemy cannons and using them to attack the remaining enemy. They also set fire to more than 200 enemy carts loaded with supplies and food. Seven of their tanks and five armored vehicles were also completely intercepted. Because the mountains were dangerous and difficult to transport, they were either blown up or buried to prevent them from returning. In this battle, our army suffered more than 3,000 casualties, and the enemy's deaths and injuries were more than double that of us, and the dangerous terrain of the Great Wall at Xifengkou was completely recovered by us.

Our Army Approaches Kuancheng 108

After this setback, the enemy dared not attack head-on, but used a force of one or two regiments to attack Dongjiakou on our left flank and Panjiakou on our right flank, but were all defeated by our army. Unable to vent their anger, they massacred three nearby villages. Because Luowenyu was a key location in our army's rear, they added an elite brigade to launch a fierce attack on the area. Division Commander Liu Ruming rushed to intercept them. The enemy used their weapons to cover their infantry and cavalry, who attacked our position fiercely. Our army rolled forward with broadswords under a dense hail of bullets, fighting a bloody battle. Regiment Commander Li Zengzhi had his leg broken by a cannonball, but he still sat firmly in a pool of blood without retreating, and cut open three enemy lines, capturing more than a dozen machine guns and killing countless enemies. Our army suffered the loss of three regimental commanders, four battalion commanders, and more than 2,000 soldiers, and the enemy was defeated and retreated more than 50 miles. Now our army at Xifengkou is pressing on Kuancheng, and our army at Luowenyu is occupying the Banbishan area. Zhenying received a telegram from the front yesterday in Beijing that two artillery battalions of the Japanese army (approximately equivalent to two of our battalions) were fiercely bombarding our army's positions outside Xifengkou with 500 shells. Most of their infantry and cavalry units are mobilizing, and it seems that their reinforcements have arrived and they are launching a large-scale attack again. Our army vows to fight to the death.

People Share the Same Hatred of the Enemy 109

Zhenying has repeatedly accompanied Dean Shao Yuan, Minister Kong Xiangxi, and Vice Minister Yu Feipeng to the front line to comfort the soldiers. The weather on the frontier is extremely cold, and even heavy fur coats cannot keep them warm. The soldiers are wearing short clothes and straw sandals, standing in the wind and snow without any sign of weariness. Upon hearing the words of comfort, they are all motivated a hundredfold. The local people are also helping with hot blood. Every time there is a battle, the people rush to the battlefield to rescue the wounded. When launching an attack, they compete to be guides. Even when the sound of cannons is booming, none of them run away. When asked why they are not afraid, they reply, "If our commander-in-chief doesn't drive away the little devils, we would have been slaves of a conquered nation long ago. The commander-in-chief is not afraid of death, so why should we be afraid of anything?" Also, at the beginning of the war, there were no hospitals in the rear, and thousands of wounded soldiers relied entirely on charitable organizations to find ways to rescue them, running around and taking care of them as if they were their own flesh and blood. All of this is due to the hatred of the enemy in the fight against foreign aggression, and I dare not say that the discipline is more strict because of this.

Urgent Need for Trucks 110

In short, spiritual strength overcomes material strength, and the sacrifice is naturally very great. Without sufficient preparation, it is not enough to talk about long-term resistance. At present, the central government has planned to replenish supplies, medicine, and bullets. However, for the transportation of 400 miles from Beiping to Xifengkou, it is entirely dependent on mules and human labor. Wounded soldiers have to spend four or five days on the way to reach the rear, which often leads to death due to delays in medical treatment. If we can get more trucks, all difficulties can be reduced. What's more, the past mistake is that every time the enemy is preparing for war, we try to live in peace. When the enemy comes to attack, we are willing to retreat. The repeated loosening and tightening has been taken advantage of by the enemy. This is the same mistake as the Southern Song Dynasty's avoidance of the Jin.

Determination to Have the Enemy but Not Me 111

The plan for the future is that the whole country should be united and determined to have the enemy but not me, and everyone should have the idea of destroying their homes to relieve the country's difficulties. When the enemy comes, we should fight to the death, and even if they don't come, we should attack. Regardless of the superiority or inferiority of materials, regardless of the amount of sacrifice, we will not stop until we have recovered the lost land. The domestic economy of the Japanese invaders is on the verge of collapse, and social thoughts are surging forward. Although a few warlords are still struggling and unable to get off the tiger, the people of their country are tired of war and afraid of war. If we can fight for another year or two, they will inevitably collapse completely. The final victory will surely belong to us. No matter what sacrifices are made, our army will not hesitate. If we are not willing to fight or dare not fight, we will retreat and the enemy will advance deeper and deeper. Apart from national subjugation and extermination, there is no other good fortune.

Tang Youren's Speech 112

The central government believes that the national crisis is urgent and is preparing to concentrate the national strength to resist Japan, that is, to open up political power and cooperate with the people of the country. Therefore, the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee recently resolved to convene the National Assembly in advance and ordered the Central Political Council to discuss the principles of the organization law and election law. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency visited Tang Youren, the Secretary-General of the Central Political Council, at his residence in Shanghai yesterday. According to Tang, after the proposal to convene the National Assembly in advance was passed by the Standing Committee, preparations will be made to formulate the organization law and election law of the Assembly to form the basis for the establishment of the Assembly. The method is that the Central Political Conference will decide on the principles and then hand them over to the Legislative Yuan to draft detailed regulations. The Central Political Council has decided to hold a meeting this Wednesday to discuss the principles, and then send them to the Legislative Yuan for drafting. When the reporter asked about the central government's attitude towards Kijuro Shidehara's visit, Tang replied that the central government allows him to come and go without expressing any opinion, and Shidehara and the current rulers of Japan belong to two factions and will not have a special mission. Mr. Wang has officially gone to the Executive Yuan and has no intention of coming to Shanghai in the coming days.

Shanghai Postal Workers Union

Yesterday's Welcome for Zhu Ziqiao 113

Mr. Zhu Reports on the Situation at the Front

The People Should be Resolved to Resist

Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union held a welcome meeting for Mr. Zhu Ziqiao in the grand hall on the third floor of the Shanghai Postal Administration. About 500 members attended to listen to Mr. Zhu's report on the situation at the front. The meeting began with an opening speech by Chairman Cao Xunye, followed by Mr. Zhu's report. He humbly stated that while the welcome was appreciated, reporting was his duty. He explained that his work at the front was based on the position of the people. Initially, he faced some difficulties, but the government provided various conveniences such as transportation and passports. While he couldn't claim any significant achievements, he could reassure the people on three points: First, that the people would not submit to the violent Japanese; second, that the League of Nations would know that the Chinese people were still determined to resist; and third, that the righteous armies were lying in wait in the three northeastern provinces, causing the Japanese to be exhausted and unable to carry out their planned invasion. He attributed the failure of the righteous armies to a lack of coordination between the various forces and transportation difficulties, primarily due to a shortage of heavy-duty trucks, with most transportation relying on camels, which was extremely slow. Fortunately, important roads are now being built and made level. The front urgently needs heavy-duty trucks, and gasoline is also in short supply. Additionally, cooked food, shirts, shoes, and socks are all needed, and he urged the people to actively contribute. In conclusion, China now has only one way out: resistance. Failure to resist will inevitably lead to national subjugation. He mentioned that he would stay for another day or two before returning to the front to continue fighting the enemy. After Mr. Zhu's report, he was accompanied by members of the union's executive committee to the Club on Bazi Road for a visit and light refreshments. During the occasion, there was a detailed discussion on matters such as the dispatch of postal worker rescue teams to the front lines for rescue work.

Representative of the Jilin Self-Defense Army

Letter Reporting on the Recent Situation in Jilin Province 114

Mishan and Fujin Counties Have Been Recaptured by Our Army

The Daily News Agency reports that the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association in this city received a letter yesterday from the Jilin Self-Defense Army, Department of Li Du, represented by the □ Brigade Commander Chen Zongdai, who arrived in Ping from the Jiandao area. The letter reported that our army had recaptured Mishan and Fujin counties. The details regarding the current situation in Jilin Province are as follows:

Current Situation in Jilin Province: There are still over 30,000 soldiers in our army in eastern Jilin, including the □ Brigade of Xu Guoguang with over 3,000 soldiers stationed at □□ to guard the artillery camp. The □ Brigade of Chen Zongdai has five regiments, including the □ Regiment led by Sun Rongjiu, the □ Regiment led by Li Jiantang, the □ Regiment led by Li Huatang, the □ Regiment led by Zhang Shutian, and the □□□ Regiment led by Zhao Lianshan, totaling over 12,000 soldiers stationed in the □□□□□□□ three counties. In the middle, the □ Brigade of Lu Yongcai has over 4,000 soldiers stationed around □□□□□. The □ Road Commander Li Xiaotong has a force including the □ Regiment, the □ Detachment led by Wang Hongru, the □ Regiment led by Commander Fan, the □ Regiment led by Li Shaozong, the martial arts regiment led by Duan Yunge, and the □ Detachment led by Zhou Yunsheng, totaling 7,000 soldiers stationed at □□. The □ Detachment led by Wang Yong has over 4,000 soldiers stationed at □□. The armies have enough firearms, but a lack of ammunition and no source of supply. They are in remote mountainous areas with sparse population, making it difficult to obtain supplies. They endure cold and hunger, yet vow to remain steadfast and continue the cause of their predecessors. The armies are in contact with each other, waiting for an opportunity to strike at the enemy.

Battle Situation at the Front: My brigade is the □ Brigade of the Jilin Self-Defense Army, and I, Brigade Commander Chen Zongdai, courtesy name Dongshan, have followed General Commander Li for many years. I am loyal, brave, upright, and skilled in strategy. Since the September 18th Incident, I have been ordered to defend Yilan. Last March, I attacked the counties of Dalelemi, Fangzheng, and Yanshou, and recaptured them after over 20 days of fighting. In April, I attacked Zhuhe in a bloody battle lasting three days and nights, and it was captured. Later, the enemy mobilized large numbers of Japanese and puppet troops for reinforcements and counterattacks, with the support of airplanes and tanks. We were unable to resist due to the disparity in equipment and retreated to Liangzhuhe. After General Commander Li retreated to Tulongshan, I retreated to Boli County in May. The General Commander was stationed in Lishu Town. In August, the Japanese launched a general offensive on Boli. Our army swore to defend it and fought fiercely for four days and five nights, finally repelling the enemy. In November, Brigade Commander Ma Xianzhang of the Nalu Hasui Line Modao Shi was betrayed by Liu Wankui. The Japanese took the opportunity to invade on a large scale, with airplane bombing and armored vehicle pursuit. General Commander Li retreated into Russian territory when it became impossible to hold out. I was ordered to continue defending Boli. On the 14th day of the first lunar month this year, over 3,000 Japanese and puppet troops and 11 armored vehicles attacked. There was a fierce battle at Sandao Gang, with several charges against the enemy. Over a dozen Japanese soldiers and 167 puppet soldiers were killed, and over 40 enemy horses were killed. On our side, one company commander was killed and four soldiers were wounded. After 11 days of fighting, we were unable to hold out due to worn-out equipment and exhausted ammunition, so we retreated to preserve our strength. The enemy pursued us to Boli and engaged in battle for one day, killing and wounding eight Japanese soldiers. We then retreated to the mountainous area at the intersection of Qizihe and □□□□□□ counties, planning to coordinate with various armies for further action. On the 15th of this month, I, as a representative, arrived in Harbin and received a report that our army had recaptured Mishan and that Wang Yong's troops had occupied Fujin. The Japan-Manchukuo Daily News also reported this, stating that 18 Japanese heavy-duty trucks and over 100 Japanese soldiers were intercepted by our regiment commander Li Huatang between Dalelemi and Dongzigou, with all the Japanese soldiers being captured. The Japanese army is currently in a state of panic in Harbin, and the Japanese army does not dare to advance east.

Taking the Opportunity to Recover: I, as a representative, was ordered by Brigade Commander Chen to travel to Guan Nei to convey the recent situation at the front and request ammunition and supplies. I departed from Qizihe in Mishan territory on the 15th of this month in disguise and traveled to Harbin, then transferred to Dalian, and arrived in Ping yesterday. Currently, Yure is in a state of emergency, and the Japanese troops are all heading west. The eastern part of Jilin, including Mishan, Boli, Baoqing, Raoyang, Hulin, Tongjiang, Fujin, Zhechuan, Yilan, Fangzheng, Bin County, Zhuhe, and Yanshou counties, is sparsely populated, with only about 1,000 Japanese soldiers and about 30,000 puppet soldiers. It is possible to take this opportunity to rise up and recover the lost territories, but there is a lack of ammunition, clothing, and food. Although the villagers express sympathy, they are unable to provide supplies due to years of disasters, and the soldiers are extremely impoverished. We earnestly request the rapid arrangement of relief measures in order to coordinate the various departments for large-scale activities and to recover the lost territories.

Chen Youren's Advice

Indians Boycott Japanese Goods 115

The Japanese Dominate Asia

China and India Are Under Threat

The Guomin News Agency reports that Chen Youren, former Minister of Foreign Affairs of the National Government, recently stated that the United States has an obligation and responsibility to assist China, which was published in various Chinese and foreign newspapers. Yesterday, he wrote another article elaborating on the Manchurian issue and the relationship to the future defense of India, calling on the Indian people to unanimously boycott violent Japan. The original text is as follows:

Japan's attempt to destroy the international system that has always maintained China's territorial and administrative integrity is of great importance to India, especially to the Indian National Congress. The British began with the conquest of India, followed by the force of historical evolution, becoming custodians. When this custodial task is completed, there will inevitably be a day when they withdraw from India. Moreover, in the face of revolutionary changes that are about to change the existing social order around the world, the event is becoming increasingly urgent. The British abandonment of Indian rule will not be far off. Once realized, the problem of defending India from aggression will arise. In the past, those who invaded India either came overland from the northwest or crossed the sea from the west. However, from now on, once India's independence is realized and the true government controlling the peninsula is transferred into the hands of Indians, the land danger will only be the invasion of border barbarians. A small number of advanced mechanized troops, with elite aviation as the main force, will be more than enough to deal with it. However, the danger at sea is far more terrifying. At that time, it will no longer come from the west but from the east, threatened by the power of the Japanese navy. Since the Anglo-Japanese Alliance was first renewed in 1905 and renewed a second time in 1911, India has officially entered the orbit of Japanese naval power. Later, as a result of the Indian boycott of British goods and the Chinese boycott of Japanese goods, Japan's trade in India made astonishing progress. Therefore, the relationship between the Japanese naval power and India became increasingly deep-rooted and difficult to eliminate. China's boycott of Japanese goods in order to resist Japan's military aggression in Manchuria is necessary because China's purchase of Japanese goods is tantamount to suicide, providing the Japanese with funds for the war to conquer China. However, the losses suffered by Japan from the Chinese boycott are now being compensated in India. Today, the Indian market is as important to Japan as the Chinese market, and it will gradually occupy a very important position in the Japanese industrial and commercial economy. Just as Manchuria is called Japan's lifeline, it is not impossible for India to be called Japan's other lifeline. From this perspective, Japan's hegemony over the Asian continent will also pose the same dangers to India as those encountered by China.

By then, preventing the development of Indian industry so as not to hinder Japan's complete exploitation of the Indian market will be an important interest for the Japanese. However, the Japanese plan to obtain control of India in the future naturally does not intend to transplant its surplus population, because India has no open land for the Japanese to live in. Therefore, the main purpose of its plot in India is to occupy the complete monopoly of the Indian market in the future and prevent India from becoming an industrialized country, so that what India makes itself will not compete with Japanese goods even in its own market. If Japan's war of conquest against China is successful today, then after the British abandon their rule over India in the future, Japan can obtain military advantages and material resources to invade India (considering the necessity of the Indian market for Japanese industry, this move is inevitable). It is expected that the Indian people, especially the nationalistic Indian people, will be able to clearly understand that the Manchurian issue is of great importance to India's freedom and security. If the Indian people allow the Japanese to invade their markets to facilitate the Japanese conquest of China, China will inevitably suffer fatal disasters. However, if China suffers today, India will suffer the same tomorrow. If the Indian people can cooperate with China to jointly boycott Japanese goods, even if this move is enough to alleviate the Indian boycott of British goods (in fact, this move is no longer necessary for the Indian people to promote independence), and when danger comes in the future, there will be a powerful China to help India by attacking the Japanese invasion of India from the side. This move is deeply related to the whole of India. Therefore, I request that the nationalistic elements of India, through the National Congress, mobilize the Indian people to truly understand the threat of Japan to Asia and jointly shoulder the work of the government. I also ask other Indians in the parliament to raise the issue of Japanese aggression, regarding it as affecting the current economic security and future national defense, as an important issue for India today. This is what we Chinese people are looking forward to immensely today.

Aviation to Save the Nation Movement

The Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Townsmen Association's Aviation to Save the Nation Fundraising Committee has set up a basic team for the sake of concentrating its forces. Each team is responsible for raising over 5,000 yuan. It is heard that the various basic teams of the association are actively raising funds, and the amount paid in as of yesterday has reached over 50,000 yuan. French Army Conducts Simulated War Exercises 118

Army Commander Laipangna Explains the Process

The Zilin News reports that yesterday (the 1st) afternoon, near Jiaotong University, the sound of machine guns and artillery fire was suddenly heard for about half an hour. However, no bullets were seen flying out. It turned out that the French army was conducting a simulated war exercise, and all the ammunition fired was blank. Later, after the enemy was driven out of the boundary and the defending army won, Colonel Laipangna, the French army commander stationed in Shanghai, gathered his subordinates to explain the simulated war exercise. According to his plan, it was assumed that the enemy invaded the French Concession from Columbia Road, penetrated 500 meters into Haig Road. The infantry defending the concession was divided into two teams to resist. However, because the enemy had set up three machine gun nests and several light artillery positions, they could not repel the enemy, so they urgently summoned tank assistance. Five tanks arrived at 2:30 PM, and the simulated war exercise began. The tanks were then divided into two groups to destroy the enemy's formations in the open areas north and south of the road. The infantry followed, but after advancing about 100 meters, the infantry was blocked by enemy fire because the tanks failed to detect two enemy machine gun nests. Therefore, three tanks returned to eliminate the machine gun nests after driving back most of the enemy, and two tanks pretended to be damaged and raised yellow flags. After the two machine gun nests were eliminated, the tanks rushed forward again, and the infantry followed. Subsequently, there were no more major difficulties. They recaptured the remaining 400 meters and drove the enemy west of Haig Road. The main purpose of this exercise was to test the effectiveness of the tanks. Several officers from the US Marine Corps were also sent to observe.

Wu Kaisheng's Speech

The International Situation and Our National Policy 119

Maintaining Treaties on the One Hand and Recovering Lost Territory on the Other

We Can Only Face Japan If We Unite With All Countries

Yesterday afternoon, Wu Kaisheng, a secretary of the League of Nations, gave a speech at the Shanghai People's Education Center on the diplomatic policies that our country should adopt in the future and the diplomacy that our country should use to deal with Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations. A reporter from the Huadong News Agency recorded his speech as follows:

Classification of International Diplomacy: From the closed-door era to the present, relations between countries have developed, and international negotiations have arisen accordingly. The policies adopted internationally are, first, to befriend distant countries and attack nearby ones. Japan's diplomacy takes this approach, attacking China nearby and befriending Europe and the United States from afar. As for the policies of the European countries, they take the approach of befriending nearby countries and attacking distant ones. The recent meeting between British Prime Minister MacDonald and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini discussed the following issues: 1. Revising the Treaty of Versailles to achieve equality in German armaments; 2. Adopting a consistent trend in colonial policies toward countries outside of Europe. This is the approach of attacking nearby countries and befriending distant ones.

Trends in Diplomatic Policy: International diplomacy initially tended toward alliances, such as the Franco-Belgian alliance, the German-Austrian alliance, and the Anglo-American alliance before the war. However, because of alliances, wars broke out. Then, in 1914, the Paris Peace Conference was held, and US President Wilson advocated the organization of an alliance to have all countries around the world join hands to stop the war. If one country invaded another, all the others would come out to intervene. However, since the Sino-Japanese Incident, countries have once again felt the failure of the alliance policy. Thus, the trend in diplomacy has shifted from alliance to friendship, such as the recent Anglo-Italian fraternization.

Form of Diplomatic Policy: Diplomatic forms are divided into four factions: (1) the Continental Faction; (2) the Anglo-American Faction; (3) the Non-European and American Faction (such as Russia, Turkey, Japan, etc.); (4) the South American Faction. The Continental Faction is led by France, and several countries in Europe, such as Romania, are under its control. Italy is extremely uneasy about France's hegemony in Europe, so it is helping Germany to revise the European war treaty with France. Italy also hopes that the French and German factions will compete again in order to solve its land development. However, France must maintain its position in Europe, so it is plotting to control the European continent, and thus the Italian-French situation may explode at any time. In such an environment in Europe, there is naturally no time to take care of the Far East issue. It only needs to express itself in the Sino-Japanese Incident. The Anglo-American Faction, the United States and the United Kingdom, are of the same race and have been inseparable in history. Although there are occasional conflicts in emotions, their rights abroad are the same. The reason why the United Kingdom and Japan are allied is that the United Kingdom wants to use Japan to obtain interests in East Asia, and Japan also wants to use the United Kingdom to control the United States. However, this is not the case now, because the United States is extremely concerned about Japan's hegemony in the Pacific, so it is actively cooperating with the United Kingdom. The United States' commercial rights in the Far East are not as good as Japan's, and it cannot deal with Japan, but if Japan forces it to the point of desperation, it may not be able to attack Japan and help China. The Non-European countries faction includes Russia, Turkey, Egypt, India, etc. Turkey and Russia are now close to each other after the two rose again after World War One. Russia and China are bordering countries, and it does not want Japan to monopolize its interests in Liaoning and Jilin. However, its Five-Year Plan has not been completely successful, and it is also under the control of the European Allies, so it dares not rashly wage war with Japan alone. This depends on what our country does. If our country is determined to resist Japan, Russia will definitely be able to help China. Although India and Egypt are alienated from China due to geographical relations, they are both oppressed nations and will naturally sympathize with China. In addition, there is the South American Faction, which is very far away from China and has been plagued by internal strife in recent years, so it can do nothing but help morally. However, our country should also pay attention because the commercial rights in the South Pacific in the future are related to our country. Outlook After Japan Withdraws from the League of Nations: The diplomatic situation after Japan withdraws from the League of Nations changes from unity to division. In other words, the diplomacy of the past was unified diplomacy, and the diplomacy of the future will be divided diplomacy. However, Japan is also aware of the diplomatic isolation after withdrawing from the League of Nations, so it is trying to remedy it by sending envoys to the United Kingdom, the Netherlands, the United States, and other countries to lobby for diplomatic assistance from various countries. But no matter what, the provisions of Articles 1 and 3 of the League of Nations Covenant (i.e., it must still comply with the provisions of the League of Nations Covenant within two years) must still be observed. Therefore, the direct conflict between the League of Nations and Japan in the future will be over the mandate of the islands in the South Pacific. Whether the mandated islands will be handed over to the League of Nations and whether the League of Nations will hand them over to Germany are all issues.

Our Diplomatic Policies: In such an unfavorable environment, our country's diplomatic policies must, on the one hand, maintain the League of Nations Treaty, and on the other hand, actively recover the lost territory. Whether all countries in the world will help our country because of the situation is a question that our country's diplomatic authorities urgently need to study. If there are those who help us now, then Japan's future will definitely fail.

How Will Our Country Deal With Japan?: How will our country deal with Japan? The most important thing is to unite with the countries of the world, most importantly the United States and Russia, and then the United Kingdom and even Germany and Italy. The United States does not want Japan to dominate the Pacific, and its psychology is the same as ours, so it will definitely be able to help us. Russia is very close to Liaoning and Jilin. When the Liaoning Incident occurs, Russia must come out and speak out. Although there are rifts between China and Russia, Russia will definitely sympathize with China between China, Russia, and Japan. The United Kingdom and Italy are each willing to occupy a seat in the Far East, and they are also willing to be friends with China. Germany is famous for its machinery, and if it can unite with Germany, it will definitely have direct and indirect benefits in military affairs.

Japan Is the One Who Created the Great War: In short, in the current world situation, if peaceful methods are ineffective in recovering Liaodong, then there is only recourse to force. If we are unfortunate enough to formally declare war, then our country will sacrifice because of this, and Japan's sacrifice will be even greater. In the future, the responsibility for creating the world war will of course be borne by Japan. On the one hand, we Chinese must have the ambition to recover the lost territory of the three northeastern provinces, and on the other hand, we must strive for world justice and humanity.

Qian Xin zhi Denies

[Rumors That the President of the Central Bank Will Be Replaced>

Yesterday's report said that Finance Minister Song Ziwen, who is currently in Beijing, feels that coordinating financial affairs is a heavy burden and intends to resign as president of the Central Bank, recommending former Vice Minister of Finance Qian Yongming to succeed him. He also said it would be appropriate to continue to have Song manage it. It is completely inaccurate that he will succeed him. Minister Song has not contacted him in any way. He is also a director of the Central Bank, and he is very busy with the duties of the Four Banks Reserve, so he has no time to hold other positions.

This spring, there was a grand plan for the old departments in Liaodong, but more than 20 comrades were arrested at the seaport in Dalian, and the military secrets were leaked, and everything turned into a soap bubble, which is regrettable. In the future, there will be other plans, and there will be developments in less than three months. Currently, the families of anti-Japanese comrades in Liaodong are having a difficult time in Ping, so I hope that you will provide extra relief. This is what I pray for. Tang Juwu, Commander of the Liaoning Ning People's Self-Defense Army, kowtows frugally.

Held at the蓬萊戲院

The government's emphasis on treating children well is because children are the vitality of the country and the life of the nation. Today's adults are the children of the past, and today's children will be the adults of the future. Children inherit the careers of adult society, continue to promote and create, maintain and promote the civilization of society. Their responsibilities are both heavy and great. Adults should respect and cherish them. At present, our country is in trouble, and most of the relief depends on adults. However, in order to permanently eliminate foreign aggression and promote national glory, it is necessary to do everything possible to plan for children all over the country, to ensure their survival and development, to strengthen their bodies and enlighten their minds, so as to achieve the permanent effect of internal security and external defense. Our bureau, etc., are aware of this, so we are happy to advocate and commemorate the commendable Children's Day. From now on, the organization for the permanent welfare of children in this city has been planned by our bureau, etc., and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval after being approved by the Preparatory Committee for the celebration of Children's Day. I am afraid that the parents of ordinary children in society are not yet fully aware of this, so this is a special announcement.

The Pickled Meat and Ham Industries

Actively Oppose Inspection 128

Telegram to the Industry to Advocate Unity

A Letter to Various Business Associations to Ask for Aid

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau is re-implementing the inspection of pickled meat and ham products. Although the fee has been reduced to 30 cents, the Pickled Meat and Ham Industry Association believes that this case has been ordered to be revoked by the Executive Yuan, so how can it be held again? Therefore, it actively opposes it. On the one hand, it urges the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to send a telegram to the Executive Yuan to request the fundamental revocation according to the previous approval. On the other hand, it sends a telegram to the industry in various places to advocate unity and to various business associations in this city to give sympathy and assistance. The two documents are as follows:

Telegram to Various Places Hangzhou, Suzhou, Jiaxing, Shandong, Rizhao, Nanjing, Yangzhou, Jinhua, Lanxi, Rugao, Taixing, Linpu, Dongyang, Yiwu, Pujiang, Yongkang, Local Pickled Meat and Ham Industry Associations, Greetings. Since the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau last year intended to implement the inspection of pickled meat and ham products, our association, etc., believes that this matter is not necessary to be held. We have stated the reasons and requested the revocation, but we have not been invited to approve it. Therefore, our association had no choice but to send representatives to Beijing to petition. The Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Industry approved the order to revoke it in accordance with laws and regulations. Unexpectedly, within just three months of the approval, the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau issued a notice on March 30 that it would implement the inspection from April 1st. There were only two days between the announcement and the date of implementation, and our industry, etc., was not notified in advance. The matter was rushed and surprising. If various places follow suit, one place for one inspection and one place for one fee, then the burden will be ten times greater than the previous likin. For the sake of the future of the industry, in addition to urging the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to uphold justice based on the facts, we are sending a special telegram to you, hoping that your industry will jointly strive for this matter of vital interest to achieve the purpose of revocation. This is very much expected. We respectfully send this telegram and wait for a reply. Shanghai Pickled Meat and Ham Industry Association, respectfully.

A Letter to Various Associations To All Industry Associations in the City, Greetings. Respectfully, our industry is unfortunate because the commodities it operates are suddenly being paid special attention by the Municipal Health Bureau, which intends to implement inspection work, and before the goods enter the market, an inspection fee of 50 cents per 100 catties must be paid first. Our industry still believes that when the two kinds of foods, pickled meat and ham, are collected and made, they are salted and soaked once in a tank and exposed to the sun once, so they can be stored for a long time and there is nothing unsanitary about them. Moreover, according to our country's customs, ham is the only side dish for those who are sick, so our association has repeatedly called for the revocation based on the facts. Later, the Ministry of Industry and the Executive Yuan approved the revocation in accordance with the Commodity Inspection Law (the original approval photo is attached separately). However, the Municipal Health Bureau insisted on doing it, so the inspection facilities were re-implemented in this city just three days after the approval. Orders were changed in the morning and evening, disregarding national credibility and commercial difficulties. There are so many kinds of food, and if pickled meat and ham are to be inspected, then what cannot be inspected? Moreover, inspection must charge a fee. One place makes a start and four places follow suit, fearing that its abuses will be ten times greater than the previous likin. Therefore, in addition to requesting the administrative authorities to maintain the previous approval and fundamentally revoke it based on the facts, our association sends a special letter to you, asking you to take the position of the business community and give sympathy and assistance. We cannot express enough hope, and we respectfully wish you good luck. (The following is omitted)

(Notice to the Whole City) Municipal Public Security Bureau Director Wen Hongen, Social Affairs Bureau Director Wu Xingya, Health Bureau Director Li Ting'an, and Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan yesterday also jointly issued a letter to the parents of children throughout the city (details omitted above). The government's emphasis on treating children well is because children are the vitality of the country and the life of the nation. Today's adults are the children of the past, and today's children will be the adults of the future. Children inherit the careers of adult society, continue to promote and create, maintain and promote the civilization of society. Their responsibilities are both heavy and great. Adults should respect and cherish them. At present, our country is in trouble, and most of the relief depends on adults. However, in order to permanently eliminate foreign aggression and promote national glory, it is necessary to do everything possible to plan for children all over the country, to ensure their survival and development, to strengthen their bodies and enlighten their minds, so as to achieve the permanent effect of internal security and external defense. Our bureau, etc., are aware of this, so we are happy to advocate and commemorate the commendable Children's Day. From now on, the organization for the permanent welfare of children in this city has been planned by our bureau, etc., and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval after being approved by the Preparatory Committee for the celebration of Children's Day. I am afraid that the parents of ordinary children in society are not yet fully aware of this, so this is a special announcement.

For the sake of the future of the industry, in addition to urging the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to uphold justice based on the facts, we are sending a special telegram to you, hoping that your industry will jointly strive for this matter of vital interest to achieve the purpose of revocation. This is very much expected. We respectfully send this telegram and wait for a reply. Shanghai Pickled Meat and Ham Industry Association, respectfully.

A Letter to Various Associations To All Industry Associations in the City, Greetings. Respectfully, our industry is unfortunate because the commodities it operates are suddenly being paid special attention by the Municipal Health Bureau, which intends to implement inspection work, and before the goods enter the market, an inspection fee of 50 cents per 100 catties must be paid first. Our industry still believes that when the two kinds of foods, pickled meat and ham, are collected and made, they are salted and soaked once in a tank and exposed to the sun once, so they can be stored for a long time and there is nothing unsanitary about them. Moreover, according to our country's customs, ham is the only side dish for those who are sick, so our association has repeatedly called for the revocation based on the facts. Later, the Ministry of Industry and the Executive Yuan approved the revocation in accordance with the Commodity Inspection Law (the original approval photo is attached separately). However, the Municipal Health Bureau insisted on doing it, so the inspection facilities were re-implemented in this city just three days after the approval. Orders were changed in the morning and evening, disregarding national credibility and commercial difficulties. There are so many kinds of food, and if pickled meat and ham are to be inspected, then what cannot be inspected? Moreover, inspection must charge a fee. One place makes a start and four places follow suit, fearing that its abuses will be ten times greater than the previous likin. Therefore, in addition to requesting the administrative authorities to maintain the previous approval and fundamentally revoke it, our association sends a special letter to you, asking you to take the position of the business community and give sympathy and assistance. We cannot express enough hope, and we respectfully wish you good luck. (The following is omitted)

Records of Whereabouts of People of the Time 131

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Submits to the Municipal Government 132

Expanding the Education of Merchants in Pudong

Approving the Appropriation of Incense Money from the Emperor-Given Yangdian Temple

To Run Schools with Funds from Superstition

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted to the Municipal Government yesterday, saying: "Submitting a case based on the facts, on March 31, Xia Xinzai, director of the Pudong branch office, reported that Pudong is densely populated, the people are closed-minded, commercial knowledge is naive, and there are many illiterate laborers. The reason is that education has not been popularized. With such a large Pudong, there is only one municipal junior high school, which is limited by funding. The school building is simple and has not yet been built, let alone expanded. Puxi is separated by a river, and schools are lined up, but the expenses are high, which is not affordable for the general small commercial class in Pudong, resulting in more out-of-school youths and more illiterate people. To popularize local education, it is impossible to succeed without allocating the local public funds to supplement the municipal treasury. It is found that the annual incense money income of the Emperor-Given Yangdian Temple in Pudong is about 3,000 yuan. The temple management committee has been established for more than two years, and the accumulated funds are quite considerable. No one knows the bottom line of how they are used. I think this superstitious incense money is one of the local public funds income. If it can be allocated to local education, the public funds will not be wasted, and the local people will benefit. Moreover, the development of education and the revitalization of commerce are closely related. At this time, the world's commercial war is advancing day by day. Looking back at our country, it is as old as ever and as closed-minded as ever. It is urgent to find ways to increase the knowledge of merchants and popularize merchant education, so that we can compete for survival. Otherwise, there is no way to save it. I would like to briefly state my humble opinion and ask your association to forward it to the Municipal Government for approval, so that all the annual incense money income of the Emperor-Given Yangdian Temple can be allocated to local education, so that the future of commerce will be greatly benefited."

Two Young People Commit Suicide 134

Both Choose Inns as Places for Suicide

One Swallow Opium and One Take Sleeping Pills

Wang Huimin 135

Wang Huimin, a native of Zhejiang, is 35 years old. He used to run a photography and film business, but he has been unemployed for more than a year. The day before yesterday (the 31st), Wang suddenly went to the China Hotel on Zhejiang Road alone and opened room 52 to spend the night alone. The night before, he returned to his residence from outside and suddenly swallowed a large amount of opium and waited for death behind closed doors. It was not until 8:00 AM yesterday that the tea servant discovered it and immediately reported it to the police station. The detective rushed to investigate and quickly sent him to the Renji Hospital for treatment. However, because he was deeply poisoned, he died at 4:00 PM. The body was carried to the Feilun Road morgue for examination. A card from a friend who opened a coffin shop at Xinzha Bridge was found in the deceased's Yuan Se Mao Ge cotton-padded jacket. The detective went to check the address and claimed that the deceased was indeed a friend, but there was no deep friendship. Now that he has committed suicide, he can only donate a coffin to show friendship. As for the reason for the suicide, it is thought that it was caused by the torment of the disease and economic difficulties.

Tong Wenming 136

Tong Wenming, a local, is 35 years old and used to run a coarse cloth business. The night before, Tong went to room 24 of the Laoxingfa Inn at 36 Mantingfang alone. At that time, he paid the room fee of 42 cents and then closed the door to sleep. At about 11:00 AM yesterday, the tea room routinely called the guest and saw that Tong was lying stiff on the bed with a pale face and unconscious. He immediately reported to the Qianlaozha police station. The detective rushed to investigate and saw that Tong was wearing a fake华达呢棉袍 and a single呢长衫. A bottle of sleeping pill water was found on the small table. It was undoubtedly Tong who had secretly taken suicide. He was immediately sent to the Renji Hospital. It is said that he was deeply poisoned and there was a danger of death.

Shanghai Will Have a Special Hospital for the Mentally Ill 138

There are many hospitals in Shanghai, but there is still a lack of specialized treatment places for both mental and physical insanity. In recent years, there have been frequent national disasters and many unemployed people. There are often those who are troubled by circumstances, feel external pressure, and become mentally ill due to worry and anxiety. If they are not treated immediately, they will become disabled if they are mild, and lose their lives if they are severe. Recently, it has been heard that philanthropists Yuan Xilian, Xu Zhimo, Xie Qiangong, Qiao Nianchun, Pan Yulin, Chen Peng, Pan Shiqing, etc., have discussed with Dr. Gu Wenjun, a specialist in the treatment of mental illness, to initiate the establishment of a specialized hospital for mental illness. Rare Treasures 140

Jadeite Trio Shipped to America for Exhibition

Bao Pagoda, Palace Lantern, and Archway Crafted Over a Decade

Hundreds of Jade Artisans' Exquisite Carvings Praised as Divine Skill

Zhang Wendi, a jade merchant from Wu County, spent over a decade and employed hundreds of artisans to carve a jadeite Bao Pagoda, Palace Lantern, and Archway, which have now been completed. Their quality is excellent, and the carving is exquisite, truly a crystallization of Chinese jade carving. They will be shipped to America to be displayed at the Chicago Exposition. Yesterday, Mr. Zhang discussed the carving process as follows: In the spring of the fourth year of the Republic of China, mineralogists Li Benren and Liu Baoju discovered a massive jadeite boulder weighing approximately eight thousand kilograms deep in the jadeite mountains of Burma. Initially, it was difficult to assess its internal quality due to the surrounding sand skin and yellow crust. However, upon dissection, it was found to be of excellent quality, complete, and with few flaws, and a portion was

Covered in Vivid Green 141

Truly a rare treasure. Over several years, it was divided into thirteen pieces of various sizes to await a good price. I was immediately astonished by this extraordinary item and spared no expense in selecting the five most outstanding pieces, totaling slightly less than three thousand kilograms. After careful dissection, I obtained 0.4 cubic meters of pure jadeite. The color was vivid, and the texture was delicate and fine. I thought to myself that having obtained such extraordinary material, it must be subjected to extraordinary craftsmanship and carved into exquisite artifacts for the appreciation of the world, so as not to fail this rare and precious material. Only skilled jade artisans can utilize the properties of jadeite, removing its flaws and preserving its beauty, allowing its natural beauty to be fully revealed without any waste. However, this requires not only rich intellect and experience. The selection of art pieces values originality and avoids uniformity and imitation. It must adopt

Artistic Splendor 142

And cultural value to be considered qualified. The Bao Pagoda is a relic that originated from Buddhism and flourished in the Six Dynasties, Tang, and Song dynasties. In ancient times, people built pagodas to commemorate parental kindness and express filial piety. Today, people also build pagodas to praise achievements and express admiration. Its solemn and wondrous appearance has long been familiar to the minds of the Chinese people. As for the styles, whether square, round, angular, seven-tiered, or nine-tiered, they all uniquely express the unparalleled ancient Chinese artistic ideas. Furthermore, the Palace Lantern is an item whose system originated in the early Han Dynasty and reached its peak in the Tang Dynasty. Its style is ancient and elegant, rich but not vulgar, and it is sufficient to represent the Chinese people's dignified demeanor and noble nature. Moreover, I thought that the old-style Chinese archways were an immortal commemoration of loyalty, filial piety, integrity, and righteousness, used to

Maintain Morals and Ethics 143

The exquisite structure also sufficiently demonstrates the ancients' heroic, solemn, and respectful thoughts and spirit. However, these three items require materials that are difficult to match and construction that is not easy to fulfill. If made of jade, even the smaller ones, no one has ever dared to attempt it. Fortunately, I obtained this beautiful jadeite material and predicted that the raw materials would be roughly sufficient for these three items. Driven by curiosity, I braved difficulties and engaged in carving. Once the goal was set, I began collecting dozens of drawings and carefully examining them, selecting the most outstanding styles as blueprints. I then made detailed modifications with the guidance of Mr. Wu Baolin, Mr. Ma Gongfu, and Mr. Xu Shaoxian, incorporating my own ideas to create drawings and samples, considering the various possible ranges of polishing, carving, assembly, and disassembly, ensuring ease of placement and storage. On one hand, I exhausted my thoughts and calculated the materials to ensure that the grandeur of the volume would match my ideal. On the other hand, I sought out skilled artisans to

Research Carving Methods 144

Hoping to reach the pinnacle and be unparalleled in the world. However, the appearance and content of jade and stone often do not match, and there are often protrusions and deformities. Cutting out regular materials results in a lot of waste. Therefore, jade artisans usually carve objects according to their shape. Now, these three are all regular items that do not allow for the slightest deviation. The archway alone is very difficult, let alone the seven tiers of the Bao Pagoda, which have a fixed proportion in size, and the two covers of the Palace Lantern, which are even more difficult to ensure are pure and flawless. While the larger ones can be made smaller, how can broken ones be rejoined? The great danger is truly frightening, causing hesitation for a long time. Then I thought that to create extraordinary artifacts, one must experience extraordinary difficulties, so I resolutely proceeded with my business and carefully engaged in dissection. Whenever encountering an important connection, my heart would tremble as if hanging a banner. Passing through one difficult hurdle brings one joy. This went on for months and years. Fortunately, thanks to Heaven's blessing, the various materials were mostly prepared,

Without the Slightest Regret 145

It can be said that the height of the Bao Pagoda can reach one meter and twelve centimeters, and the diameter of its roof is slightly more than one-third of a meter. The total height of the Palace Lantern is more than half a meter, and the diameter of its two covers is nearly one-quarter of a meter, completely covered in green without any flaws. The archway is as high as 41% of a meter and nearly half a meter wide. The materials are uniform in color and brilliant in color. Such a fine product has never been seen or heard of in my life. At this time, even the most extravagant writing is not easy to describe it. Li Hanchen from Beiping, the number one jade artisan, respected throughout the country, was sincerely introduced by Mr. Cheng Shixiang and hired with heavy capital to take full responsibility for supervision. I also recruited hundreds of skilled artisans with specialized expertise, giving them generous wages to relieve them of their livelihood concerns, allowing them to concentrate on their work and seek perfection. Therefore, the Bao Pagoda carved by them is uniform and consistent, without the slightest deviation or inclination. The bells on each of its eight corners are carved from the pagoda itself, and the close structure and exquisite construction of its dougong brackets are breathtaking everywhere,

Praised as Divine Skill 146

The Palace Lantern is not only elegant in style, but also exquisitely carved with figures, each lifelike and beautiful, surpassing ancient works of art. The beauty and perfection of the archway is even more so. When the project was completed, it was placed in the hall and illuminated with electric lights, emitting a great light. I stared attentively and imagined with rapt attention. The successful completion was truly something to be proud of. It can be called the "Trio of Wonders", and I am not exaggerating. Recalling the past, I spared no expense to purchase this natural giant jadeite boulder, nor did I skimp on extravagant wages to gather hundreds of skilled artisans from all over the country, each of whom exhausted their thoughts and talents, working for nearly ten years to achieve perfection and beauty, combining fine jade and skilled artisans to create this unprecedented masterpiece. Overjoyed, I describe the process to art connoisseurs at home and abroad.

Guangdong Youth Exploration Team

Chen Yiqin Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 147

Traveled for Years Across Guangdong, Fujian, and Zhejiang Provinces

Plans to Go North to Join Teacher Weng's Work

Chen Yiqin, the leader of the Chinese Youth World Exploration Team, arrived in Shanghai by train from Hangzhou yesterday morning. A reporter from the Riri News interviewed Mr. Chen at his lodging yesterday. He spoke in detail about the organization process, travel situation, and future plans, which are recorded below.

Organization Process 148

I grew up in Hong Kong and graduated from an English-language secondary school. I often saw Westerners organizing exploration teams to search for historical sites not witnessed by modern people in various places. This kind of adventurous undertaking is commonplace and unremarkable for people in their countries. However, looking around our country, there are very few organizations of this kind. I have always admired exploration and have been influenced by books such as adventure. Therefore, when the January 28th Songhu Anti-Japanese War broke out last year, I invited several classmates to go to the rear office of the 19th Route Army, abandoning my studies to join the army. My request was not approved, so I returned to Hong Kong with my companions and organized an exploration team. The purpose was to: (1) Seek out secluded and mysterious places to advocate the dumb mysteries of hundreds of years ago; (2) Investigate local customs and compile them into magazines; (3) Photograph strange activities on the spot and fearlessly gain experience to save China's precarious country. I plan to contribute what I have learned to people all over the world in the future.

Travel Experience 149

In June of last year, I planned to hire four local porters with my younger brother Yike, my sister, and myself, to divide up the luggage and start organizing this team. After leaving our hometown in Zhongshan County, my younger brother Yike was seriously injured when he ventured to photograph the Huangchao Cave waterfall and lost his footing in the rock. He was escorted back to Hong Kong by my sister for treatment, but it was ineffective and he died. My sister also stopped moving forward because she could not stand the mountain mist and miasma. I had no choice but to stop the trip. However, my ambition did not diminish. I re-solicited comrades in Hong Kong: Lin Xiehe, Feng Yaozong, Li Yuanzhu, Zeng Lirong, Song Jinming, Cen Yaman, and others. Eight people set off again in December. When we arrived at Kowloon Mountain, Shatin, and Tai Po, Song and Zeng returned halfway because they could not endure the hardship. After passing through Guangzhou to Huiyang, Feng and Li also quit, leaving only Mr. Lin, Ms. Cen, and myself. When we set off, we had a lot of luggage. At that time, we hired four local porters. Unexpectedly, when we arrived in the Hailufeng area, we encountered bandits. We immediately fought the bandits. Mr. Cen was killed by the bandits first. All the materials we searched for and the accompanying moving cameras, guns, cameras, curtains, clothing, passports, etc. were looted, resulting in a loss of more than 4,000 yuan. Mr. Lin and I were also arrested. We escaped to Shantou penniless. We sought travel expenses and planned to return to Hong Kong to stop moving forward. Later, the Shantou Bureau persuaded us and provided us with a lot of money. After experiencing security, Yunxiao, Zhangpu, Zhangzhou, and Haicheng, we arrived in Xiamen. Because we received too many travel supplies from various agencies and groups along the way, we hired local porters. Fortunately, Huang Zhichang from Xiamen volunteered to take on the task. Therefore, we passed through Tongan, Quanzhou, Huian, Putian, and Fuqing to Fuzhou. After arriving in Fuzhou, Mr. Huang was too tired and was admitted to the hospital for treatment, so we stopped again. When we set off from Fuzhou, a student from Fujian, Huang Changli, joined us. When we arrived in Wenzhou, we could not reach Ningbo and also returned halfway because we could not endure the hardship. Considering the national crisis, I planned to temporarily reorganize. When I arrived in Fuzhou, I had asked General Cai Tingkai, the Director of the Pacification Commissioner's Office in Fujian, to change my passport and go straight to the Northeast to participate in the Anti-Japanese War. Later, I passed through Wenzhou, Taizhou, and Ningbo to Hangzhou. After arriving in Hangzhou, Mr. Lin withdrew again. However, I am willing to do my best to move forward and will not temporarily stop because my comrades have retreated. Therefore, I came to Shanghai alone by train from Hangzhou. I stayed for a day or two to ask various agencies and groups to stamp their seals to keep as a souvenir. Then I followed Nanjing to the Northeast.

Perseverance 150

Mr. Chen is from Zhongshan, Guangdong. He is young, heroic, lively, and able to endure hardship. He continued his second attempt after the first failure. He has overcome many twists and turns along the way. He is truly a rare modern young man. All travel expenses for the exploration team in the past were self-funded and self-prepared. He also signed a contract with the Hong Kong and Guangzhou Weifeng Public Review newspapers to send photos and texts every week. Now, because it cannot be implemented, it is difficult to realize the reward of sending money from the two newspapers once every half month. Before the disaster, the purpose was to seek out secluded and scenic spots and explore ancient sites. Therefore, the places we passed through were mostly remote mountains and rocks, and we had to explore them. The cities we passed through were nothing more than purchasing supplies, receiving mail, and conducting investigations. Now, because the property was looted at one time, the economy is very panic. Therefore, we have to call for help everywhere we arrive. From Shantou to this place, we have relied on the help of local agencies, which is very grateful. Mr. Chen is scheduled to visit Mayor Wu of this city today, and then plans to go to Nanjing and then to Tianjin to join Teacher Weng Zhaoyuan and participate in the Anti-Japanese War.

An Elderly Man from Nanhui Dies in a Car Accident 155

Cui Yuanchong, a 20-year-old driver from Yangzhou, drove his private car No. 6024, owned by a British man named Mai Ding, through Feilu Road in the French Concession from west to east at 9:15 a.m. the other day. In front of door number 1004, Wang Amiao, an elderly man from Nanhui in his sixties, was crossing the road from the south to the north. Cui's car could not avoid him and knocked him down, injuring his head and causing him to lose consciousness. The police saw him, rushed to record the number, woke Wang, and sent him to Guangci Hospital. Due to his old age and serious injuries, the treatment was ineffective, and he died that afternoon. The hospital notified the police station, who took the body and car to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall for an autopsy. The next day, the Traffic Management Office reported to the Second Special District Court, which appointed Prosecutor Deng Baosun to conduct an autopsy. After confirming that Wang Amiao had died from a car accident, the court ruled that the body should be collected by Wang Yousheng, the son of the deceased. The defendant was returned to the Traffic Management Office for questioning. The police station will send the defendant to the court for questioning today.

Zhabei Fire Report 156

Haichang Road, Zhabei The two storefronts at 251-253 Haichang Road, opened by Gao Jialin from Anhui, are the Sanyixing Fried Noodles Restaurant. This morning at 1:15 a.m., a fire broke out, and the smoke and flames quickly spread, burning down a total of six houses, including Gao Jialin's fried noodles restaurant at 249, 255, 257, and 259 next door. The fire was extinguished at 3:30 a.m. after the fire department rushed to put it out. When the fire broke out, Gao Jialin was out, so the police took his accountant, Sun Yulin, to the 4th District Public Security Bureau for investigation. Gao's wife and seven-year-old son were terrified.

Huasheng Road, Zhabei At 11:30 a.m. yesterday, a fire broke out in a row of old buildings near the intersection of Guangfu Road and Huasheng Road, behind the famous Small Chimney Silk Factory, where Ni Dingxing and Xiao Shunxing No. 2 stored broken cloth and paper scraps. The fire quickly spread through the roof, and more than a dozen buildings were destroyed in an instant. Although fire engines from various sections rushed to the scene to try their best to put out the fire, they were unable to control it until about 2:30 p.m. When the reporter left the fire scene, the water was still raging. The 4th District Public Security Bureau arrested Xiao Panfu, a suspect who started the fire. He claimed to be a 48-year-old man from Changzhou who ran a used goods business and also stored broken cloth and other items in the house. However, he refused to reveal the cause of the fire. Zhongxing Road At around 9:00 a.m. yesterday, Zheng Jiasheng, a 42-year-old man from Shaoxing, opened a yarn dyeing factory at 1378 Zhongxing Road. Sparks from the chimney fell onto the reed mat shed while dyeing yarn, and it immediately caught fire. After the fire department from various sections drove the belt cars to put out the fire, three thatched sheds had been burned down. Zheng Jiasheng was subsequently arrested by the police and taken to the 4th District Public Security Bureau to await trial.

Lawyer Zheng Dingying Practices Law 157

Lawyer Zheng Dingying, also known as Yifan, is from a well-known family in Zhejiang. He graduated from the Department of Law of Chizhi University last year with a Bachelor of Laws degree. When he was at school, he immersed himself in the study of law and was admired by his classmates. He was also highly valued by the headmaster, Mr. He. After the September 18th Incident, he led all the students to work hard to resist Japan and did not spare any effort in running and calling. Clothing Store Apprentice Hangs Himself 158

Qian Minsheng, a 17-year-old apprentice from Changshu in the clothing store opened by Huang Ada at No. 18 Jinjiafang, South of Fangbang Bridge, has been an apprentice in the clothing store for four years. Yesterday, because the guest entrusted him to make a jacket, he was negligent and made the wrong size of the pants. When a dispute arose, his master Huang Ada happened to arrive in Shanghai from his hometown in Changshu and returned to the store, so he reprimanded his apprentice Qian Minsheng a few words. Unexpectedly, the apprentice was usually very depressed, so he was resentful and tired of the world. At about 1:00 a.m. yesterday morning, he hanged himself in the back of the store. Gu Han'gen, who lived with him, noticed it, but it was too late to save him. The store owner Huang Ada reported it to the 1st Section of the 2nd District, and the detective Zhu Songqing was sent to investigate everything. The local bail was reported for an autopsy. In the afternoon, the court sent a prosecutor to conduct an autopsy, and then ordered the store owner to prepare a coffin and collect the body, and ordered the store owner to wait for questioning.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Shandong coast would be cloudy with a fairly tight wind from the southwest to northwest.
