Reader Advisor

A Third Discussion on the Power of Supply and Western Civilization 166

丨Reply to Mr. Xu Xianfu of this city's letter丨

Answer: Your repeated letters "all have the masses of the nation in mind. All discussions, self-assessment, suicides, love, careers, inheritance and other issues are truly superior." Indeed, indeed! Therefore, our reply to you is tirelessly detailed, but due to the limited space of this column, we have not been able to exhaust all points, causing you to repeatedly explain. However, the more a principle is debated, the clearer it becomes, and the more an issue is analyzed, the more refined it becomes. We welcome your eloquent debate. However, looking at the recent two letters, there are too many things that should be discussed. Here are a few key points to discuss with you again.

(1) The previous letter said "This was a momentary feeling,"

And the letter of March 14th said, "The feeling in my first letter was a kind of strong 'expression' that arose after the accumulation of past 'feelings.'" Since this feeling was accumulated, it is not a "momentary feeling." Isn't this a bit contradictory? Feelings first, research later. This kind of fact may exist, but it is limited to simple and easily felt things. If your long discourse lists some statistics and cites many historical facts, this is not a simple feeling, but rather a "concept of national survival and national rise and fall" that can only be formed after considerable research. We are not ignoring feelings, but we feel that your statement is self-contradictory and does not escape the exaggeration of old scholars in China. You clearly wrote something with thought, but you insist on saying that it was written casually; you clearly researched it (at least to a considerable extent), but you insist on saying ... ... "We think this attitude is unacceptable, so we tell you this. As for your citing of classics, most of them are irrelevant. Fichte's Addresses to the German Nation were expressed with fervent emotions due to the defeat in the Battle of Jena, but they were not, as you said, a 'momentary feeling.' Fichte was a great philosopher of the time, rising after Kant. He must have thoroughly studied the ways of national rise and fall and national survival in peacetime, and then published his extremely valuable historical documents at the appropriate time. However, you use them as a defense for a 'momentary feeling' and writing things down haphazardly ... ... "This is wrong!

(2) Your first letter said: "Western civilization ... ... one is the power of supply, the other is the power of control." The second letter also said: "The division between capitalism and socialism lies only in the power of control." You also said: "The difference between capitalism and socialism lies only in the power to guide human evolution." In fact, the difference between socialism and capitalism lies not only in the power of control, but also in the power of supply. According to your explanation of "the power of supply": "The so-called power of supply is the invention of people's knowledge and skills, the control of nature, and the production of raw materials for human evolution ... ... ... ... "Simply put, it is controlling nature. That's right, controlling nature is necessary in capitalist society and in socialist society, but there is a quantitative difference between controlling nature in capitalist society and controlling nature in socialist society. Because capitalism cannot fully utilize science, materials, and the intelligence and talents of the majority of people, the power of socialism to control nature surpasses the power of capitalism to control nature, that is, it further develops the "power of supply." The difference in quantity develops to a certain extent, and then it becomes a qualitative difference. Therefore, after socialism is completed, humanity's only task is to conquer nature, that is, to control nature. Therefore, when we study the difference between capitalism and socialism, and forget the greatness of socialism's control of natural forces, that is, we forget a difference between it and capitalism, the result is that we will inevitably lose half of its true content. Otherwise, capitalist society certainly wants to control nature. Even in feudal society, wouldn't people want to control nature? A ship, an airplane, certainly controls nature. Isn't a wooden boat, a mule cart, also controlling nature? The only difference is that due to the difference in quantity, it reaches a certain degree and then becomes a qualitative difference, thus becoming a difference between capitalism and feudal economy. By analogy, this is true everywhere. You only see the power of capitalism to control nature, but you have no time to carefully study its dialectical changes, and thus ignore its great role in the difference between socialism and capitalism. Lenin once said that socialism is the dictatorship of the proletariat plus electrification, which has profound meaning. Of course, capitalist society also utilizes electricity, but socialism must utilize it to the greatest extent, from quantitative change to qualitative change. This is why it is different.

(4) We are not fundamentally opposed to youth, but we want to ask what kind of youth? Looking at your statement "public opinion advocates, youth leads, and the masses of laborers practice it, and then the revolution can be observed and accomplished," setting youth apart from the masses of laborers, the meaning is as if only people who have received higher education now can lead the revolution, and the masses of laborers are only obeying orders. This is completely unacceptable. The cultural level of the revolutionary masses cannot be proportional to the education of schools.

(5) The capitalism and socialism we are talking about refer to economic organizations and social organizations. Therefore, we can say that the economy of capitalism and the economy of socialism, or the society of capitalism and the society of socialism, or the country of capitalism and the country of socialism. The socialism we are talking about is a product of modern capitalist society, not Plato's Republic. They are a world apart, with no similarities at all. They must not be confused. There are only two futures for current society, one is capitalist society and the other is socialist society. There is no third road. However, you forcibly combine "social policies, fascism, and ideal reohnocracy, etc." and list them together. Social policy is a kind of social reformist policy adopted in capitalist countries. However, its political environment and economic organization are still capitalist. For example, Bismarck stole one or two points from the demands of the labor movement in the socialist theories of the time and changed them beyond recognition. This is his social policy. As for fascism, it is only a last struggle when capitalism reaches its end. Its society is still capitalist, because it further intensifies the oppression of the laboring masses. They cannot but compete for the market; they cannot but compete for colonies and divide the colonies. Mussolini's Italy is like this, and Hitler's Germany is also like this.

(6) You said that "Marx's materialist conception of history believes that capitalism will evolve to a period of natural collapse, the power of the proletariat will increase, and communist socialism will be realized." I am very ignorant of such a fresh Marx's materialist conception of history, and I have never read such a Marx's theory. I remember that Liang Qichao seemed to have such a view. After the end of the war, when he returned to China from Europe, he criticized the materialist conception of history, saying that since the materialist conception of history says that capitalism will inevitably collapse after it develops to a certain period, then we should just wait for it to collapse. Why do we still need to have a revolution? In fact, this is laziness, fatalism, not Marxism, not the materialist conception of history. Capitalist society does not "naturally collapse." It must be destroyed by human power before it can be both sent to its end and give birth to new life. Even more strangely, you said that "Lenin's Soviet Russia is no longer the communist society that Marx idealized." This is really wrong. Lenin's Soviet Russia is not a communist society. Where did you see Lenin say that Soviet Russia is a communist society? Your mistake lies in: 1. Not knowing the difference between the dictatorship of the proletariat and communist society: 2. Not knowing the society that Marx idealized as a communist society and the transitional social form (the stage of the dictatorship of the proletariat) that he used to achieve this society. Now try to tell me: What kind of society is the communist society that Marx idealized? How does he teach us to achieve this society? What kind of society is Lenin's Soviet Russia?

(7) The so-called national self-determination is the right of each nation to decide whether to join a certain national federation or withdraw from a certain country, and it does not mean that each nation has the right to decide on federal politics within a federation. You did not distinguish this point, so it is appropriate to mistakenly regard the constitutional provisions of federal administration as interfering with national self-determination. This is really deliberately nitpicking. To be honest, we study theory, recognize the facts, and we can go anywhere, do anything. However, when we criticize the Soviet Union, we should also reflect on ourselves. The various ethnic groups under the Soviet Republic are the true epitome of "national self-determination" in the world. You can understand this by reading Dewey's recollections after visiting the Soviet Union. Finally, I would also like to offer a word of advice. You are really a good student in Chinese universities now, at least in Shanghai universities. You have read some books, but they are disorganized, and your thoughts are confused as a result. It is best to read a few theoretical books first and clarify your thinking methods, so that you will not say one thing from the east and another from the west. However, I must repeat, you are indeed a good student in the university now!

Discussion Meeting on Astronomy, Mathematics, and Physics

More than 60 members attended丨General Assembly in the morning

Group meetings in the afternoon丨Ministry of Education banquet

In addition to more than ten experts and members such as Sa Mudong and Zhu Kezhen who explained in letters that they could not attend due to circumstances, more than 60 members actually attended. Members attending: Feng Zuxun, Hu Junji, Wang Shoujing, Jiang Zehan (Peking University), Sun Guangyuan, Zheng Zhiban, Wu Youxun, Zhou Peiyuan (Qinghua University of Peiping), Hu Gangfu, Ding Bianlin (Central Research Physics Institute), Xiao Junyuan, Tang Caozhen, Pan Zuwu, Zeng Zhaoan, Cha Qian (Wuhan University), Hu Wenyao (Shanghai Aurora), Lu Shuyin (Jinling Women's College of Arts and Sciences), Qian Baozong, Su Buqing, Zhang Shaozhong, Shu Xingbei (representative) (Zhejiang University), Zhang Yun, Huang Xun (Guangdong Zhongshan University), Tu Yuqing (Shanghai University), Zhao Zhongyao, Ni Shangda, Zhang Yuzhe, Fang Guangqi, Jiang Shaoji, Xu Renqian, Xu Yingqi, Zheng Yaoban (Central University), Li Shuhua, Rao Yutai, Yan Jici (Peiping Research Institute), Ding Zuocheng (Shanghai Dahua Scientific Instrument Company), Zhu Yongben (Beiyang Institute of Technology), Gu Jinghui, Jiang Lifu (Tianjin Nankai University), Chen Zunyan (Baoding College), Zhang Yihui, Fan Huiguo, Zhao Jinyi (Beijing Normal University), Xia Yuan (Peking University Women's College), Xu Guobao (Shanghai Jiaotong University), Hu Dunfu (Datong), Huang Jiyu (Qingdao Shandong University), Zhu Gongjin (Guanghua), Zhou Changshou (Daxia), Qi Kaizhi, Ding Xuxian (Anhui University), Zhu Wuhua (Tangshan Jiaotong University), Yang Jianchu, Dai Yuntian, Yu Guanglang, Wei Xueren (Jinling University), Li Mingzhong, Yu Qingsong (Astronomical Institute), Jiang Bingran (Qingdao Observatory), Cao Mo (General Bureau of Land Surveying), Sun Guofeng (Peking University Institute of Technology), Gu Cheng (Peking University Women's College of Arts and Sciences), Zhu Guangcai (Sino-French University), Gui Zhiting (Wuchang Central China University), Yu Dawei (Arsenal Physics and Chemistry Institute), Chen Zubing (Jinan), Gao Lu (Supervisory Yuan), Kang Qinggui (Translation and Compilation Bureau), and other 60 people.

General Assembly in the Morning: The meeting began at 9:30 AM, chaired by Minister of Education Zhu Jiahua, who explained the reasons for the meeting and said that the Ministry of Education had previously held a chemical discussion meeting and now a theological discussion meeting on astronomy. In the future, when the opportunity arises (such as during the summer vacation), it is also planned to hold discussion meetings on other subjects. In addition, regarding the research of various specialized societies, the Ministry of Education has asked the municipal government to find land to prepare for the construction of clubhouses as research institutions for technology. Zhu expressed his intention to be responsible. Then, Chen Kezhong, director of natural science at the National Translation and Compilation Bureau, reported on the preparations. Then, the method of dividing groups was discussed, and it was decided to divide into three groups: astronomy, mathematics, and physics. Photos were taken and the groups were divided. After a brief discussion, lunch was served.

Group Discussions: There were eight members in the Astronomy Group, including Yu Qingsong, Zhang Yuzhe, Zhang Yun, Cao Mo, Li Mingzhong, Chen Zunjiao, Gao Lu, and Jiang Bingran. They met in the guest room of the institute, chaired by Gao Lu and recorded by Li Guoding. The issue of astronomy courses was discussed, and it was decided that all universities should add astronomy courses, and high schools should also add an astronomy lesson. There were twelve members in the Mathematics Group, including Sun Xianyuan, Hu Wenyao, Hu Dunfu, Feng Zuxun, Yu Guanglang, Zeng Yiyi, Zheng Yaoban, Jiang Shaoji, Fan Huiguo, Zhu Gongjin, Xiao Junyuan, Su Buqing, Jiang Lifu, Qian Baozong, Jiang Zehan, Zheng Tongsun, Gu Cheng, Tang Caozhen, Zhao Jinyi, Huang Jiyu, Hu Junji, and Ding Xuxian. First, the proposals were divided into four categories: translation names, curriculum standards, compilation of good books, catalogs, and others. Feng Zuxun, Jiang Lifu, Huang Jiyu, and Zheng Tongsun were appointed as the presidium. There were thirty-two members in the Physics Group, including Ding Xielin, Zhang Yihui, Li Shuhua, Zhou Changshou, Zhu Guangcai, Hu Gangfu, Sun Guofeng, Zhou Peiyuan, Zhu Shuiben, Shu Xingbei, Yang Jianchu, Rao Yutai, Ding Zuocheng, Gu Jinghui, Xu Guobao, Lu Shuyin, Xia Yuanli, Xu Renqian, Chen Zubing, Zhao Zhongyao, Ni Shangda, Kang Qinggui, Dai Yunzhi, Wei Xueren, Huang Xun, Pan Zuwu, Zhu Wuhua, Gui Zhiting, Wu Youxun, Yan Jici, Wang Shoujing, and Fang Guangqi. Thirty-two people attended the meeting in the auditorium of the institute in the morning, chaired by Li Shuhua and recorded by Qian Baojun and Wang Zuoqing. It was decided not to divide into smaller groups and to appoint Fang Guangqi, Ding Xiezhu, Wei Ren, Wu Youxun, Zhou Changshou, and one other person as proposal review committee members. After the meeting, the proposal committee members decided to divide the proposals into seven categories: (1) translation names (2) curriculum standards (3) instrument manufacturing (4) list of books that must be compiled (5) national defense (6) popular science education (7) others, and set the discussion schedule for the group.

Group Meetings: Group meetings continued in the afternoon. Eight people attended the Astronomy Group meeting, which was still chaired by Gao Lu and recorded by Li Guoding. It was decided that four types of books must be compiled and the issue of astronomical translation names was discussed. Ministry of Education Banquet: It is also reported that the Ministry of Education specially hosted a banquet for the members of the association at the Overseas Chinese Hostel that evening to express its welcome.

Yesterday at 9:00 AM, the special expert meeting continued at Rong Hong Hall. Attendees included: Yu Yan, Director of the Business Department of the Ministry of Railways; Wang Shengshan, Chief of the Locomotive Department of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways; Zhao Zengjue, Director of the Zhejiang Telephone Bureau; Li Yunliang, Chief Auditor of the China Merchants Bureau; Kang Deli, Advisor to the Ministry of Railways; and Li Zhaohuan, President of the school; Zhong Weicheng, Dean of the Management College; Zhang Tingjin, Dean of the Electrical Engineering College; and Li Qian, Dean of the Civil Engineering College, along with professors from various colleges and experts from various fields, totaling over seventy people. Chairman Yu Yan discussed the scope of "Industry, Transportation, and Education." Subsequently, Mao Yisheng, Yu Tan, Wang Shengshan, Li Yunliang, and Zhao Zengjue each presented the main points of their prepared papers. Mao Yisheng's paper was titled "The Way Out for Chinese Industry." Yu Yan's paper was titled "The Relationship between Industry and Railways." Wang Shengshan's paper was titled "The Needs of Industry and Transportation in Relation to Education." Zhao Zengjue's paper was titled "The Current Status of Telecommunications in Zhejiang." The content of each was extremely profound. It is reported that the meeting intends to publish all the experts' papers in a special volume after the meeting.

Inauguration Ceremony of the Fountain 174

Yesterday at 2:00 PM, the inauguration ceremony of the Class of 1920 Fountain was held at Zhixin West Dormitory. More than thirty alumni, including Sun Jiaqian, Wang Zongyang, and Xiong Dahui, attended. Sun Jiaqian reported on the preparation process and its significance, briefly stating that the Class of 1920 decided to build a fountain in the west of Zhixin Dormitory upon graduation, with Sun Jiaqian, Wang Zongyang, and others responsible for the undertaking. Due to funding and contracting issues, the completion was delayed until today. The total cost of the project was approximately eight hundred yuan. Its significance is embodied in the four characters inscribed on the stone tablet: "When drinking water, think of the source." Next, Li Zhaohuan performed the unveiling ceremony, removing the national flag covering the school emblem in the pool, and then music was played to mark the completion of the ceremony.

Xiang Ling Technical Performance 175

Yesterday at 10:00 AM and 5:00 PM, at the gymnasium and Wen Zhi Tang, respectively, the Gemini Kings, Jin Youshen and Pu Ziheng, performed Xiang Ling (shuttlecock kicking) techniques. Mr. Jin carried a small wooden box containing five shuttlecocks, each six inches in size and in red, white, and blue, displayed on a table. Although the two gentlemen are advanced in years, their kicking skills were remarkable. Whether with foot, knee, head, or shoulder, no part of their body was unable to make contact with the shuttlecock. The styles included jumping, kicking, twirling, and [unclear], and the two men could kick the same shuttlecock in unison. While kicking, the shuttlecock appeared and disappeared, circling around the two gentlemen's front and back, with exquisite and unparalleled skill. It is reported that the two gentlemen came south at the invitation of Mr. Chu Minyi and held a shuttlecock competition in Nanjing, which was highly praised. This type of exercise is very hygienic, nourishing blood, strengthening the brain, and not straining the body. It is truly the most outstanding sport among national treasures.

Municipal Elementary Schools to Merge 177

Shangwen Elementary School expands ▲ First Shishi Elementary School to be abolished

The Shangwen Elementary School on Shangwen Road in Nanshi has seen considerable development in its school affairs in recent years. The original school buildings were insufficient, and the Municipal Education Bureau approved the allocation of the former County Education Bureau site and the First Public School campus to the school for the reconstruction of new school buildings. However, the First Experimental Elementary School still has students on campus, but their number is less than that of Shangwen. For the convenience of school management and development, the Municipal Education Bureau has decided to merge the First Shishi Elementary School into Shangwen Elementary School starting next semester.

The Shanghai Open Six-Mile Cross-Country Run was held yesterday at 11:00 AM in Hongkou Park. The Russian Emigrant Sports Association won the championship with 31 points. The French Army was second with 32 points, and the British Lancashire was third with 41 points. The individual championship was won by Lancashire's Grant with a time of 31 minutes and 47 seconds, about fifteen meters ahead of second-place Amany of the French team.

Bai Hong's Crushing Defeat

Starting Forward 180

At exactly 11:00 AM, the eighty athletes stood together at the west end of Hongkou Park, along the gate of the East Sports Association. As the pistol was fired, over one hundred and sixty swift feet raced west towards the Sports Association, turning onto East Sports Road and into the fields of Jiangwan. The Bai Hong generals were all in the lead. Wang Zhenglin and others, including Huang Shengbai, were slightly unwell midway, but still bravely pushed forward.

Mid-Course Situation 181

After crossing the fields, they turned east again, rejoining East Sports Road near Shuidaian Road, about four miles from the starting point and about two miles from the finish line. At that time, the leading person was Wang Zhenglin of Bai Hong, with the Russian Lifcuntsuv closely following three feet behind, and Dong Jiashe, also of Bai Hong, in third place.

A Major Mistake 182

At this crucial moment to determine the outcome, a huge mistake was discovered. Five or six people, including Wang and Dong, had taken the wrong route. After rejoining Sports Association Road, they should not have gone straight but should have turned again onto East Sports Association Road. Wang and others had to double back, covering thirty or forty meters unnecessarily. Grant, who was originally in seventh place, jumped to first place.

Impossible to Recover 183

Wang Zhenglin, Dong Jiashe, and the Russian Lifcuntsuv bravely chased after them. Lifcuntsuv still had energy to spare and gradually caught up with them, but Wang and Dong were limited by their strength and could not recover. When they reached the finish line, Lancashire's Grant of the British Army was fifteen meters ahead of the Frenchman Amany to take first place with a time of 31 minutes and 47 seconds. Kirat was only a hair's breadth behind Amany in third. Dong Jiashe was eighteenth, Huang Shengbai nineteenth, and Wang Zhenglin twenty-third. The first Chinese to arrive was Chen Xuzhou in fourteenth place.

Spring and Autumn

What Era Is This? 190

— Zhan Lu

In this day and age, southerners who were unwilling to serve the puppet government have successively returned home. One returning guest from Zhadong, amidst sighs, spoke of the corrupt officials in the Northeast before its fall who lacked common sense and were unaware of the global situation.

The officials in the Northeast only cared about flattering foreign powers and exploiting the people. They lacked all other common knowledge. There was a high-ranking official who could be considered relatively clear-headed among the Northeast officials. He familiarized himself with the drafts prepared by his secretary and could eloquently deliver speeches from the podium. One day, at a celebratory commemoration, many consular officials from foreign countries came to observe. He was again about to take the stage and show off his signature deceptive act. He did not use a draft prepared by his secretary, because he had recently read a booklet that he considered an excellent source of information for his speech. Thus, he boldly lectured on the global situation.

He was afraid that the foreign guests would not understand his wonderful arguments and that he would not be able to fully display his talents, so he ordered the interpreter to simultaneously translate his words into Western languages on the stage for the appreciation of blue-eyed people. He had a wonderful argument: "World civilization is advancing by leaps and bounds. In the past, aerial warfare required huge amounts of bombs to bombard enemy positions. Now, new British aircraft only need to pour some sleeping potion from a small glass bottle onto the enemy's territory to put all soldiers within ten miles to sleep for forty-eight hours, depriving them of combat power and leaving them to be captured."

After he left the stage, the British consul was the first to ask him: "I have never heard that your country has an aircraft with this sleeping potion. Where did your statement come from?" He said: "This is written in the booklet. There is a book to prove it." The British consul simply smiled. Later, he told his secretary about this matter. The secretary asked him what booklet he was referring to. He said: "The Air Force of the 21st Century." The secretary laughed and said: "This is an idealized novel predicting the air force a century from now. How can it be used as proof?" He widened his eyes and said: "Isn't it the 21st century now?" The secretary said: "It is currently the 20th century. At least sixty or seventy years must pass before it is the 21st century."

The high-ranking official's purple face turned red, and he tightly closed his mouth, adorned with a German-style mustache, and remained silent for a long time.

Seizing the World 191

— Xian Xian

The phrase "Seizing the World" has been passed down from father to son, from son to grandson, and even to the great-grandchildren in our Suzhou region, for countless generations. Therefore, I believe that in everything, only "fighting" can seize the world, and only "fighting" can lead to a way out. I remember that in my neighbor's house, there was a daughter who was simultaneously having affairs with two young men. One day, the two young men happened to meet. Each rolled up his sleeves, and without a word, they fought each other to the death with fists and feet. After a chaotic fight, one was sweating and panting, while the other was bleeding from the head. It was clear that the sweating and panting friend had won. The friend who was bleeding from the head, fearing a second beating, had to give up his lover. Thus, the victorious friend single-handedly possessed the girl without any scruples. This is what is called "Seizing the World."

Let me give another example. Suppose a wife and concubine are fighting over a husband. The wife does not allow the husband to spend the night in the concubine's room, and the concubine also wants to possess the husband exclusively. At first, they only exchange cold words. Later, they gradually escalate to the point where one scolds the other for being a shameless wife, and the other scolds the other for being a rotten prostitute. If this still cannot be resolved, they have to resort to the final measure: a comparison of who can make a bigger mess. If the result is that the refined wife is beaten by the rough concubine, who smashes the furniture in the room, pulls out a lock of hair, and bites off a piece of flesh from her arm, then the wife can only watch as the husband is taken over by the concubine and enjoys it all alone. Apart from pounding the pillow five thousand times, there is nothing else she can do. Because the concubine has ultimately "Seized the World." In this world, no matter what environment you are in, if you want to stand your ground and not be taken advantage of, you must have the mindset of "Seizing the World." Just sitting at home sighing at the sky and stamping your feet at the ground is just like a saying in Suzhou dialect: "Do Tou," because the "world" is "seized" by oneself through "fighting."

A Bunch of Roses 192

— Mu Yin

For Youthful Young Men

When you want to kiss her, you must ask for her consent, and I believe she will definitely refuse. It is best if you know that she will not refuse, and you can first test her intentions before making a move. Then, her eyes will tell you that she is willing to accept!

To make her love you, your actions should be lively, but not too slippery, because this will make her not only not love you but also fear you.

Observing whether a woman has a lover is very important in the process of courtship. Here, I will tell you a secret: if you see her looking straight ahead, that is a sign that she does not have a lover; if she looks up, not only does she have one, but she is also very satisfied; if she looks down, she has some interest in you, no, at least she is waiting for you to love her.

If you are afraid of divorce, please do not get married.

If she is older than you, you must not call her "dear sister." You should be tactful and call her "dear younger sister."

Telling her that a beautiful female neighbor has moved away will often make her very happy.

Do not believe her, even though she is very solemn on the surface and often scolds that there are no good men in the world, but in her heart, she hopes that someone will come to pursue her. When she tells you about singleism, she is telling you: this is the time to attack her!

If she scolds you, you should be happy, because this is her expression of love for you!

If you fall in love with her, you should not let her know that you are in love with her, if possible, because after she knows, she often reveals arrogance out of complacency.

The "aspirin" in your pocket should always be prepared. If you go out with her and you are short of Yuan Shikai [silver dollars], take out the pills when you have no other choice and say to her: "Oh! I have a terrible headache! I need to go home!" This will definitely work.

Fool 193

— Confucian Monk

That the great Chinese nation, with its thousands of years of cultural history, still has so many useless fools to this day is truly a regrettable thing.

乂乂乂乂

Those who don't go to the cinema, don't enter dance halls, and bury themselves in study rooms are called literary fools, or "bookworms."

When "bookworms" cast aside their books and enter society, they don't know how to "boast" or "flatter," so naturally they won't "get promoted" or "get rich." If they don't seek office or wealth, then they are "idiots."

If these "idiots" don't commit suicide but instead want to write honest complaints with a worn-out brush, they will still run into the barrel of a gun, either being thrown into prison or sent to the underworld. And then people will give them a new name, calling them self-inflicted "Ah Sens."

乂乂乂乂

Passionate telegrams often contain tragic phrases like "Even if one soldier remains, we must resist to the end." But in reality, at most, even that one soldier is finished, while those who send the telegrams are still alive and become "national heroes." Those who die, who truly use their bodies as shields against bullets, are invariably fools.

乂乂乂乂

Those who don't retreat to "preserve strength" but insist on fighting the enemy head-on, never realizing the truth until they die, are fools.

乂乂乂乂

Those who can support themselves and even feed many clever people who exploit others for their own benefit, but who, because they wear tattered cloth clothes and go to the city, are treated like "locust mothers," everywhere being called foolish "country bumpkins."

乂乂乂乂

China's national fortune seems to have been a bit unlucky in recent years. So, is it because there are too many or too few fools?

Novel

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 194

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Three: Ultimately Failing to Untie the Knot, Entering the Door Casting a Mistake, Secretly Pitying the Maid's Wishes to Push Food to Share

Zhao Ziqiang said, "I just came back from the city and saw a large pot of beef being carried out of the halal restaurant. It looked very fresh, and I thought I'd buy two catties for you to taste. It's definitely better than the camel meat they use to fill orders outside the city." As he spoke, he lifted it high in front of Zhao Weng and said with a smile, "Look, isn't this fresh? How would you like to eat it? I'll get the seasonings." "It's going to snow. How about slicing it thin and having a hot pot?" Zhao Weng smiled and said, "We don't have that kind of equipment at home. Eating it that way would be a little forced and less fun. Besides, I'm afraid I won't be able to digest it." Zhao Ziqiang said, "That's true. I'll buy two big radishes and braise the beef with them." Zhao Weng stroked his beard and nodded with a smile. So Zhao Ziqiang went to the kitchen himself to cut the beef and told the errand boy, Xiao Lin, to buy radishes. Xiao Lin went to the front yard, and he chased after him from behind, calling out, "Xiao Lin, be careful when you buy radishes. Don't buy ones that are frozen inside. The old master won't eat them." Jiang heard this in the house and said to Guizhi, "Company Commander Zhao is really good to his old father. He thinks of everything. If I had a son who could support me, I wouldn't want him to be a company commander or anything. As long as he had a heart like Company Commander Zhao, I would die content." Guizhi said, "In this day and age, men and women are equal. Sons can support their parents, and daughters can do the same. Do you believe me? I'm determined to support you for the rest of your life." Jiang sighed and said, "It's not enough just to have that heart. When you go to someone else's home, they will still make half the decisions." Guizhi replied, "What do you mean, someone else making half the decisions? Listen, I'm going to support you for the rest of your life. I'll stay with you and definitely... definitely... never marry into the Yang family." Jiang said, "Why?" Guizhi said, "Didn't I say? It's to support you!" Zhao Ziqiang stood by the gate of the courtyard, listening to these words, and couldn't help but nod. Then he returned to the kitchen to cut the beef. After preparing the dishes properly, he went to Zhao Weng's room to chat with his father. Zhao Weng said, "Xiao Lin hasn't made the radish and beef yet! You're busy all day at the camp. When you come back, you should rest properly." (31)

Women's Paradise

Women's Maxims 195

— Silver Maple

When men whom you don't know well or haven't been formally introduced to approach you for acquaintance and dates, don't consider it a fortunate thing, because they are only using you for pleasure. If you earnestly associate with them, they will consider you a very foolish and careless woman and won't respect you. If they really want to marry you, that's only if you're the only woman in the world.

A happy union is when both husband and wife acknowledge the existence of their differences, and they only know how to cooperate and help each other, without intending to eliminate those differences. This is the most proper way, because husband and wife are originally meant to complement each other and become one. What destroys the happiness of a couple and breaks the bond of a family is not just important issues like economics, which is very unfortunate. Often, very small issues greatly affect the peace and tranquility of married life. Men or women who are too serious or too talkative can damage family happiness.

New-era women are neither parasites nor dependents. Even if she becomes a wife and mother, she still continues her career. If her husband's income isn't enough for household expenses, she earns money to supplement it. If she marries a wealthy man, she still refuses to depend on him for a living, not seeking self-sufficiency and becoming an insignificant idle woman. She wants to be a self-reliant, complete person, not a parasitic wife.

The old-style family is dead, that much is certain, but this is only because the renovation of the environment and the progress of science have produced a new and better family to replace the old style. What we are witnessing is not the destruction of the family, but the evolution of the family. However, women have obtained a good opportunity to develop their abilities, which can promote its evolution. The mission that women bear for humanity is none more noble, sacred, or important than building a happy and fulfilling family. Because fully perfect family construction must have educated and capable women to achieve it.

A certain writer said, "Women waste so much time dealing with those decorations and furniture that are both useless and unattractive; they could save this wasted time and use it to train their bodies, cultivate their knowledge, and refine their spirits." New-era women absolutely do not waste their energy on precious decorations and useless furniture. She has a great purpose in life and is very capable of being active in public affairs, and the spirit of prosperity is also more evident in her family. The more knowledgeable, educated, and experienced a wife and mother is, the more successful she will be in creating a family.

If you constantly blame your husband, he will naturally become resentful. If a husband treats his wife this way, the same result will occur. There was a woman of outstanding will who married a man who easily made small mistakes. Because she loved her husband, she urged him every day after they got married. At first, she looked for his mistakes; told him what he should and shouldn't do; and criticized his behavior and words everywhere. This man respected his wife and always tried to make her happy. At first, he always accepted her will and did as she said, but later he couldn't stand it anymore. His good character was ruined by her, and he became an easily angered, depressed, and unhappy person. As a result, both of their lives were miserable. He was not only not influenced by her, but also resented her meddling. His love for his wife was completely extinguished.

Free Talk

On Compromise 196

— Yu Dafu

John Morley's theory of compromise is actually a lash at the contemporaries' lack of compromise, while China's lack of compromise with Japan is actually the most thorough compromise. One concession, then another, then a third, and then the three northeastern provinces, then Rehe, and then... if this isn't compromise, what is it? Having seen the contradiction between name and reality at home and abroad, I want to say a few words about compromise. Zhuangzi said, "Name is the guest of reality." How great are these words! The excellent roots of the Chinese people lie in this.

To speak of the origin of compromise, it is because of this and that, vaguely and ambiguously, that individuals can profit from it. A certain ruler became an emperor through compromise, a certain general gained territory through compromise, and a certain gentleman consolidated his own power and position through compromise, borrowing the power of others to achieve his own desires. What does the country matter to me? What do the people matter to me? If this isn't the function of compromise, then what is it?

In China, not only are people the most fond of compromise, but even the upright and selfless deities are generally fond of compromise. In the village operas I saw as a child in the Hundred Longevity Picture, that short-lived ghost could actually add to his lifespan through the power of a single meal and drink. When people die, they only need to burn more paper money at the City God Temple, and the ghosts will also reduce the severe punishments they inflict on the dead because they are greedy for bribes. Therefore, Chinese dignitaries who do much evil often go to repair temples and offer incense, while foreign tycoons who squeeze the poor are often charitable and benevolent. Charity prevails, sins are eliminated, and the common people become more and more miserable. This is another reflection of the Chinese heaven and deities' love of compromise.

These are originally compromises among the big shots and gentlemen, but among us common people, it is not so. The poor and the poor often quarrel, fight, and lose their lives over a penny. The residents of poor and remote areas love to litigate and often engage in armed fights over trivial matters. Leaving that aside for the moment, just taking Shanghai's streets as an example, day and night, among the common people, occasional open and secret struggles, scolding, and killings are caused by an unrelated word or action. It's truly unknown how many tens or hundreds of incidents there are, and in the end, it benefits the officers in the police station, making their business flourish and their wealth abound. This is also the harm of not compromising.

In this case, the conclusion of my short article is naturally "From this perspective, can one not compromise?"

Primary School Teacher H. Barbusse, translated by Li Qingya. The weather is very hot. We hear the bees flying and see them swarming in the fiery air. Pedestrians carefully dodge into the shadows at the foot of the row of gray houses. This is the scene on the square of the village of Gavadar in the province of Santander, Spain. This village is similar to most villages in Spain, and also similar to the villages in the area where Spain and France border. In the past, the scenery in this place was certainly more picturesque than it is now, but it is not weak now, and the mysterious and dry flavor of Spain, with its towering peaks and worried people, is shrouding this area.

In addition to the buzzing of the bees, there is another large array of murmurs with a monotonous rhythm that is窜到outside from that row of walls. This is the village's elementary school. The interior of the elementary school is similar to the interior of elementary schools all over the world. The walls are dark and solemn; perhaps the hard shell of the elementary school must be changed to the hard shell of society before anyone will change it; many rows of black desks, many small heads, which are also black, but round and square; in the middle, a standing person is clearly a great man, this is the teacher in the elementary school.

He, too, like those fellow workers all over the world, unfolds his extraordinary ingenuity and patience to guide and focus the attention of those thirty small heads, and tries to put as much of the grand view of the real world into those heads as possible.

The village elementary school teacher in Gavada is named Bartolomeo and his last name is Zori. He is a peaceful, simple and kind person, and everyone says that he serves wholeheartedly. In the small scope of this village, his uncompromising attitude has long been recognized by all. If he is occasionally late, the public will say with a firm tone: This is because the clock is out of order.

Because he maintains an upright attitude in his thinking, just as he does in his life, his thoughts cannot satisfy everyone, especially his thoughts that contain the meaning of joint responsibility and cooperation, and some people even say: This is a red party. However, even those who are surprised in their hearts, in their servile and pitiful hearts, that a person can be a red party and be upright at the same time, cannot help but admire Zori.

However, the two important people in Gavada, the two people wearing black robes, the pastor and vice-pastor of the village church, did not think this way. They equally hated this elementary school teacher, even though they could not condemn him except for his intense love of freedom and public happiness.

These two priests monitor this elementary school, which is the factory that manufactures the thinking of the next generation that will follow. Therefore, if they do not want to let the future world escape from their grasp, they should naturally seize this factory in their own hands.

More than ten years ago, there was a person named Francisco Ferrer who wanted to liberate all of the elementary schools in Spain from the cold and dark world of the priests. As a result, he was shot by the Spanish government. At that time, those bullets shattered his body before he could finish saying the last sentence that he regarded as the highest slogan of his life, "Long live the elementary school." (To be continued)

Beasts in Clothes 197

— Guangmo

What distinguishes humans from animals is mostly just clothing. There is not much difference otherwise.

It is said that dogs symbolize righteousness. The dog owner feeds them some leftovers, meat scraps, and bones. If you kick or hit them, not only will they not get angry, but they will also wag their tails incessantly. Horses symbolize loyalty. The horse owner gives them some straw stalks to eat. If you whip them on their backs, they will run as fast as they can, carrying their owner. As for bees symbolizing obedience and ants symbolizing unity, everyone knows that. Therefore, ancient emperors and great Confucian ministers who promoted benevolent rule loved to use these animal ethics, adding explanations of loyalty, filial piety, chastity, righteousness, the three bonds, and the five constants, to show the model and inspire people. To put it plainly, it means that to be a human, you must learn from animals. Only by learning to be like animals can you be considered a human. In this century, we can find "people" who are as righteous as dogs, as loyal as horses, as obedient as bees, and as united as ants everywhere without using telescopes or microscopes, which is the ideal of great Confucian ministers who promote benevolent rule. We cannot help but sing the efforts of ancient sages and praise the fact that people in this century are like animals, creating the culture of this century.

From the above theory of animals symbolizing humans, then humans, without a doubt, can also symbolize animals. If this implication is not contrary to logic, then humans are animals, and animals are humans, becoming a human-animal unity. However, humans are, after all, humans, and animals are, after all, animals, because humans ultimately have an extra set of clothing.

"Midnight" and National Goods Year (Continued) 198

— Le'ai

The war of the masses, although it has not yet defeated those kings of national goods with stock, has already surged up like a tide. Especially during the period described by "Midnight," there was a wave of Xun surge, and then it temporarily receded a bit. This wave is constantly agitating, pushing from here to there. Even if there are some ups and downs, the prospect of breaking through everything is obvious. Those "dogs" use all means to suppress this wave; pretending to be a Gidde-style "national goods struggle" is just one of these means.

Whether it's Wu Sunfu, Lao Zhao, or Zhou Zhongwei, these various kings, whether in the city or in the countryside, are all carefully guarding against it. Landlords like Feng Yunqing cannot but hide in Shanghai to invest in public bonds, and even sell their own daughters, watching their mistresses mess around without rhyme or reason. And although Shanghai is relatively stable, it is also constantly闹ing with labor strikes every day, and the kings of national goods do not have a moment of peace in their dreams, often dreaming of workers overturning their "thrones." This is certainly not an ideal paradise for them, who devour each other. They, even the "industrialists" who do not linger on the old rural life, must "seriously negotiate with the battalion commander and ask him to pay attention to the communists in the surrounding villages;" they also want to deal with the workers by intrigue and want to "wipe out those bad guys in one fell swoop." Are they "surrounded by landmines? Stepping on one will set off an explosion!"... Their "authority has already revealed signs of defeat everywhere, becoming a total collapse!"... The steel wire cushion under them suddenly turned into a mountain of knives. Yes, their future is decline and destruction, although the total collapse is not yet at hand, and although the tip of the knife on the mountain of knives has not yet cut through their throats. Surrounding them, there is indeed Tu Weiyue, who has some small military strategist means, who can use some deceptive and provocative traps, but he can only always "dispatch an additional police force to protect the factory." And what other talents are there besides Tu Weiyue? Empty-talking university professors, interest-eating noble poets? Swords and iron fists? Even Wu Sunfu himself, who thought he was steel, gradually exposed his "outward strength but inward weakness," an indescribable feeling of cowardice, pessimism, decadence, and decline.

On the other hand, some of those intellectual youths who participated in the May Thirtieth Movement five years ago can now only "sit high on the second floor of the Dasanyuan Restaurant, hoping to follow the elegant interest of Emperor Nero (Nero) climbing high to watch the city of Rome."

All of this almost reflects the entire Chinese society, but with large cities as the center. This is a "fragment" from the middle of 1930, and it quite implicitly suggests the connection between the past and the future. This is China's first successful realistic novel, with a very obvious influence from Zola (Zola's "Largent" - "Money"). Of course, it has many shortcomings, even errors. However, applying real social science to express the social class relations of China in literature and art cannot be said to be a great achievement for "Midnight." Mao Dun is not Zola, and he at least no longer has Zola's stupid Proudhonism.

Here, it is not possible to study "Midnight" in detail, analyzing it. What I want to point out is just a major event in the Chinese literary world! The appearance of "Midnight" coincided very humorously with the so-called National Goods Year. In the future history of literature in 1933, there is no doubt that the publication of "Midnight" will be recorded; but this "National Goods Year" of 1933 will probably be of no other use than to serve as a humorous contrast to "Midnight"! Originally, this is "Midnight." Before the red sun of the morning shines all over China, how can there be a real National Goods Year? And by that time, this country will no longer be the country of the "kings," nor will it be the country of their backstage bosses.

Crossroads of Era and Love 200

Haiquan hesitated for a moment and did not answer. Li Yixiang only thought that Haiquan did not believe that he had such great supernatural powers to communicate with the headquarters figures of the S Society. In fact, this was a mistake in Yixiang's observation. Haiquan thought, what is the big deal about being able to know the figures of the S Society headquarters? For a young man, even if this is not feudal thought, it can at least be said to be the thought of hero worship, and both of these thoughts are enemies of the revolution.

"No. Everything, everything, everything, is hidden in me. I, I, in here..."

Yixiang pointed to his belly and said to Haiquan. Haiquan felt that Yixiang was completely a book fanatic again.

"If you have, have, have, any works, send them to me. I, I, I, can find a way to publish them for you."

Haiquan was a little happy again after hearing this.

After saying goodbye to that revolutionary literature specialist Mr. Li Yixiang, Haiquan was shivering in the cold wind again. The north wind was blowing very hard, calling out sounds like the bombing planes of the Japanese imperialists. He felt a cold wind attacking his back in bursts.

"It must be twelve o'clock now. Tonight, I am a homeless person!"

As he walked thinking this, he felt infinite sadness and wanted to cry several times. But it seemed that the degree of sadness was not enough. His eyelids flickered a few times, but no tears came out.

Economic Special Issue No. 16 Published Every Monday 201

An Anatomical Analysis of the Technocracy Theory by Xu Yu 202

The name Technocracy is currently extremely fashionable. America is the place where this term originated, so naturally American newspapers and magazines are filled with discussions about this theory, even newsreels in sound films use Technocracy as a rallying cry. Magazines and newspapers in our country have also provided considerable introductions. This article studies the social environment that produced Technocracy entirely from an economic perspective, examines its intellectual origins, and then critiques whether its theories are sound.

(1) The Social Environment that Produced Technocracy

America is a large and resource-rich country with a relatively small population, and because it was founded not long ago, its resources have not been fully utilized. Therefore, most American economists have an optimistic outlook. Henry C. Carey, an American economist from a hundred years ago, was a very optimistic person. Of course, Carey's theory is completely different from Technocracy's theory. The former acknowledges that the world is gradually becoming harmonious, and that all social conflicts, such as labor disputes, can gradually disappear on their own. The latter believes that there is a contradiction between the current methods of production (i.e., mechanical technology production) and methods of distribution (i.e., distribution of money based on human labor). If we want to save the current society from the suffering of unemployment, we must abolish the monetary distribution system and use a capacity distribution system instead. However, both share a common feature, that is, optimism about the future. Carey believed that Ricardo's land rent theory was incorrect. Humans do not cultivate good land first and then poor land; on the contrary, they cultivate poor land first and then good land. Therefore, the future society should gradually prosper. The Technocracy group believes that the current methods of production are very developed and that the society can enjoy true happiness simply by changing the monetary unit to a capacity unit. Their future society is one where "everyone only needs to work 660 hours per year, but the standard of living can be higher than in 1929, the most prosperous period of commerce."

Carey's theory that poor land is cultivated before good land was completely influenced by the social environment of America at the time. At that time, the westward movement in America was in full swing, good land was gradually being developed, and the population was relatively small, so Carey had this kind of theory. This theory was very suitable for the situation at the time, but today, due to the progress of civilization and the increase in population, it has begun to waver. As for whether the optimism of the Technocracy group has a sound basis, we will discuss it later. However, if America were not so mechanically advanced and its production technology were not so advanced, this kind of discussion would never have occurred. Therefore, we can say that Technocracy is a product of the social environment.

(2) The Technocracy Theory of Internal Contradictions of Capitalism

As mentioned in the previous section, the Technocracy group believes that the capitalist method of production has entered the age of complete mechanization, while its distribution method is still based on human labor, resulting in a lack of balance between consumption and production. This is a major contradiction of capitalism. This theory seems very new, but in fact, Marx had already discussed it seventy or eighty years ago. Marx believed that the internal contradictions of capitalism had both material and artificial aspects. The material aspect includes the contradiction between the method of production and the relations of production. The so-called relations of production are class relations and property relations, in other words, distribution relations. From this, isn't Technocracy's theory of internal contradictions of capitalism greatly influenced by Marx?

Not only in terms of theoretical outline, is Technocracy seemingly similar to Marx; even when exposing the shortcomings of capitalism, the two groups' voices are almost identical. The Technocracy group believes that the owners of machinery account for a very small number in society, and under today's price system, the consumption power (i.e., purchasing power) obtained by this very small number of people far exceeds what they can use. Therefore, they can only reinvest this surplus purchasing power into machinery, resulting in the continued expansion of industrial machinery, a large increase in output, and the inability of society under the price system to accommodate it. The next step is a drop in prices, capitalists cannot make a profit, production stagnates, workers become unemployed, and consumption power further declines. According to Technocrats, commercial recession is unavoidable unless the price system is abolished, and this is the reason for the collapse of capitalism.

What did Marx say? Marx believed that the goal of capitalists is to obtain as much surplus value as possible, so they try their best to increase working hours. However, the wages earned by workers are only enough to maintain the survival of their families and themselves. At the same time, in order to obtain greater profits, capitalists reinvest the surplus value they have obtained into factories, or add machines, to increase the speed of production. As a result, output increases greatly, but the laborers who constitute the majority of consumers, their wages are only enough to maintain survival, without sufficient consumption power, thus forming overproduction, which is one of the internal contradictions of capitalism.

Now we can see the striking degree of similarity between the Technocracy group and Marx regarding the theory of internal contradictions of capitalism.

(3) Technocracy's Theory of Capacity Value

Since the Technocracy group believes that the main cause of social unemployment and panic is the monetary price system, their method of reform lies in abolishing the price system. They believe that the necessary condition for the price system is human labor, but human labor is no longer important in today's production, so the price system has become a burden on current society, preventing industry from continuing to work and reducing the purchasing power of the masses. They also say that gold and silver are inaccurate currencies and are not suitable for today's technologically advanced society, because what gold and silver represent is not wealth, but a debt to industry. To reform the contradictions of current society, we must recognize that the purpose of wealth is to seek social welfare, that wealth is the product of capacity, and that its measurement should be in units of capacity. The concrete form of the capacity unit is the "Energy Certificate." An Energy Certificate is based on the amount of human labor or fuel consumption required to produce a certain commodity. After obtaining this Energy Certificate, consumers have the right to equal consumption.

The concept of the Energy Certificate seems very novel. A similar concept is Owen's Labor Note in the 19th century. Owen established a labor exchange where anyone who brought goods to the labor exchange was given a corresponding labor note based on the time required for their work. The labor note is slightly different from the Energy Certificate, because the labor note is marked with human labor, while the Energy Certificate is marked with capacity. Human labor only occupies a small part of capacity. However, we can very well say that the Technocracy's concept of the Energy Certificate is greatly influenced by Owen.

(4) Can Technocracy Really Break the Price System?

Above, we talked about how Technocracy originated in America because America is mechanically advanced, its production technology is advanced, and its natural resources are abundant. It is the same as Carey's economic theory from a hundred years ago, both taking American society as the background. We also explained that their theory of internal contradictions of capitalism is almost entirely derived from Marx's economic theory, and that their theory of capacity value and Energy Certificate plan are undoubtedly influenced by Owen. As for their theory of insufficient consumption causing panic, economists have long talked about it, and the idea that wealth should focus on social welfare is similar to the welfare economics advocated by Hobson. But can we say that it is worthless because it copies from the east and borrows from the west?

This is obviously not possible. No theory in social science can be strictly said to be uniquely created. Most are hinted at and inspired by other people's theories, and then integrated. If we want to discuss whether the theory of Technocracy is sound, we must see whether its entire theoretical foundation is sound.

The Technocracy group believes that the crux of current society lies in the price system, which is an oversimplified view of social problems. This is because most of the figures in Technocracy are engineers and physicists, so when discussing economic problems, they often focus on the relationship between people and things and ignore the relationship between people. Currency is only a medium of exchange, chosen by humans as a standard of wealth. Of course, this medium has some negative impacts on society, but abolishing the monetary system cannot solve all social problems. Stepping back, even if the price system is the crux of society and currency is not enough to represent wealth, the price system still exists even if gold and silver are abolished and replaced with Energy Certificates. Because no matter whether the medium of exchange is currency or Energy Certificates, the ratio of exchange will always exist. Where there is a ratio of exchange, there is price; only the expressed names are different. Therefore, it is a mistake for Scott, the leader of Technocracy, to believe that Technocracy can break the price system.

(5) The Basic Shortcomings of Technocracy

The Technocracy group believes that price can be abolished, which shows that they do not understand the principle of scarcity. Not understanding scarcity is the basic shortcoming of the Technocracy group. Scarcity is not only the basic principle of economic phenomena, but also the main reason for the occurrence of all social phenomena. If there were no scarcity, we would not need laws, politics, or morality. What the law protects is only people's property rights, etc. What morality teaches is nothing more than how to adapt to social survival. Politics is a regulatory mechanism set up for public purposes. If all goods were absolutely abundant, what conflicts would people have? What need would there be for laws to protect? What need would there be for morality to teach? What need would there be for politics to maintain order? Price comes from scarcity. Air is absolutely abundant. Does air have a price?

The Technocracy group says: "The era of scarcity of consumer goods has passed. The current century no longer requires labor and thrift as conditions for survival in the world. ... America has rich natural resources and great machine capacity, and will surely enter a new era of civilization." However, these are only empty words without proof. They only tell us how much labor a certain flour mill uses and how much flour it produces, how many car frames a certain automobile factory can produce per day, and that a certain rayon factory only needs one worker to manage the entire factory. Even if these statistics are completely accurate, at most they only tell us that production technology has improved. The improvement of production technology and the increase of production are two different things. They cannot prove that the wheat used to make flour has increased several times, that the wood used to make car frames has increased several times, or that the raw materials used to make rayon have increased several times. There are many raw materials that cannot be produced without limits by advanced production technology. If raw materials cannot be produced without limits, what is the use of advanced production technology? How can "everyone work 660 hours per year and the standard of living be higher than in 1929?"

They also say that America accounts for 40% of the world's iron ore, 50% of the coal mines, 69% of the oil, and 81% of the natural gas, with 1/12 of the area and 6% of the population, which can be considered abundant. They do not know that this is still scarce, because scarcity is a relative concept. Even if all the world's resources were concentrated in America, it would not necessarily be abundant.

Now we can make a temporary conclusion: Technocracy is a monster that collects the theories of various schools, such as those of economists, integrates them, is influenced by the American social environment, and rises amid the decline of the American economy. The people who created this theory, because they ignore the economic principle of scarcity, inevitably make mistakes in their propositions. Although it is very popular now, it will probably be eliminated soon.

(Note) Although the above conclusion is said to be temporary, it is still inevitably arbitrary. Because the formal books written by the Technocracy group themselves have not yet been published, their ideas are scattered in magazines and newspapers. However, from these newspapers and magazines, we can already see the general outline of their thoughts. Whether the conclusion is reliable, let the facts prove it. March 30th, at Shanghai Business School

On Technocracy by Lin Bingzhong 203

In the autumn of 1929, a major financial crisis occurred on Wall Street in New York, opening the curtain on the world economic panic. Until today, there is still no sign of recovery, and the angry tide of panic is only increasing. Economists and politicians are at a loss and simply have no way to break this situation. During this period, some people have proposed the Technocracy system to solve all economic problems. Newspapers and magazines have vigorously promoted it, and many people in our country have recently introduced this new theory. I personally have a lot of doubts about this system. Now I will briefly describe its important significance as follows:

(1) Proponents of Technocracy believe that the severity of the world economic panic and unemployment problems is due to the current monetary and price system. This system is a tool for capitalists to profit, so it has resulted in the concentration of capital in the hands of a few people, while the majority of people have nothing to eat. Solving the current unemployment problem means preventing capital from concentrating in the hands of a few people, which also means overthrowing the monetary and price system.

(2) After abolishing the monetary and price system, all goods can be measured by "Energy," and "Energy Certificates" can be issued as a medium of exchange.

(3) The thinking of this group of people is that the basis of the economy is in machines, so all economic undertakings should be managed by scientists, who should determine the amount of production from a technical standpoint, so that it is sufficient for consumption.

The above three points are the propositions of this group of people. Now I will talk about my opinions on this new system based on these three points: (1) We know that the biggest reason for this economic panic is that the supply of production is too large, exceeding what consumption needs, so prices have fallen, and capitalists have tightened production and eliminated subordinates, thus forming the currently acute unemployment problem. Why has production expanded so much? In simple terms, it is because of the development of machines. Since the introduction of machines, general scientists have been improving them day by day, trying all kinds of ways to increase the efficiency of machines, so that they can produce the greatest effect with the least labor in the shortest period of time. The more developed the machines, the less the use of labor. On the other hand, the population is increasing day by day, so the unemployment problem has reached today's point. This is the cause of this world economic panic, so the more developed the machines are in a country, the more unemployed people there are. The United States is an example. This group of proponents of the Technocracy system believes that the crux of the economic panic lies in the monetary and price system, because with money, capitalists can monopolize everything, so it must be overthrown. This argument is a bit like chasing shadows. We know that money is a medium, because it is convenient, so it is used to buy goods. The ultimate desire of human beings is not for money but for goods, because with money, there can be goods, so they turn their attention to money. Even if the monetary and price system is completely destroyed, capitalists may not necessarily have no desire to seize goods, and they may not necessarily be unable to seize goods, right?

(2) In the past, Adam Smith advocated that "Labor" should be the basis of the value of all goods. He also knew that "Labor" cannot be accurately valued, so there is also a "Theory of Exchange Value." Now, the proponents of the Technocracy system also advocate using energy as the standard of value. The so-called energy here is of course the energy of human labor and machines. Then how should "energy" be valued? The energy used to manufacture a car can be measured. How should the teaching of teachers be measured? Service is also a kind of production!

They also advocate issuing "Energy Certificates" to purchase goods. Then "Energy Certificates" can be regarded as a kind of medium of exchange. What is the difference between them and money? If capitalists can seize money, can't they seize "Energy Certificates"? So this is not a fundamental solution.

(3) It is undeniable that current production is purely machine production. The manufacture and improvement of machines depend on the research and inventions of scientists, but it cannot be assumed that scientists can solve all economic problems by inventing machines. Economic undertakings cannot start without scientists, but scientists may not necessarily be omnipotent. With science, other social sciences can be abandoned. This group of people attaches too much importance to scientists. They want to cross the boundaries of natural science and invade the scope of social science, talking a lot about solving the recent economic panic with technology. However, they do not know that the problems in natural science are completely different from the social environment. Technology can only improve production and cannot solve the economic panic caused by overproduction and falling prices.

This system is just being established, and detailed works have not yet been published. The above are just my doubts that I have raised and talked about. Perhaps the papers they publish in the future will be able to explain all my doubts, which is unknown.

A Review of "Technocracy" by Liang Ming 204

The emergence of all theories is nothing more than adapting to the needs of the times. Their ability to be welcomed and disseminated is mostly due to adapting to the times. For example, the severity of the unemployment problem caused by the industrial revolution in the 18th century created the position of Malthus's "Theory of Population." The economic reconstruction required by Germany and Italy after the war led to the rise of fascism. The "Technocracy" that is currently making a lot of noise in American newspapers and magazines is nothing more than a product of the economic panic in the golden country.

"Technocracy" is now not only being enthusiastically studied in academic circles in America, but is also attracting attention in various European countries. In the future, its power may further increase and have a greater impact, but its content, as it currently exists, is very simple.

"Technocracy" is advocated by a group of scientists in America, whose leader is Howard Scott. They organized a group to study the material aspects of society's functions in North America. The object of their greatest attention is production technology, that is, English Technology. Based on this word, they call their group Technocracy. Since its establishment twelve years ago, they have studied no fewer than 3,000 industries and created many patterns, analyzing the material functions of North America very clearly.

As a result of Technocracy's research on North America's material capabilities, they recently published their reports and propositions. They believe that in the past 30 years, the invention of new machines and the application of automation have progressed rapidly, and all production organizations have been technologized. The result of this excessive technological progress has conflicted with America's old economic system, that is, the price system in the original distribution can no longer adapt to the new technologized production organization. The most obvious example is the severity of the widespread unemployment problem. It was previously thought that it could be solved by improving production technology, but now it is known that the improvement of production technology causes unemployment problems. The more advanced the production technology, the more it will promote the severity of unemployment problems.

But they are not like the early Guild Socialists or individual anarchists who hate the improvement of production technology because the invention of machinery causes corresponding evils. They are all the opposite. They believe that the improvement of technology is an inevitable trend, and what is wrong is that the current price system cannot adapt to the emerging production technology. They believe that finance or prices expressed in gold and silver belong to the past and cannot do anything about the current economic panic. All social life is dominated by the laws of physics. In the laws of physics, "Energy" is the source of all production and social life. With the progress of technology, since money belongs to the past, the distribution system should be determined based on each person's "Energy." Although the expression of energy has various forms, the size of energy can be determined by the unit of work. Therefore, issuing "Energy Certificates" to replace the current currency can enable the balanced development of production technology and work distribution, so that there will be no problems of unemployment and economic panic today. For example, Scott expounds on this theory in his article "Technology Breaks the Price System." As for the detailed implementation methods, they have not yet published them, and how their insights are is unknown. The explanation of the principle is only this much.

We do not deny the influence of "Technocracy," and it may become even more lively in the near future, but there is no need to overemphasize its actual value. Some people criticize the once-sensational Malthus's theory of population, which still has lingering effects, saying: "It is only the prejudice of factions that makes people pay attention to this little book." Similarly, it is only because the American economic panic has no way out that people pay attention to the voice in the silence, Technocracy. With the progress of social science, the fact that human social relations are by no means comparable to natural relations such as the laws of physics is something that does not need to be debated.

However, this theory is not without some lessons for our country now. That is, technology and social relations are inseparable. Revitalizing China is not something that can be achieved by simply improving production. On the contrary, America has been harmed under the condition of high production.

Letter of Correction

To whom it may concern, In my article "Obstacles to Cooperatives" in the last issue, there were occasional references to the cooperative office of the Central Political School in Nanjing, which was actually due to errors in hearsay. I now know that the school's cooperative is indeed one of the most successful consumer cooperatives in the country and does not receive any subsidies. It is said that those in charge of it are Mr.s from the China Cooperative Society. I am specially introducing it and asking for a correction.

Respectfully, He Fajing (March 29)
