Securities 207

Public Bonds Continued to Advance to Higher Levels Last Week

Rose by About One to Three Yuan Compared to the Previous Week

Trading was Most Active Among the Northern Factions and Money Shops

Stock Exchange Closed for Three Days Starting Today for Arbor Day

From March 27th to April 1st of last week, the market for public bonds at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange was extremely robust, with a promising upward trend. Firstly, the market price did not weaken after settlement; secondly, the May futures, once launched for trading, opened high one after another. Both of these factors sufficiently demonstrate the continued high demand from various factions and the increasing number of investors. In reality, since the government has not issued new bonds since 1932, the market feels a shortage. On the other hand, it can also prove that the government's finances are in order. Taken together, it is clear that domestic bonds have gradually gotten on the right track. Calculating at the highest market price on Friday, most were equivalent to 758 per one tael of customs gold for the 1918 issue, and around 76 for the 1918 customs issue. The 1931 and 1932 issues were still insufficient. Once the U.S. silver loan is established, the government will have no need to issue new public bonds. Furthermore, bonds have withstood the severe situation after the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, as well as the serious situation in North China. Under such extreme pressure, the financial community still absorbed them, so the public's understanding of bonds has gradually become clearer, especially with the painful realization of the difficulty of speculative trading. Recently, there has also been talk of the Japanese abandoning the use of force. Except for Thursday, when the market was closed for settlement, and Saturday, when rumors caused a drop of about one yuan, the price rose gradually every day for the remaining four days of last week. The most significant increase was on Friday. As a result, the price rose by about one to three yuan compared to the previous week. Trading was mostly done by the Northern factions and money shops, with quite busy trading by retail investors. Buying treasures was quite active, and financial short-term public bonds, which had long been unattended, suddenly began to be traded. Three sessions were opened throughout the day, with market prices ranging from eighteen yuan to fifty-eight yuan and one dime. It is said that this was due to banks closing in on millions, with no other reason. The total number of transactions for the week amounted to 52.802 million yuan, including 22,000 yuan in spot goods and 12.835 million yuan in futures. Salt tax alone accounted for 19.77 million, and disbandment accounted for more than 8.1 million. The 1918 customs gold and general issues together accounted for 8.73 million, and the 1931 and 1932 issues accounted for 12 million. The remaining issues ranged from 500,000 to 2 million. The stock exchange will be closed for three days starting today for Arbor Day.

Sugar Market 211

Domestic Sliced Qing Label Plate Further Declines

Yesterday, the sugar market trend was still relatively stable. The association's plate for No. 24 coarse granulated white ordinary was still marked at 15 liang and 2 fen and a half, without any ups or downs. However, the top coarse RA mark rose by 5 fen due to lack of bottom goods, marked at 15 liang and 3 qian and a half. No. 20 medium granulated white was called at 14 liang and 6 qian, and No. 18 at 14 liang and 4 qian, but there were few transactions and seemed to be loosening. No. 89 Dutch red was still at 11 liang and 9 qian. Sliced Qing suffered from sluggish sales and the weather was gradually getting hotter, so there was concern about oil production. Therefore, the label plate initially loosened secretly and then clearly decreased. Yesterday, the market opened with about 300-400 small boxes of sliced Qing, priced at 6 liang and 4 qian, down 3 qian compared to the previous day. According to the label family's intention, if there is a whole batch transaction, it is still possible to continue loosening. Hainan red North City label family continued to open more than 100 bags, priced at 10 liang and 4 qian and a half. Sufficiently high-grade ice white sugar was expected to increase by 4 qian and a half, but each bank could not agree for a while and no plate was formed.

Silk and Tea 212

Foreign Banks' Silk Inventory Still Low at the End of the Third Month

Foreign firms are purchasing little silk as spring arrives, total inventory is only over 800 bales.

Global economic instability has caused European and American silk sales to plummet, and Chinese silk quotations are gradually decreasing. Since the beginning of spring, foreign firms in Shanghai have not dared to risk buying silk, either for spot or futures. Silk inventories are low. According to a survey of various foreign firms, the total inventory of factory white, yellow, and gray silks at the end of March was 860 bales, of which 305 bales were prepared for shipment to the Americas, 340 bales to Europe, and 215 bales to Asia. This is a decrease of about 100 bales compared to the end of February.

Rayon Delivered

Inland Silk Merchants Have Over 300 Boxes 213

Rayon, which inland silk merchants in Shanghai purchased the right to manufacture summer silk fabrics, has been delivered by various foreign firms at the end of last month. Because inland silk factories are in great need of raw materials, the factories have successively shipped out the remaining silk. Yesterday and today, 343 boxes have been exported, of which 260 boxes were loaded to various ports along the Yangtze River and 83 boxes were transported to Hangzhou and Huzhou.

Shen Bao Medical and Pharmaceutical Weekly

Contents of This Issue 214

A Brief Overview of Medicine and Pharmaceuticals in Shanghai in the Last Decade (Continued) ·················· Pang Jingzhou

Several Important Discoveries and Inventions in the Developing Process of New Medicine ········· Gu Shoubai

A Brief Overview of Medicine and Pharmaceuticals in Shanghai in the Last Decade (Continued) 215

— Pang Jingzhou

Chapter Four: The Situation of Business

We in the medical community value those physicians who specialize in serving in hospitals and medical school professors because they receive very little salary and do a lot of work, and do not want to extract any great profits from society. This shows that they are willing to sacrifice their own enjoyment and go into the direction of academic research. In the future, all medical progress in China will mostly rely on this group of people. Unfortunately, the Shanghai Medical School has not made much progress in the last ten years, and most of the hospitals are still in the hands of foreigners. There are not many such people. People in society often think that very popular practicing physicians can definitely invent something in medicine, but the more popular they are, the busier they are, and the result is the opposite. In addition, we must also strongly encourage physicians in charitable hospitals, no matter how their academics are. Only then will people be willing to serve in hospitals for charitable causes for life. At present, people in society pay the least attention to these two types of physicians, and especially do not sympathize with physicians in hospitals, because physicians who are willing to stay in hospitals for a long time have calm personalities, and may not be well-rounded in dealing with patients. However, our country's patients have been hypnotized by the historical contempt for doctors, and they most like the doctor's flattery and perfunctory treatment. Many foreign professors often use a commanding attitude to treat patients, which is not acceptable in China. Therefore, even foreigners in Shanghai cater to social psychology to a great extent, and the general wealthy merchants are most easily fooled.

Most of the old foreign doctors in Shanghai are still quite disciplined. In terms of academics, even if they were not very good in their early years, they have now experimented very well by taking China as a testing product. However, they are gradually taking some "appeasement measures" when treating Chinese people. This is their way of catering to social psychology, and it is also proof that they are familiar with China. It is the result of the Chinese themselves being good at being perfunctory. In the last ten years, the number of foreign doctors coming to Shanghai has greatly increased. Because after the European War, foreign medicine made rapid progress, a group of formal experts came because of the needs of foreigners in Shanghai. Also, because of the large number of doctors trained in various countries every year, a group of people who are not very good also came to solve the problem of bread and butter specifically for the Chinese. The steps for this type of foreign doctors to open a business in Shanghai are nothing more than first finding his own country's merchants in Shanghai, and being introduced by his own country's merchants to his Chinese compradors. The Chinese compradors invite him to eat Chinese food and get to know a group of Chinese merchants. During the dinner, he flatters and brags to the fullest extent. How can Chinese people resist the flattery of blue-eyed, high-nosed people? Naturally, they are flattered. Then, they introduce some patients to him. If the treatment goes wrong, they really dare not say half a word of complaint. If the treatment goes well, they will fall to the ground in admiration. When the business is good, the clinic will be bigger, and the bills for the equipment owed to the foreign firm will be paid off. They will then settle down in Shanghai. At that time, when someone in the family of the original introducer is sick and wants to ask him to come, he often puts on airs, saying that a certain military commander has asked him to quit smoking, and a certain minister's wife has asked him to deliver a baby, and he is too busy to get away for a while.

The most ridiculous thing is that there are also a few people in our medical community who like to cooperate with foreign slippery doctors to do business. I don't know whether it is appropriate to call them accomplices or accomplices? Last winter, I also saw a case of chronic breast cancer with a Russian doctor. According to his opinion, it was a minor problem and would be cured after taking a few days of medicine. I said that the cervical glands were swollen and the head was affected. I am afraid that the small size of the local cancer cannot be ignored. He seemed not very understanding. Later, the patient certainly took his manageable and simple statement. So the Russian sent two bottles of black medicine made with Eubiosae (a kind of tonic), but it was not Eubiose. Unfortunately, the patient died after taking it for only three days. He could not be a long-term customer of the Russian. Although the fact is like this, I always feel that in Shanghai, where there are no rules for medicine and pharmaceuticals, perhaps the Russian doctor will still have a very bright future by relying on language barriers. Only Dr. Schmidt and so on, who once sued me eight years ago and specialized in using anti-aging to appeal to people, was finally bombarded back. It seems that he did not even pay off the equipment fees of a certain foreign company. He can be considered one of the most unlucky foreigners.

Reasons Why Gonorrhea is Difficult to Cure and the Correct Treatment Method (Part 1) 216

— Xie Junshou

The most common medical and pharmaceutical advertisements in newspapers are for gonorrhea. Electrical therapy, injection therapy, internal medicine to eradicate the root, secret prescription for white turbid urine, white turbid urine grass, etc., are really diverse and strange. However, since there are so many treatment methods, why can't gonorrhea be cured? Now, I will first write down the reasons why gonorrhea is difficult to cure one by one below:

(1) The nature of gonococcus: Gonococcus most likes to exist in the urethra and has the nature of permanent survival. Therefore, if gonococcus is not eliminated, gonorrhea cannot be cured. However, to kill gonococcus, it is necessary to use bactericidal methods. For example, if drug therapy or physical therapy is used, if a severe method is used, although it can completely kill the gonococcus, the urethral tissue will be damaged. If a mild method is used, it is difficult to see results.

(2) The relationship of urethral tissue: The urethral mucosa itself has an epithelial cell lining to prevent the invasion of external harmful poisons. When gonococcus invades the urethra, it multiplies and develops, and the urethral mucosa is attacked by gonococcus and its toxins. Inflammation occurs in the mucosa, and the epithelial cells are peeled off. At this time, the patient feels pain when urinating and yellow-white pus flows out, which is the time of acute gonorrhea. However, gonococcus not only invades the surface of the mucosa, but also invades the tissue under the mucosa. Although this invasion of the deep part of the gonococcus causes severe inflammation for a while, the urethral tissue soon undergoes changes due to the inflammation, and because of the accumulation of its own toxins, the reproductive power of gonococcus is significantly weakened. Therefore, the symptoms on the urethra are reduced, just like a cure. In fact, at this time, it has moved to chronic gonorrhea, and the treatment is even more difficult. Moreover, in the case of chronic gonorrhea, gonococcus often lurks in the urethral lateral ducts, Ma's selling, Li's gland, etc. When washing with drug liquid, only the gonococcus on the surface of the urethra can be killed. The lurking gonococcus will still come out to make trouble when it encounters an opportunity.

(3) There is no ideal treatment method because

gonorrhea is difficult to cure. Although there are various treatment methods, there is no ideal good method, that is, there is no method that can completely cure gonorrhea. Now, I will describe all the therapies one by one below:

A. Internal medicine: There are many internal medicines used for gonorrhea, but there is no specific medicine (specific medicine means that a medicine has a specific effect on a certain disease and can cure the root, such as 606 for syphilis, diphtheria serum for diphtheria, quinine for malaria, these can all be called specific medicines). This is the most commonly recognized by the medical community around the world. The most used are sandalwood oil agents, Cuban balm agents, urotropine, methylthionine, etc., all urethral disinfectants, and analgesics, sedatives, anti-inflammatory agents, hemostatics, etc., can be used, but none can be called specific drugs. Moreover, some people have taken sandalwood oil agents and have developed loss of appetite, nausea, vomiting, diarrhea, nephritis, etc. Some people have taken Cuban balm agents and have developed skin rashes. Therefore, medicines can be used, but unfortunately there are no specific drugs.

B. Diathermy: Gonococcus can die when it encounters high heat, but if the urethra needs to get such high heat, the urethral mucosa has already been unbearable for such high heat before the gonococcus dies. Therefore, diathermy therapy, which was started thirty years ago, still failed.

C. Light and electricity: Some people say that light (such as purple light) and electricity can kill gonococcus, but in fact, after various experiments, it has not been recognized by the academic community.

D. Injection of vaccine: Injection

Observations on the Current State of Medicine in Society (Part 1) 217

— Ji Jilin

If someone were to ask: "Which country in the world has the most widespread knowledge of medicine?" Then I can offer an answer without hesitation: "Only the Republic of China." Because no matter how remote and desolate a place you go, if you find an ignorant old woman or old man and ask them, they can at least rattle off many, many names of medicines and their uses – for treating cold or heat, detoxification, or aiding digestion. Moreover, quack doctors hanging up signs to practice, hereditary doctors, specialists in internal medicine, pediatrics, gynecology, and even those selling dog skin plaster and concocting infallible elixirs are ubiquitous.

Logically, since medical knowledge in China is so widespread and there are so many medical experts, the national mortality rate should be the lowest in the world. But the result is quite the opposite. Why is that? To answer this question, let’s first take a look at the general state of medicine in Chinese society.

Deeply rooted in Chinese society and believed by the majority of the people is, of course, traditional Chinese medicine. China is such a large country with such a long cultural history; can it be that there are no effective prescriptions or skilled medical practitioners? Why has Chinese medicine remained stagnant for thousands of years? This requires a discussion of the fundamental problems of Chinese medicine.

Chinese medicine has always been mentioned alongside astrology and divination. Yet the foundation of medicine, which concerns human life, is built on the highly mysterious principles of yin and yang and the five elements. The general public still flocks to it, which is truly perplexing.

Because Chinese medicine lacks a scientific basis, and the government does not have procedures for licensing or registering doctors, anyone who recognizes a few characters and can scribble a jumbled list of memorized drug names into a prescription can hang up a sign and start practicing medicine. Inevitably, people come to them to die. Fortunately, science in China is underdeveloped, so there is no way to verify whether someone died from illness or from being poisoned by medicine. And our people are generally content and accepting of fate: "If they die, then so be it; it's destiny." Among these many executioners – the incompetent doctors – most can be divided into two groups: one is the itinerant quack, who has learned a few catchphrases and remembers some stock terms like wind, cold, heat, dampness, ascent, descent, dissipation, and can then spout nonsense. This group mostly treats external and miscellaneous ailments. The other group is the pedantic scholar: they can’t understand the books they read, can’t make a career in government, find teaching unrewarding, and private schools are being banned. They lack the qualifications and prestige to become local leaders or gentry, and are unable to do anything else. Helpless, they hang up a sign as a Confucian doctor and muddle through. That's another group. Besides these two groups, there are also not a few who transform

Page 16

from shop assistants in pharmacies into doctors. Although their origins are different, they are united in killing without shedding blood. They all believe that "medicine relies on intention," and are accustomed to hearing the mantra "the five elements generate and overcome each other." The only thing that is vaguely unclear in their minds is how many unjustly dead spirits are accumulating under their respective signs.

Since Chinese medicine is so unreliable and everyone values their life, logically it should be declining day by day, and Western medicine should be rising in response. But in fact, the influence of Western medicine in society is still far behind that of Chinese medicine. Why is this?

There is a popular saying in society: "Medicine depends on luck, illness depends on chance." The state of medicine in general society is truly summed up in a single phrase. Because many ailments can heal without medicine, and many ingredients in Chinese medicine are irrelevant or of minimal relevance to the human body, many patients who are examined by a doctor and take Chinese medicine gradually recover. Naturally, the credit is given to the doctor, so both the doctor and the patient are lucky. As for the possibility that the illness might have healed faster without medicine, they don't consider it. As for those who die after taking Chinese medicine, they have another popular saying to explain it: "There is no medicine for fatal illnesses." This is the biggest reason why Chinese medicine can remain popular in general society.

A Scientific Essay on Prenatal Care (11) 218

— Yu Songyun

(2) The Delivery Bed

Ordinary bedding is suitable enough. Soft and thick bedding is actually more inconvenient. Cover the bedding with oilcloth or rubber sheeting, and then cover it with a clean sheet. If you want to be even more meticulous, add another layer of oilcloth or rubber sheeting on top of the sheet, and then cover it with a clean sheet. Be sure to avoid staining the bed with filth during delivery.

If the delivery room is large, the delivery bed can be placed in the center of the room. Otherwise, the mother should face the wall with her head, and her feet toward the end with light.

(3) Delivery Clothing

Delivery clothing should be loose-fitting. A single-layer garment or nightgown is fine. If wearing a long gown, the lower half must be lifted to avoid staining it with blood or other filth. After delivery, immediately change into pre-warmed clothing.

The pillow should be slightly high, and the blanket should be light and thin. Immediately after delivery, change to a thicker blanket to keep warm.

(4) Position to be Taken by the Mother During Childbirth

Each country in the world has its own traditional customs, but even within China, each province, county, township, and village has its own different customs. The most common practice for childbirth is for the mother to sit on a basin. This is presumably to increase the force of expulsion and shorten the duration of labor. Although the intention is profound, excessive force can cause excessive pressure on the uterus, leading to uterine inversion or prolapse, or even premature rupture of the membranes, causing the baby's hand or umbilical cord to prolapse, which is extremely dangerous. The most common practices now

are the "supine position" or the "lateral position." These two positions have little effect on the expulsive force.

For the expulsion and afterbirth stages, or when applying abdominal pressure, the "semi-recumbent position," with the upper body propped up, is most appropriate.

If the uterus is in the correct position, the abdominal wall is sufficiently tense, the fetal position is normal, and the presenting part of the fetus is already fixed in the pelvis, then the mother can take whatever position is comfortable for her.

If the baby's head is still moving at the upper end of the pelvic inlet, then the "supine position" should be taken, because the pelvis is wide. If labor pains are severe and delivery may be too rapid, then the "lateral position" should be taken.

The Aesthetics and Scientific Protection of Breasts (Part 1) 219

— Translated by Tao Bingzhen

Three Types of Breasts

There are originally three shapes of breasts: disc-shaped, hemispherical, and conical. A disc-shaped breast is one in which the height is shorter than the radius of the base. A hemispherical breast is one in which the height is roughly equal to the radius of the base. A conical breast is one in which the tip tapers sharply. Ugly barbarians tend to have conical breasts. As for civilized people, hemispherical and disc-shaped breasts are more common. Moreover, it is best if they are neither too large nor too small. Too large indicates excessive fat; too small indicates weak secondary sexual characteristics. Neither is good for health or beauty.

The Proper Position of Breasts

The most important thing is their position. The ideal position is with the nipple at the fourth rib, or at least at the fifth rib. If both arms are extended to the left and right, draw a straight line from the base of the upper arm along the lower edge of the pectoralis major muscle toward the chest. Also, on the chest line, draw a vertical line connecting the armpit. The intersection of these two lines is where the nipple, the center of the breast, should be located. In that configuration with the curves of the whole body is most beautiful. Moreover, it is best if its position remains unchanged during body movement. The breast must be slightly firm, tight, and strong, with the mammary glands closely attached to the pectoral muscle. If there is too much fat and the skin is loose, then it will immediately droop. When lying down, it will droop to the left and right, making it difficult to maintain a proper position. The nipple should not be too small, too large, or inverted, but should protrude appropriately. The areola surrounding it should be a perfect circle.

The Development Process of Breasts

During infancy, there is no difference between males and females; only a slight trace is visible. Girls from the ages of eleven to thirteen, the nipple and surrounding areola take on a milky red color and rise slightly, this shape resembles a flower bud about to open. Later, the mammary glands inside the breast develop and gradually rise, forming a conical hill. This is the bud-like breast, the state of development of a girl around the age of fifteen or sixteen. After this, it enters the third stage of maturity. Fat increases and the whole body completes a beautiful curve. At the same time, the breast also becomes round and soft due to the subcutaneous fat.

The Destruction of Breast Beauty

If the beauty of mature breasts is not affected by constitution, pregnancy, breastfeeding, living conditions, nourishment, etc., it can be maintained until a considerable old age. However, for most women, once they reach middle age, due to obesity or thinness, the beauty of the breasts disappears.

More Than One Pair of Breasts

The number of breasts is originally limited to one pair, but some women have two pairs, three pairs, or even more. In these women, one pair of breasts develops in the normal way, but there are smaller breasts above and below them. These are usually not very noticeable. However, once pregnant, although small in size, they also develop into the shape of breasts. This is a kind of atavism. It is said that such women are likely to have twins.

Breasts of Different Sizes

Breasts of different sizes only become apparent when the breasts develop to maturity at a considerable age. Most differences are not significant. If the size difference is large, it is ugly. Usually, the left breast is slightly larger.

Prevention of Drooping Breasts

If the attachment of the breast to the pectoral muscle below loosens, its position will change and become a drooping breast. Breasts that are too fatty and have too much fat, and breasts that are too thin and atrophied, often turn into drooping breasts. The method of prevention, of course, requires efforts to protect the breasts during pregnancy and breastfeeding. Paying attention to exercise and gymnastics at ordinary times is also effective, but it is only: exercising muscles to support the breasts, and making the chest protrude to maintain the beauty of the breasts.

Several Important Discoveries and Inventions in the Development of Modern Medicine 220

— Gu Shoubai

In 1776, Priestley discovered nitrous oxide gas; later, Humphry Davy also discovered that this gas has anesthetic properties. Davy then became the Director of the Bristol Institute. He had many opportunities to observe the inhalation of gases. He had also experimented with nitrous oxide. On April 9, 1799, he experimented on himself and found that the gas had toxic effects and could cure toothache. In 1800, he published this fact and suggested that this nitrous oxide could be used in surgery. However, until 1844, no one ever used this gas as an anesthetic. Ether was discovered by Raymond Lully in the 19th century. Later, many people studied its properties, but until 1730, it had not yet been named "ether." Before that, it was only used as a stimulant. In 1795, Pearson of Birmingham used it as an inhalant for asthma and tuberculosis. A few years later, Woolcombe of Plymouth also used ether inhalation to treat asthma attacks and discovered that continued inhalation for a long time would cause the patient to lose consciousness.

In 1818, Michael Faraday reported that inhaling ether vapor could produce the same anesthetic effect as inhaling nitrous oxide. In the following twenty years, the anesthetic properties of ether were further confirmed by many American physicians; however, it had not yet been applied to surgery.

In 1842, American doctor Crawford Long used ether inhalation to excise a small tumor on the neck of a patient; the patient did not feel pain at the time. In September 1846, Morton of Boston, on the advice of C. P. Jackson, used ether to extract a tooth; the patient also felt no pain. Therefore, Morton patented ether in England and the United States under the name "Letheon." On October 16 of that year, he assisted J. C. Warren in using this drug to perform anesthesia and remove a tumor on the neck. This anesthesia was completely successful, which aroused the interest of many doctors present. At that time, because Morton kept the composition of the drug a secret, some surgeons were still hesitant about the application of this drug. However, from that peculiar smell, it was soon known that the composition of this anesthetic was actually ether; thus, the use of this drug became much wider than before. Soon after, the news spread to London. On December 19 of that year, a dentist, Robinson, performed a tooth extraction under ether anesthesia in London. Two days later, Robert Liston of the University Hospital also used ether anesthesia to saw off a patient's leg. This operation only took thirty-two seconds. Because Liston was not yet completely convinced of the effect of ether, he performed the surgery particularly quickly, just as if no anesthesia had been used.

From then on, ether was widely used in surgical operations. Although some people still did not use it at the time, their opposition could not last long.

Dr. James Simpson of Edinburgh adopted ether very early; however, he still felt dissatisfied and wanted to discover a substance that had the advantages of ether but none of its disadvantages. He collected many medicinal liquids that were considered to have anesthetic effects and conducted experiments. Every night, he and his assistants would first inhale one substance and then inhale another to test their relative benefits. They experimented with so many medicinal liquids that it was almost a year before they experimented with chloroform. This chloroform was a medicinal liquid discovered separately by three researchers in 1831. At the time, it was thought to be of little use. Later, Simpson, on the recommendation of Waldie, a chemist from Liverpool, added his small gift for testing and discovered the anesthetic effect of this medicinal liquid.

On November 4, 1847, Simpson and two friends began to inhale chloroform vapor. Soon they all lost consciousness. When they woke up, they realized that they were all lying on the floor. At this time, Simpson realized that chloroform was stronger and better than ether. At that time, they compared and studied each other and were all convinced that what they had discovered was a useful new anesthetic. That night, they experimented several times again, not dispersing until late at night until they obtained satisfactory results. Subsequently, three patients underwent surgery with chloroform anesthesia, and the results were very good.

Soon after, the British immediately began to use chloroform instead of ether; however, around 1868, a change occurred, and a part of the doctors continued to use ether from then on. Now it is said that although Scotland is still using chloroform, England is exclusively using ether. As for the United States, especially the northern part, ether is preferred.

In the tropics, such as in India, chloroform is still more suitable. This is because ether evaporates at lower temperatures, such as around 96 degrees Fahrenheit, while the boiling point of chloroform is at 140 degrees.

Although nitrous oxide was the first anesthetic, it was soon abandoned; however, in 1863, American dentists reintroduced it, saying that it was most convenient for simple operations such as tooth extraction, not only could it completely anesthetize, and it was safe to use, acted quickly, and patients recovered quickly, and there were few unpleasant aftereffects. Because the effect does not last long, its use is limited to tooth extraction and incision of abscesses and other short-term operations. However, in recent years, mixing nitrous oxide with oxygen has also been suitable for longer-lasting surgeries, but the cost is higher. Although there are still various anesthetics and mixtures of various anesthetics, their use is not very large after all. In fact, ether, chloroform, and nitrous oxide are still the most widely used.

No Threats to the Little Entente and Poland

Mutual Consultation to Maintain European Peace for Ten Years

Reuters, Paris, 2nd - The French Ambassador to Italy, Yvon, yesterday issued an article to newspaper reporters, stating that France has accepted the view of the France, Germany, Italy, and England group. However, France is currently very concerned about not threatening the ten countries. Recently, it has been said that the Roman agreement is not a true agreement. He has taken responsibility from Rome to the North, which is of utmost importance, in order to avoid misunderstandings and ensure European peace for ten years.

Those who carry European peace for ten years are using this kind of view in the countries involved, so as not to use excuses that are not conducive to neighboring countries. According to reports, after Italian Prime Minister Mussolini talked with British Prime Minister [MacDonald] in Rome, the above remarks were issued by the French official.

Reuters, Paris, 2nd - The British Ambassador to France yesterday submitted a document to the French Foreign Minister that has been revised from Prime Minister Mussolini's plan submitted to British Prime Minister MacDonald in Rome. According to French newspapers, this document is a completely new draft of the British revised plan. It is closely related to the British Prime Minister's disarmament plan, but there are no unconditional statements regarding treaty revisions.

Havas, Paris, 2nd - French Ambassador to Italy Jouvenel has made an important declaration to the representative of this agency regarding Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's Four-Power Treaty plan, and has further explained that "Mussolini's proposal makes the effectiveness of the Locarno Treaty even more substantial. According to the Locarno Treaty, Britain and Italy guarantee the boundaries between France and Germany, as well as between Belgium and Germany, in order to maintain peace between those countries. If Britain and Italy show a preference for one of the aforementioned countries, the Locarno Treaty will lose its effectiveness. Mussolini's plan does not intend to subject the three continents of Europe, Asia, and America to the will of the four powers. There are other countries on each continent, which were not suddenly dismissed during the four-power talks. This is something that the public should recognize. All current issues can be summarized as follows: Should the four Western powers reach a compromise, or should they allow their respective opinions to exist? The key to the whole situation lies in this."

Havas, Paris, 2nd - Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu continues to meet with various important French figures. This morning, he met with former Prime Minister Taittinger, the leader of the right wing, and in the afternoon, he met with Jouvenel, the recently returned French Ambassador to Italy.

Saito Visits Saionji, Japanese Political Situation Temporarily Stabilizes 238

Retaining Takahashi as Finance Minister and Koyama as Justice Minister

Dentsu, Tokyo, 3rd - Prime Minister Saito arrived at Tokyo Station at 4:50 p.m. yesterday. After returning to his private residence in Yotsuya Minamicho, Chief Cabinet Secretary Horikiri visited him and had a cordial talk for several hours before leaving.

Nichiren, Tokyo, 3rd - Regarding Prime Minister Saito's meeting with Prince Saionji, before reporting to the cabinet meeting, he must obtain the understanding of the elders of the Seiyukai and Minseito parties, Finance Minister Takahashi and Home Minister Yamamoto. The Prime Minister decided to meet with the two ministers before the cabinet meeting on the 4th.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 3rd - Prime Minister Saito plans to summon Finance Minister Takahashi, Home Minister Yamamoto, and Justice Minister Koyama to the official residence separately before the regular cabinet meeting on the 4th to report on the results of his visit to Prince Saionji. He will also openly and honestly express his beliefs regarding the future political situation and seek the opinions of the two elders and Justice Minister Koyama. He also plans to retain Finance Minister Takahashi and Justice Minister Koyama.

Nichiren, Tokyo, 3rd - Minseito observers have temporarily decided on a policy of no political change, restoring the credibility of political parties, and establishing policies, and are now actively carrying out their plans: (1) Establishing policy guidelines, the Policy Investigation Council will establish a new agency to investigate new foreign policies after withdrawing from the League of Nations, as well as the reorganization of administration, finance, and taxation, and concrete methods for ideological education countermeasures. (2) Expanding the youth department, the city council election battle starting on April 8, the headquarters will dispatch a large number of activists to lobby, and President Wakatsuki will control the national lobbying plan.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 3rd - Prime Minister Saito's visit to Prince Saionji is of great significance to the future situation and is highly valued by all parties. However, after the Prime Minister met with Prince Saionji, he strongly denied the rumors of political change and claimed to deal well with the situation, even to the death. Therefore, the voice of political stability spread for a time. However, the Prime Minister's statement was aimed at stabilizing the political situation for a time. In fact, his state of mind was the opposite of this. After the aftermath of the Diet is completed, the May 25th Incident comes to an end, and before the next fiscal year's budget is compiled, he will resign. This was the original intention and remains unchanged to this day. Also, Prince Saionji believes that if Prime Minister Saito resigns at the present time, when it is not yet determined who will succeed him, it is better to let the Prime Minister stay in office temporarily and retire at an appropriate time. This is the truth. Yesterday, at Okitsu, Saionji and Saito met with this intention. On the one hand, Finance Minister Takahashi, the central force of the cabinet, has a very firm intention to resign. Prime Minister Saito is trying his best to retain him because of his associated relationship. However, Finance Minister Takahashi's intention is that there is no problem for the Prime Minister to resign within a few days. If he stays, it is to respect the position of Suzuki, the President of the Seiyukai. It is heard that he has already told the Prime Minister about this matter. The government department plans to approve Finance Minister Takahashi's individual resignation and replace him with someone else in order to extend the life of the cabinet. However, if Finance Minister Takahashi resigns, then Public Works Minister Hatoyama, etc., who also belong to the Seiyukai, will naturally be uneasy. In addition, Justice Minister Koyama, when meeting with the Prime Minister on the 31st, stated that he would take responsibility for the unfortunate incident and wished to resign immediately. Therefore, the Justice Minister will resign after the May 15th Incident and the Redification of Judicial Officials come to an end. As a result, Home Minister Yamamoto, Education Minister Hatoyama, etc., will also not be able to stay calm. Therefore, although the Prime Minister plans to visit each cabinet member separately within a few days, report on the details of the meeting with Prince Saionji, and retain them again, it is impossible for Finance Minister Takahashi to stay in office. Moreover, the Prime Minister himself has always had very weak confidence in his ability to govern the country in times of emergency and will still resign at an appropriate time after observing the situation. This is the general observation.

British Engineer Released on Bail Now Detained Again

Rumors that British Embassy Staff are Preparing to Pack Up and Return Home

Reuters, Moscow, 2nd - Six British technicians from the British company Vickers Electrical Company were previously detained on March 12th, accused of sabotage, hoping to destroy Soviet electrical plants in order to achieve the goal of destroying the Russian electrical industry. Subsequently, all but one were released one after another, but now they have been detained again. Mengkers and Nordwal, the first two who were released on March 14th, were arrested again today and formally charged with espionage of military and economic secrets, sabotage, and serious bribery. The remaining four technicians, three of whom were released on bail, have also been detained, but the charges against them have not yet been announced. What is currently known is that all six will be tried by the Soviet Russian court. Today, the British Charge d'Affaires in Russia, Sterling, accompanied a Soviet Russian prosecutor into the prison to visit. After leaving, he told people that the health of those arrested was normal. There are rumors that the staff of the British Embassy in Russia are now preparing to pack up and return to England, but Reuters has learned from responsible sources in London that there is no basis for the statement that British diplomats stationed in Russia are about to return home or plan to leave the country. British Ambassador to Russia, Voffan, is currently in London and will discuss the arrest of British technicians with the government.

George Bernard Shaw Warns Japan, Saying "Japan Destroys the League of Nations" 243

The Japan English Chronicle published an interview with George Bernard Shaw on March 2, covering China, Japan, the League of Nations, and nationalism. An excerpt of it is as follows:

Shaw spoke about the League of Nations not long after he started to speak with irony. He answered the question of a certain reporter, "Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, do you agree with it? Is it good or bad that I agree with it? Japan has already made up its mind, has already destroyed the League of Nations, and has already proven the League of Nations to be completely useless. The League of Nations has two aspects, this is what you all know. One aspect is the secretariat where officials work, handling diplomatic events. The secretariat convenes meetings, votes on cases, and prepares reports, but no one has ever paid any attention. I have attended a meeting once, and I never want to participate in it again, because this kind of meeting is just a conversation to seek nothing."

The other aspect of the League of Nations activities, the International Labour Office, was praised by Shaw. He sketched out its organization, saying that it was a "very disorganized group" that had always done good work there before.

He continued, "But you have already overthrown that aspect, dismantled their arena."

"They should have taken some action when you first dealt with China and first broke the alliance, they should have severed ties with your alliance, without any scruples, but they did not take any action, and they never thought of taking any action, they instead sold arms to China and Japan, and they are still selling arms, you have provoked this war, you can not win by courage or Bushido, but by armaments, the ancient style of risking one's life and dying for honor has passed, and now the infantry charge will not be better than what I saw in 1914, when the infantry charge was just a ridiculous massacre, you are not like that, you are preparing to use armaments to defeat them (referring to the Chinese), and they must also prepare to use armaments to defeat you, as long as they can."

All Wars are Self-Defense

"You say everything is self-defense, you are fighting for self-defense, you must know that all wars are self-defense, your past actions have been very appropriate, because you have not declared war."

"But if the League of Nations intends to just do some official business, and if you only intend to let others abuse your power and do the work of slaughter and destruction, then what is the use of the League of Nations?"

"However, in the capacity of a third party, I am anxious to know whether you ask yourself, what is the benefit of what you have done for you? Now I am an Irishman, Ireland is a small vegetable garden of a country, with about four million residents, and England has forty million residents, but England wants to prevent the Irish from restoring their nationality, and will not succeed in the end, in order to suppress the Irish, they have also abused the policy of iron and blood, and carried out the means of burning and killing, the Irish leader Michael Collins, once said that for every milk shop that is destroyed, he must burn two suburban villas as revenge, have you considered this point? In 'Manchukuo,' there are 28 million Chinese, how do you plan to pacify them? You cannot handle this matter with the police, the police are useless no matter what, if the residents do not allow him to enter, it will be useless at all, the Chinese will certainly not do this, so you cannot avoid this current problem, that is, whether you are prepared to suppress them for the next few hundred years."

Mr. Shaw reminded the person who was visiting him that he was seventy years old, and when he was young, England had a kind of horse-drawn carriage, and sometimes the horse would slip and fall on the ground.

"What happens when a horse slips and falls? Why do everyone hurry to sit on the horse's head? It's nothing more than because if the horse struggles to stand up, it will definitely move the harness and the shaft, and the carriage may overturn." "Suppressing patriotism is like sitting on the horse's head, and there is no time to do other things, the Irish have made the British parliament unable to do anything but discuss the Irish issue for more than 30 years, this is a proof."

"If you have to spend the next hundred years riding the horse's head, then what will you encounter? Who is preparing to work there, or must this work be done? Nationalists or patriots will never come to do it, they are busy making speeches." Idiots Embracing Nationalism

Mr. Shaw interrupted with a little bit of discussion about nationalism when he spoke here.

"Any idiot can say the words of a nationalist, any idiot can talk about freedom and historical glory, since nationalism is easy, it can also be a big obstacle to the public, when you finally lay the foundation of your country, you will probably feel that you must shoot the nationalists as soon as possible, but at this moment, the work is stopped, have you really looked far away and investigated all of this? When conquering China, have you thought about what kind of situation Japan will become? Riots and intimidation will arise one after another, and you will eventually feel that peace is impossible unless every Chinese person, you send a policeman to monitor him."

While Mr. Shaw was giving this high-profile speech, the reporters' pencils stopped moving. Mr. Shaw may have noticed this, and not long after, he took the opportunity to say that he had passed his proper age and had reached a period in which everyone began to look at him and secretly said that he had lived to such an old age and was still ignorant of the times. "You must understand that I can ignore everything, if I were still only twenty years old, I would never speak bluntly."

The Meaning of Bushido

Someone corrected him and said, "There is also Bushido."

Okay, what is the meaning of Bushido, what is Bushido, is it what you call patriotism? A patriot is a person who makes himself and his country ridiculed and must probably be shot."

Mr. Shaw began to ask his own questions.

What religion do you believe in? Since you are newspaper reporters, you probably don't believe in religion, but... what religion do the people of... believe in? Are they Buddhists, or Shintoists, or other religions?"

Mr. Shaw is really a clear person.

"You must understand that I look at all kinds of religions together, I am very curious about religions, there is a part of truth in every religion, so I believe in all of them, but all religions have gone astray, such as the Buddhism here in your place, it is not real Buddhism, you are just setting up a statue of an Indian Shinto, to deceive the people and pray for blessings."

"What do I want to visit in Japan? There is nothing to see, I don't want to visit anything, I just came here by chance, I wanted to take a long trip, so I boarded this ship, I heard that this ship was going to this place, I came here without end, I am writing a play to comfort myself, writing a play is my career, just like the career of a shoemaker is sewing boots."

However, Mr. Shaw admits that he is curious about Japan's Kabuki-za, playhouses for performing songs and dances, and music, as long as Japanese dramas are not like the Chinese, who all hum the same unnatural tune.

At that time, several Beppu visitors arrived, and Mr. Shaw only said that he was very interested in his trip to North China, and that General Zhang Xueliang was an educated and refined person, completely unlike the warlord he had imagined before. After saying these two sentences, he ran away.

Newspaper Discusses America's Ambition Toward the South Seas Islands 244

Seeking Mandate Territory from Japan

Planning to Ensure Air Control in the Pacific

According to the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun on March 27, the situation regarding the return of the South Seas Islands under Japanese mandate is becoming increasingly urgent worldwide. In addition to Japan and Germany having begun preparations for negotiations, the United States, due to Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, has expressed a tendency to intervene. The reason is that the South Seas issue is closely related to American Far East policy. Recently, the ambition of the U.S. Navy and Air Force to advance into the Far East has been fully exposed. In order to connect its fundamental routes, the US intends to secure the route across the South Pacific with the following locations: San Francisco, Honolulu, Midway Island, Wake Island, Guam Island, Philippines. By gaining control over this air route, this secures its military advance into the Far East. If the South Seas Islands in this air route were under Japan's control, the United States would feel uneasy about its advance into the East. Therefore, the US military has been trying hard to remove the South Seas Islands from Japan's control. At the same time, the United States incited the Southwest faction in China to start a war against Japan and established a naval aviation base in Guangdong. On the surface, the United States seems to be assisting the Southwest faction, but in reality, the United States is preparing for a war against Japan. In the event of a sudden crisis in the Pacific, Japan might seize the Philippines. Therefore, the US plans to cut off the connection between Japan and the Philippines and ensure an air base at the shortest distance from Japan. However, the only major obstacle to the implementation of naval air control in the Pacific is Japan's South Seas Mandate territory. For this reason, the United States, taking advantage of Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, is seizing the opportunity to take the mandate territory from Japan.

Opening of the Four-Province Farmers Bank 245

Two Million Yuan in Savings Received on the First Day

Approximately 500,000 Auxiliary Currency Vouchers Issued

Henan, Anhui, and Jiangxi Have Sent Personnel to Prepare for Establishing Branches

Hankou correspondence: The Four-Province Farmers Bank of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi, after several months of preparation, with a capital of 10 million yuan, has been fully paid up to one-fourth. According to the regulations of the headquarters, it can be opened for business. All important staff members have already been announced a few days ago. The directors are Xu Fu, Jia Shiyi, Zhou Xingtang, Pu Zhengdong, Zhou Cangbai, Wang Zhengying, and Guo Waifeng. The supervisors are Ye Yu, Wen Qun, Li Jihong, and Mao Bingli. Guo Waifeng is the General Manager, Chen Huaizhong is the Assistant Manager, Jin Xueteng is the Director of the General Affairs Department, Guo Jian is the Director of the Business Department, Ling Jingshan is the Director of the Voucher Department, Ni Wenshuo is the Director of the Accounting Department, and Chen Jian is the Director of the Investigation Department. The internal arrangements were completed, and it officially opened for business on the first of this month. The flag was raised at 9:00 a.m., and Guo Waifeng opened the door, and then the business began. No ceremony was held. Many military and political figures went to congratulate. Also, whenever a bank opens, the industry has a tradition of "piling flowers", that is, sending deposits of cash. On that day, the bank received 1.93 million yuan in silver coins and 681,514 taels, 3 mace, and 9 fen of silver from the silver shops in the city, totaling more than 2 million yuan. In terms of business, the savings department received more than 300,000 yuan in savings deposits from various households. Auxiliary currency vouchers of 10 cents, 20 cents, and 50 cents were issued for more than 100,000 yuan. Approximately 500,000 yuan was transported to the provinces of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi. At the beginning of business, the bank issued a declaration, stating the main purpose, saying "The four provinces of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi have suffered bandit disasters, and the rural economy has been completely destroyed. Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission and Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, Chiang [Kai-shek], is extremely concerned and believes that post-disaster reconstruction must be based on revitalizing the rural economy and promoting the improvement and progress of silkworm industry production, and especially establishing farmers' banks to provide farmers with funds as the foundation for rural revitalization. Our bank bears this important responsibility, and the management and planning are all carried out in accordance with this main purpose and actively carried out. Now, the head office has been established in Hunan Street, Special District Three, Hankou, and business has started today. Within the four provinces, branch offices and sub-branches will be established in sequence. We are saddened by the outflow of funds from our country, the rising cost of living, the destruction by bandits, and the withering of agriculture. The way to save the country and resist foreign aggression must rely on strengthening national strength. Our China is founded on agriculture, and farmers are the largest majority. The decline of farmers in the four provinces in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River is related to the prosperity and decline of the national strength of the whole country. Our bank specializes in the business that farmers' banks should have and will do its best to assist farmers. However, the rural organizations in the four provinces are mostly unsound. Although cooperatives are being promoted, the actual number of those established is considerable, but in proportion to the number of households and population, it seems that it is not yet sufficient. Our bank and the rural cooperative have the relationship of auxiliary wheels. We especially hope that the authorities and enlightened people in the four provinces will fully promote the universal organization of cooperatives to assist our bank in order to achieve the effect of using funds. Our bank itself will also strive to promote sound progress gradually in order to live up to Chairman Chiang's hard work in creating and the ardent expectations of the people of the four provinces." It is heard that the bank has decided to establish branches in Anqing, Kaifeng, and Nanchang, and sub-branches in Jiujiang, Wuhu, and Zhengzhou. Ouyang Hancun has been sent to Nanchang to prepare first, and the staff preparing for Kaifeng and Anqing can also be appointed within a few days. (April 1)

Red Bandit Harassment in Southern Jiangxi, Xunwu 246

Gangster Chief Gu Dacun of Eastern Guangdong Surrounded and Suppressed

Shantou Correspondence: Red bandits in southern Jiangxi, surrounded on all sides by the National Army and facing difficulties in finding food, are fleeing in desperation, seeking to survive. In early March, a fake Independent 3rd Division and 10th Division, numbering about six or seven hundred, arrived at Xun Guan from Anyuan. They attacked the local militia in a village west of the county. Troops of the Yue Army's Ye Shou Regiment, stationed in Che, launched a two-pronged attack, routing the bandits, who retreated into Xunwu City. The bandits immediately gathered local people from the bandit areas near Xunwu City, forcibly organizing hundreds of them into spear and shield teams. On the fourth, they attacked Xiang Mountain, east of Xunwu, which is a very strategic location. The local militia, led by Pan Jin-di, had been stationed there with over a hundred men. For more than a year, the bandits had attacked many times, but all failed. That day, the bandits advanced from all sides, and after a fierce battle all day, the militia, outnumbered and without ammunition or reinforcements, was finally forced by Pan Jin-di to lead the men safely to Pingyuan County in Guangdong via the ridge of Xiang Mountain. At that time, one group of bandits, numbering about a hundred, detoured around the back of Xiang Mountain from Congkeng, pretending to be National Army reinforcements. The refugees fleeing Xiang Mountain fell for the ruse, and over four hundred were tied up in Duihe. All the clothing and luggage they had managed to carry out were looted. After the fall of Xiang Mountain, the villages and towns of Congkeng and Dazhong on the border of Fujian and Guangdong were successively raided by bandits. The villages of Huyang Xin Village on the Guangdong side and Pingyu Jiuguo on the Fujian side were robbed several times a day. The suffering was unprecedented. On the eleventh, after the bandits had plundered to their fill, they retreated to Jianxi, Cixi, and other places in Xunwu territory, leaving only a few Red Guards to guard Xiang Mountain. After this battle, the number of refugees on the Guangdong side increased even more.

Also, the gangster chief Gu Dacun of Eastern Guangdong Province is hiding in the mountains of Baxiang in Fengshun County. Chen Jitang had offered a reward of 20,000 yuan for Gu's capture, but so far he has not been found. Gu has a bodyguard of forty people, twenty-four Mauser pistols, two light machine guns, and five rifles. On the nineteenth, the military police stationed in Fengshun carried seven days' worth of dry rations and searched for him in Houyan and other places in Baxiang Mountain. Meixian also sent police to Ye Tian to encircle him. On the morning of the twenty-second, the First Company engaged in a fierce battle with the bandits below the stone wall of Daqiwei. Company Commander Yang Zikuan and Deputy Su Jiezhong bravely charged and fought hand-to-hand, killing the bandit squad leader Wu Yaliu, beheading him, and seizing a gun. Gu Dacun, wearing a military uniform, fled into the deep mountains. That day, the Second Battalion also launched a raid against the bandits from Jiulongzhang, killing more than ten bandits and beheading two. The bandits' arrogance has been slightly suppressed.

Anhui Province Handles the Aftermath of the Establishment of Lihuang County 247

Selecting a Special Commissioner for Post-Disaster Relief

Assisting in County Administration Design

Anqing Correspondence: The bandit suppression headquarters decided to establish Lihuang County in Jinjiazai, which belongs to Liu'an County in western Anhui. Forty-five wards were demarcated from Liu'an, Huoshan, and Huoqiu Counties in Anhui and Gushi County in Henan. Recently, the headquarters has confirmed that the county belongs to Anhui. The Anhui Civil Affairs Department submitted a request to the provincial government to appoint Yan Er'ai as the county magistrate of the county (Yan was appointed by the headquarters). On March 28, at the 180th meeting of the provincial government, the Civil Affairs Department proposed that a special commissioner be sent to the county to comfort the disaster-stricken people and to handle the design of the county administration. After discussion, it was decided to rename the Comfort Commissioner as a Special Commissioner for Post-Disaster Relief, and the main points of the design are as follows: (1) In order to establish the foundation of Lihuang County's administration, the provincial government will select a Special Commissioner for Post-Disaster Relief to work with the county magistrate to plan all reforms. (2) The Special Commissioner for Post-Disaster Relief will, in accordance with the following items, work with the county government to understand the actual local conditions and propose various implementation plans: 1. Matters concerning rural improvement and the livelihood of unemployed farmers; 2. Matters concerning various productions and production education; 3. Matters concerning the construction of highways and the establishment of telecommunications bureaus; 4. Matters concerning the division of regions and the establishment of district offices for compiling and checking the baojia household registration. (3) The design period is limited to two months. (4) This outline will be abolished after the design is completed. (5) This outline will be implemented after being decided by the government committees (March 30).

Issues Concerning the Sino-German Joint Steel Plant 248

The Ministry of Industry Explores the Coal Reserves of Leijia Gou

The Location of the Plant is Still Unresolved

The total capital of the Sino-German joint steel plant was originally set at 80 million yuan. However, due to the outbreak of the war, Minister Chen Gongbo, considering that it would be difficult to raise 40 million yuan, decided with the German Xiwang Company to reduce the capital to 50 million yuan, which would still be borne jointly by both parties. The current Ministry of Industry has sent technicians to Leijia Gou to explore the coal reserves there and will conduct a detailed test to determine whether the coal quality is suitable for smelting steel. Details are recorded below.

Reducing Loans 249

When the Ministry of Industry and the German Xiwang Company were proceeding with the joint steel plant, the total capital was originally set at 80 million yuan, with each party raising 40 million yuan. However, the 40 million yuan to be borne by the Xiwang Company could be offset by a portion of the machinery. Therefore, the German side expressed considerable support for this proposal from the Ministry of Industry. However, due to various reasons, the formal contract has not yet been signed. After the outbreak of the war, central finances were inevitably affected. Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo, considering that it would be difficult to raise 40 million yuan in cash, repeatedly consulted with representatives of the Xiwang Company on the proposal to reduce the capital of the steel plant. Finally, it was decided to reduce it from 80 million yuan to 50 million yuan, which would still be borne jointly by both parties, and a draft agreement was signed to proceed with the exploration of the Leijia Gou coal mine.

Exploring Coal Mines 250

At the suggestion of Minister Chen Gongbo of the Ministry of Industry, the best location for the plant would be either in Ma'anshan or Leijia Gou, because the coal reserves in these two places are abundant. However, the German representatives strongly advocated locating it in Zhaojiagou, fifteen li from Pukou. However, the Ministry of Industry did not agree because of national defense considerations. After repeated discussions, the German representatives finally agreed to first explore the coal reserves in Leijia Gou and test the quality of the coal produced to determine whether it could be used for smelting steel in order to determine whether it was suitable for construction. The Ministry of Industry has now sent technicians to Leijia Gou to arrange for exploration. As for whether the coal quality is suitable, it will be decided after a detailed test by the German representatives of the contract.

Predicting Plant Location 251

As for the location of the steel plant, although the German representatives no longer insist on locating it in Zhaojiagou, they have not yet made a definite decision on Leijia Gou and Ma'anshan. According to news from our side, the Ministry of Industry believes that if the above two locations are still not suitable for building a steel plant, it will send personnel to the upper reaches of Hankou to find a new location. However, this proposal must be discussed with the German representatives after the coal quality test of Leijia Gou.

Northeast Association to Hold Executive Council Meeting Tomorrow 252

Underground Righteous Armies in the Three Provinces are Actively Planning

Since its establishment, the Northeast Association has focused on planning the activities of righteous armies within the three provinces. Recently, underground righteous armies in the eastern parts of Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces have been launching attacks, disrupting the defenses of the Japanese and puppet troops. However, due to the fact that the spring screening season has not yet begun, there is no safe cover, so the date for a large-scale uprising will have to wait until May or June. The first executive council meeting will be held tomorrow at 4:00 PM to discuss association affairs and the solicitation of members, and work will begin after the meeting.

Japan's Karafuto Timber Company Stealing Timber for Dumping in China 253

The First Batch of Over Two Thousand Tons Arrived in Port Yesterday

Five Thousand Tons Will Continue to Arrive in Shanghai Tomorrow

The Northeast region is the most abundant forest area in our country, with annual exports of over 70 million yuan. Since the September 18th Incident in Shenyang, the forests in the Northeast have also been seized by the Japanese, and the Karafuto Timber Company has been officially established to manage all export affairs. Recently, due to the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and the Soviet Union, Soviet timber exports to China have been increasing rapidly. The Shanghai representative of the Japanese Karafuto Company, in order to compete for sales, telegraphed the company to quickly arrange for the shipment of large quantities of timber to Shanghai in order to meet market demand. Therefore, when the Japanese ship Shengjing Maru sailed from Dalian to Shanghai yesterday, it carried over two thousand five hundred tons of timber, and another five thousand tons will continue to arrive in port tomorrow. According to Japanese merchants, the Chinese timber market will be dominated by Japan and Russia in the future, but the Soviet Union will inevitably fail because the transportation of timber from the Northeast to China is faster than from the Soviet Union, and the lower prices are a fatal blow to Russian merchants.

Sino-German Aviation to Conduct Test Flight Next Month 256

New Aircraft Will Fly from Germany to Shanghai

Regarding the matter of Sino-German air traffic, a reporter from the Central News Agency visited Mr. Li Jingzong, manager of the Eurasia Aviation Company, this morning at the company. According to him, plans for Eurasia air traffic have been in the works for a long time, but have not been realized due to various reasons. A telegram from Berlin recently stated that the Sino-German air traffic test flight is scheduled for May 1. However, according to what this person knows, in order to develop the aviation industry, Eurasia Aviation Company previously ordered five aircraft from Germany. Two aircraft have been shipped to Shanghai by sea and are being assembled. The remaining three aircraft are scheduled to fly from Germany to Shanghai via Russia in May for the first Sino-German air traffic test flight. The Sino-German route is 9,000 kilometers long, so it will take six days to arrive. After the aircraft arrives in Shanghai for a test flight, the test flight results will be studied before a decision is made on the date of the air traffic. As for the Northwest route, it has already been opened to Dihua. However, the section from Dihua to Tacheng is sparsely populated and there are very few passengers, so it may be difficult to realize in the short term.

China National Aviation Corporation is a Sino-US joint venture, with the Chinese side holding 55% of the shares and the US side holding 45%. However, this move has nothing to do with the Chinese shares, as it is a transfer procedure outside the company. Umbrella Industry Workers Petition 260

To Visit the Social Affairs Bureau Today

Demanding a Livelihood

Recently, over twenty companies in the city's umbrella industry, including Huanqiu, have organized a joint business office, forcing various factories to join, causing eleven companies, including Hualishi, to suspend operations. Workers petitioned the Social Affairs Bureau this morning. The various suspended factories plan to submit the bylaws of the business office to the Party and government for their opinions. Details are recorded below.

(Workers' Petition) This morning, the workers of the various suspended factories each sent a representative, including Hua Lishi Gongshi He, Xin Dalu Lu Amei, Da Youyu Sun Shida, Zhixin Chen Junyi, Fengli Zhu Wanhe, Tailai Wang Tongfa, Dongnan Min Liangcai, Nanchang Lu Yiming, Ruilin Cao Renqing, Sanyuan Cai Dehuai, Ming Huasen Yao Cancheng, and others, totaling eleven people, to the Social Affairs Bureau to petition, demanding that the factories be ordered to resume operations in order to maintain the workers' livelihoods. They were received by Wang Xianqing of the Third Section, who promised to send personnel to thoroughly investigate and then convene a mediation.

(The Capitalists' Opinions) According to Zhu Chunbo, manager of Hualishi, the organization of the National Goods Umbrella Trade Joint Business Office by over twenty factories, including Minhua 1233 Factory, Huanqiu, Nanhua, Yingfeng, Huadong, Minghua, Xintai Long, Dahua, Xin Dahua, etc., is, on the surface, to promote national goods, which is something that should be done in the current era. However, the various factories that have suspended operations cannot sympathize with the methods and bylaws that have been set. For example, Article 3 of the bylaws states that the output of each factory joining the office shall not exceed the reported number per day, but when market demand increases or decreases, it can be adjusted proportionally by the office. Article 6 stipulates that six jiao per dozen of goods will be deducted from the price paid to each factory as operating expenses. Article 7 stipulates that factories joining the office shall not sell privately, and if discovered, a fine of 200 yuan per dan will be imposed, and retail sales must be made through the office. All profits belong to the interests of the business office. It should be known that after deducting various expenses, each factory only profits two jiao per dozen umbrellas, so adding expenses will only result in losses, and there are no profits to be made. There is no choice but to suspend operations, which is a result of being oppressed. We only hope for the workers' understanding and plan to submit these unfair bylaws to the Party and government for adjudication.

The Fifth District Administrative Commissioner's Office Will Be Established 262

Zhen Fei to Visit Yan Shenzi Today

Commissioner's Office Organization and Procedures

Cao Zhenfei, the administrative police commissioner for the Shanghai-Chuansha-Baoshan District and concurrent county magistrate of Shanghai County, arrived in Shanghai and is scheduled to visit Yan Shenzi at the Baoshan County Government today to discuss the date of takeover. He will also establish the Commissioner's Office in Shanghai immediately. Details of Cao's brief biography and the office's organization are recorded below.

Cao's Brief Biography 263

Mr. Cao is a native of Yangzhou, Jiangsu Province, and is 46 years old this year. He was a tribute student in the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty and passed the examination for county magistrate in the fourth session. He has served as the county magistrate of Yanshi, Baofeng, and Anqing in Henan and Anhui. He is currently the Administrative Inspector Commissioner of the Fifth District of Jiangsu Province and concurrent county magistrate of Shanghai County.

Office Organization 264

The office organization includes one commissioner (appointed as a simplified position), one secretary (recommended position), two to four staff members (appointed positions), two or three investigators (appointed positions), and two clerks.

Responsibilities 265

The administrative commissioner concurrently serves as the county magistrate of the first county and the director of the district security branch (the organization of the security branch will be determined separately). His responsibilities are: (1) The commissioner handles the affairs of the district under the orders of the provincial government director and the chiefs of various departments; (2) The commissioner directs and supervises the county government in implementing laws and regulations; (3) The commissioner assesses the county magistrates and government officials in the district for corruption, laziness, and other illegal activities; (4) The commissioner suppresses bandits in the district and investigates security matters in the district; (5) Inter-district related matters; (6) Inter-county related matters.

Robbery Case on Tangshan Road 266

Loss of Three Thousand Yuan and Injury to the Victim

Reporting the Case and Requesting Strict Arrest and Prosecution

Yesterday (the second) late at night, around 11:00 PM, He Laowu, residing at 422 Tangshan Road, Hongkou District, was robbed because he had just received a hui loan of four hundred yuan, resulting in a thorough search of his home and a gunshot wound to He Laowu's right leg. The robbers then left. Details are recorded below.

Hui Loan of Four Hundred Yuan Causes Trouble 267

The victim, He Laowu, is over forty years old. Yesterday, he received a hui loan of four hundred yuan in Pudong and brought the money home at 10:00 PM. Unexpectedly, the robbers heard about it and caused trouble. Around 11:00 PM, five robbers, two guarding outside the door and three entering the house, held pistols and monitored all the people in the house, prohibiting them from making noise. One robber conducted a thorough search, only leaving at 12:20 AM this morning, shouting and firing a shot, wounding He Laowu in the right leg.

Loss of Three Thousand, Reporting the Case and Requesting Prosecution 268

Last night, in addition to the hui loan of four hundred yuan, there were also soft goods, clothing, jewelry, and other items, totaling a loss of around three thousand yuan. The injured victim, He Laowu, was sent to the hospital for treatment this morning and reported the case to the Hongkou police, requesting strict arrest and prosecution of the criminals.
