Fellow Provincials from Sichuan Mourn Wang Runbo 274

Martyred in Action Against the Japanese at Gubeikou

The Sichuan Kai County Alumni Association of Students from Beijing and Shanghai held a meeting yesterday morning at 11:00 AM at the Shanghai Lawyers Association, located at the intersection of Baylor Road and Lafayette Road in the French Concession, to mourn Wang Runbo, the head of the regiment who was martyred in the war of resistance against Japan. Many people attended. After the meeting began as scheduled, Chairman Wei Anzhi reported that the martyr graduated from the third term of the Huangpu Military Academy, dedicated himself to the revolution, and always possessed a spirit of sacrifice. He was the current regimental commander of the 149th Regiment of the 25th Division of the National Army. This time, he fought against the Japanese at Gubeikou, leading by example and sacrificing himself. His loyalty and bravery are exemplary. He also gave a speech, calling out slogans such as "The spirit of the martyrs will not die." The meeting adjourned. The eulogy is attached below: "On April 3, 22nd year of the Republic of China, the fellow provincials from Kai County who are traveling to Beijing and Shanghai, with fresh flowers, clear fruit, and sincere hearts, pay tribute to the portrait of the regimental commander Wang Runbo, the martyr who died in the war of resistance against Japan, and mourn with the following words: Alas, the violence of Japan's invasion has lasted for half a lifetime. They forcibly occupied the eastern provinces and attacked Shanghai. Their ambition has not ended, and the flames of the invaders are even more fierce. They advanced into Rehe, plundered and raped without restraint, destroying the remnants of justice and peace. We hate our superiors who did not resist at all, abandoned their posts and fled, leading the invaders into the hall. The fall of Chengde made Tianjin and Beijing panic. Outside the Great Wall, the bandit's power was like a frenzy. They wanted to destroy us and dominate the East. Only our martyr, disregarding his own safety, led the troops north, defending Gubeikou, launching a great crusade, and being the bravest of the three armies, discouraging the enemy's courage. He charged and fought in close combat in the bloody battlefield. The isolated army fought hard, but it was difficult to last for long. The enemy outnumbered us, and you died in battle. Alas, martyr, your spirit is magnificent. Wrapped in horse hide, a man's ambition is strong. Your great achievements will be passed down for generations, achieving benevolence and taking righteousness, shaking up cowards and awakening the foolish. The death of the martyr is the light of the nation. Alas, please accept our offerings."

Procedures for Transferring Opium Offenders from Nantong 275

Yao Zichun Temporarily Detained

Awaiting Evidence Before Transfer

Regarding the government's policy of banning opium through taxation, Jiangsu Province has also established a Narcotics Investigation Bureau under provincial orders, with branches in various counties specifically for investigation and enforcement. Nantong serves as the fifth branch. Locally, the trafficking of narcotics has seen red pills surpass opium in sales, and the profits are even greater. Consequently, a large-scale red pill manufacturing operation was established locally and flourished greatly. Since the establishment of the fifth branch, this operation has been deemed illegal and harmful to society, even more so than opium. Therefore, the facility was sealed off last month, and fifteen key offenders were arrested and sent back to Zhenjiang, where they were detained at the Narcotics Investigation Bureau. The director has repeatedly interrogated them to uncover accomplices. Recently, an old offender confessed that Yao Zichun from Xiamen, Fujian, was one of the masterminds behind the manufacturing operation. However, Yao had already fled to Shanghai during the arrests and was hiding in the concessions, evading the law. In addition to sending a formal letter to the First Special District Court of Shanghai requesting extradition, the Narcotics Investigation Bureau also instructed investigator Fan Mingfu to come to Shanghai to track down Yao. Yesterday, it was discovered that Yao was hiding at 25 Changfeng Lane on Tongban Road. The investigators immediately contacted the Xinzha Police Station, requesting additional detectives to raid the address and arrest Yao. This morning, Yao was escorted to the First Special District Court, where Judge Hua Yugui conducted a preliminary hearing. Wang Yaotang, the police station's lawyer, stated that according to the agreement, any extradition request must be accompanied by substantial evidence. This case only relies on an official letter, which seems insufficient to prove criminal suspicion. Since it is claimed that Yao was implicated by an accomplice's confession, the authorities should be ordered to produce that confession before extradition can be granted. Judge Liu briefly questioned Yao and ordered his temporary detention, pending the Narcotics Investigation Bureau's submission of evidence for further review.

170 Pounds of Opium 276

Discovered by Detectives on Jichang Road

Sun Caiyuan Claims Friend Entrusted Him

Yesterday morning at 6:40 AM, Ding Baoxiang, a Chinese detective of the Hongkou Police Station, detectives Mu Chunrong, Indian constables Nos. 341 and 146, and Chinese constable No. 1825 of Santoudu, saw several people on Jichang Road loading two leather suitcases and two baskets into car No. 17885, which was parked there. Suspecting their behavior, they moved forward to arrest them. A Ningbo man named Sun Caiyuan was apprehended on the spot. Upon opening the suitcases and baskets, they found opium weighing a total of 170 pounds, worth over fifty dollars. The car driver, a local named Shen Fulin, was also taken into custody. This morning, Xiao Xiexun, a judge from the First Special District Court, accompanied by prosecutor Ren Zuzhe, conducted an interrogation at the Third Criminal Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, presented the facts and stated that Sun Caiyuan confessed at the police station that Chen Jinshan, a friend working at the Ruhe Wheel office in Hankou, had asked him to wait at the dock and receive items to be carried and collect payments, but he was unaware that they were opium. According to Sun, Chen Jinshan is from Hankou, tall and thin with a long face. Shen Fulin, the driver, stated that the person who hired the car spoke with a Ningbo accent and was fat. The two testimonies did not match, and a request was made for an extension for further investigation. The opium was then presented for inspection. Constables Nos. 341 (Indian) and 1825 (Chinese) testified that there were many people present at the time of the arrest and that the others had left in Chen Yi's car. Questioned about this, Sun Caiyuan stated that the opium did not belong to him and that he was there to collect payment from Chen Jinshan, a Sanbei native, and was mistakenly arrested. He retained lawyer Ge Zhaoji to represent him. However, Chinese constable No. 1825 stated that Sun Caiyuan was already in the car at the time of the arrest. Shen Fulin stated that he worked as a driver for the Zhejiang Automobile Company at 739 Zhejiang Road. A man in Western attire came to hire the car. This person had a yellow complexion, a stout build, and spoke with a Ningbo accent. He told him to drive to the location and wait, then got out of the car and boarded the ship. After a while, two laborers dressed in blue cloth brought the leather suitcases, etc., and he did not know they were opium. He asked for consideration. Judge Xiao ordered their continued detention, with a rescheduled hearing in seven days.

Commentary

China Will Not Perish 277

— Geng

Since the unfortunate confrontation in the Sino-Japanese War of 1894, China's national destiny has been constantly facing setbacks, incurring financial losses and substantial population decline almost every year. The year before last was particularly disastrous, plunging thirty million compatriots into misery and turning the beautiful landscape of 3.8 million square miles into a scene of desolation. The insatiably greedy Japanese aggressors are now using aircraft, bombs, cannons, tanks, and other weapons of war in Rehe, actively committing inhumane acts of slaughter. Faced with such trials and emotions, the Chinese people are deeply saddened and worried about the imminent demise of their nation.

However, the principle of "heaven's justice prevails" and "good fortune follows extreme adversity" suggests that as China's national destiny has deteriorated to its nadir, it may be the turning point for a prosperous future.

In terms of divine will, the imperialist executioners, warlords, and financial magnates of Japan are constantly being assassinated. The Japanese Emperor himself was once alarmed. Although the traitor Zheng Xiaoxu survived an assassination attempt, the sudden death of his beloved son Zheng Chui, the puppet mayor of Changchun, may be divine retribution. The heroic generals Ma, Su, Feng, and Li, who have been fighting hard in Northeast China for years, have safely escaped, which may be due to divine protection. Furthermore, the monk Quan He has donated one hundred thousand "divinely blessed yellow bags." It is unknown what kind of divine courage the soldiers at the front will have when they wear these bags.

In terms of popular sentiment, people of all backgrounds in the country aspire to "love the country," discuss "saving the nation," hear about "sharing national difficulties," and witness "resistance articles." Even the merchants, who were previously hesitant and unreliable in boycotting enemy goods, have now issued a notice stating that "daily necessities of clothing, food, housing, and transportation, except for the 'unavoidable,' should all be Chinese goods." Furthermore, inspiring slogans such as "long-term resistance" and "sacrificing family fortunes to relieve national distress" are widely supported by both military and civilians.

In terms of geographical advantages, China is vast in territory and rich in resources, blessed by nature. The winding Great Wall can temporarily prevent the southward advance of the invading army, and the river and sea mouths are heavily fortified to prevent enemy ships from easily entering. Stepping back, if necessary, the tactic of "attacking from high ground" can be adopted by relocating the entire nation to the Pamir Plateau and establishing the headquarters on the highest peak of Mount Everest, thus avoiding enemy aircraft. When the enemy attempts to attack uphill, they can be repelled by simply throwing down rocks and wood, causing them to tumble and retreat in disarray.

In terms of military affairs, the national army consists of two million troops, who have gained abundant combat experience through years of actual combat practice. Therefore, reviewing the history of anti-Japanese battles since the September 18th Incident, there is not a single record of "defeat," which is indeed significant. Just as the French dictionary does not contain the word "difficult," China's war history will henceforth be free of the word "defeat," creating a magnificent echo between East and West.

From this, it can be concluded that "China will not perish" is a certainty. If we continue to abandon the right to complacency and indulge in unnecessary worries, we would not only be foolish but also undermine the national character of a great nation. How can we allow that? How can we allow that?

Literature and Art

Miscellaneous Poems on Shanghai, Eight Long Sentences 279

— Yu Heqin

Nine avenues, beautiful trees lined with flags and banners,

Hundreds of markets flow beside, waiting for prosperity,

Repeated layers of pearl lamps, arranged like constellations,

Fragrant streets, brocade clothes, laughing beautiful women,

Buildings fly, gold and jade, heavenly splendor,

Cars run, thunderous at midnight,

Attire from all corners of the world, shared and admired today,

Hua Xin alone, sorrowfully shuts his heavy door.

···············

Modest wealth, food and drink comparable to princes and kings,

Mostly starting from humble beginnings,

Teams of carriages, connected like Zhuo and Zheng,

Southern neighbors, northern villages, millions of gold Zhangs,

At the banquet, boldly striking coral trees,

Competing in the next room, boasting amber halls,

Only Yang Xiong could wield ten thousand dances,

Holding his writing brush, chasing sheep in the pen.

···············

The racecourse opens, green grass aligned,

Enclosure circles, white fence low,

A gunshot, watching flying manes,

Four seats of people, shouting as if to breach a dike,

Sometimes together, sometimes apart, heart and mind urgent,

Looking ahead, suddenly behind, eyes lingering,

Champagne in hand, gold thousands,

Competing to thank guests, bowing to swift horses.

··············

Guests disperse, banquet songs, embroidered mats put away,

Purple robes, casually playing with gamblers,

High buildings, rotating, losing thousands of moves,

Separate pavilion, ball returns, winning a trick,

Bridge rushes, wind flies, cool night moon,

Hua Liu electric swift, blue sky autumn,

Now, gambling has many tricks,

Not comparable to the rustic, leisurely sentiment.

···············

Guest residence deeper, dance hall opens,

Plucking zithers, playing flutes, jade as the stage,

Fairies sitting, connecting barbarians and Chinese,

Loving couples, dividing lines, coming and going repeatedly,

Entering the cup, jade wine, spring fragrance rich,

Responding to the strings, silk sleeves, snow fluttering,

The ancient Wu Palace, used to have much merrymaking,

Not comparable to today's various beauties combined.

Announcement Seeking Supplements of This Newspaper

Clerk Correspondence

Swine Epilepsy 280

Editor Sir:

I am a clerk in a pharmacy, and I am nineteen years old this year. When I was seventeen years old, by the command of my parents and the words of a matchmaker, I was engaged to the daughter of XX. I originally wanted to marry her formally next year; however, unfortunately, something happened: she now has a terrible disease, and when it attacks, it is as if she is dead. I am very dissatisfied with this, and I am very worried. I am now asking the Sir for guidance. I want to break off the relationship with her. Her illness will make it impossible to maintain a family in the future, and it will hinder my future. Therefore, I am determined to break off with her. Is it possible to achieve my goal legally? Her illness is commonly called "swine epilepsy." She did not have this illness at first; it was only recently noticed. When I found out, I relayed the matter to the matchmaker and negotiated to break off the engagement. Unexpectedly, they refused and said that this was my misfortune and that I absolutely could not break off the engagement. I think marriage is a serious matter and should not be misunderstood. I am in this kind of environment, and I am very worried. What should I do? Editor Sir, do you have a good plan? Please do not hesitate to guide me! I wish you good health. Written by Yao Shangqing.

XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX

Editor's Note: Swine epilepsy is indeed an incurable disease; although we should pity those who suffer from it, we should not marry them. Because this can ruin our happiness and absolutely cannot reduce their suffering. Mr. Yao should insist on breaking off the engagement. The law stipulates that "if the other party has a serious incurable disease," the engagement can be dissolved. As for the fact that she contracted the disease after the engagement, it is also not a problem and can be applied. We must know that if she already had this disease before the engagement and did not explain it at the time of the engagement, Mr. Yao can now not only request the termination of the engagement but also demand compensation for damages!

Fiction

Time in a Dream (Nineteenth Installment) 281

— Qin Shouou

This almost made Wu Yi immediately dismiss his intention and leave, but then he thought that it was not easy to have such a high-ranking friend, so he should not offend him and ruin his future.

"Qianli,... Mister Zhao,..." Zhao Qianli had changed his title, and Wu Yi had to change his as well. "Director Zhao, I am very ashamed that I have not achieved anything yet. To be honest, this trip to Beijing to visit you is of course..."

"Of course, you want to find a job here!" The cunning Zhao Qianli had already anticipated Wu Yi's intention when he received his card. "Haha! We are old friends! If you are willing to help, there is no reason not to welcome you, but, but you studied education, and what is needed here is finance!"

"But, Director, I think if you can give me a job as a secretary, it doesn't seem necessary to know accounting; I probably can..." Wu Yi honestly and politely stated his needs.

"Secretary, that is of course very good. Unfortunately, ... unfortunately, ..." Zhao Qianli did not expect that he would actually open his mouth directly, so he tilted his head and pretended to be very difficult. "Unfortunately, we only have three here, the three old ones; I cannot change them for the time being, because...!"

Before he could finish speaking, a servant in a white bamboo cloth uniform suddenly pushed the door open and said:

"Director, Secretary Liu has arrived, especially to thank you for the appointment!"

"Wait a minute! Get out! I have a guest here!" This powerful refutation made even Director Zhao, who knew no shame, blush half of his old face, and he had to give the ignorant servant a fierce look.

The situation was already deadlocked. Zhao Qianli suddenly woke up and thought that Wu Yi was, after all, a terrible newspaper editor. For the sake of his own fame and fortune, he should not offend him too much, so he immediately changed his face.

"But we are old friends after all. You have traveled thousands of miles to come to me, how can I disappoint you too much? Then, ... then, ..." As he spoke, he picked up a salary schedule for employees from his desk and quickly flipped through it. "Then, I will appoint you as a tax collector! The monthly salary is one hundred and twenty yuan, but you don't have to go to work. You can go back to Shanghai, and I will remit the money to you every month..."

Originally, Wu Yi also knew that there was a set of flexible methods in the Chinese officialdom, such as supporting concubines and younger brothers-in-law, but he never expected that Zhao Qianli was also such a bastard who used state funds for personal gifts.

"Specialized talents, or accounting technical talents, that is, people with business experience, are very much needed..."

"Finance," "accounting," "specialized," "technical," these steel-hard special nouns almost scared Wu Yi. He had to turn his head and face to the left, not daring to look him directly in the eye. On the left was a huge bookshelf, filled with foreign books, three or four inches thick, with leather covers and gold letters. Nineteen were the great works of the world's major psychologists. Although Wu Yi had also studied psychology, at this time, he could not help but suspect that the psychology that Zhao Qianli studied in the United States was perhaps a special kind of psychology that could replace finance; otherwise, he believed that since Zhao Qianli himself was not a financial expert, no matter how absurd it was, he would not use these special nouns of "finance," "accounting," "specialized," and "technical" to embarrass others again.

Film Supplement

The Autumn Waves of Movie Stars 282

— Zhong Qin

A person's personality and behavior can be guessed from their eyes, right into their heart. If they have a kind personality, their eyes will always have a kind and gentle expression. If they have a vicious personality, their eyes will reveal a fierce light. At the same time, a woman's bright eyes can fully express beauty. The so-called "a glance of autumn waves is enough to captivate the soul." If we examine the eyes of movie stars, we can find certain styles in their bright eyes, which is quite interesting. Joan Crawford is a famous big-eyed sister. Of course, there is no need to mention her eyes are large. Joan Crawford's big eyes, frankly speaking, slightly hinder the beauty of her face, but her big eyes are full of energy. She has achieved her energetic and lively style because of these big eyes. In "Grand Hotel" and "Rain", her brilliance lies in her two big eyes, which is undeniable.

In contrast to Joan Crawford is Norma Shearer. Norma Shearer's eyes are particularly small. Her pupils are large and often set high under her upper eyelids, so at a glance, you know she is a careful and restrained young lady, giving a sense of awe and respect. Her style is revealed in the middle without reservation.

Greta Garbo's eyes are very deep and sad. When she plays tragic and charming characters, she can give people a lot of sympathy. Her gentle autumn waves, like a pool of spring water, can make people intoxicated and immersed in them.

"It" Girl Clara Bow's eyes show full of heat, and have the taste of strong and unruly. The space between her upper eyelids and eyebrows is extremely close, which is a characteristic of strong and unruly.

Jeanette Loring's eyes show a lot of gentleness and pleasantness. Her style is petite and exquisite, infinitely lovely, all in the gentleness.

Marlene Dietrich's eyes are sharp and transparent, so her style tends to be mysterious and unpredictable, requiring speculation behind the scenes and finding the meaning beyond the words.

Tallulah Bankhead's eyes are flirtatious and moving, her style can be dazzling and soul-stirring, making people drunk.

Constance Bennett's eyes show a clumsy and strong attitude, so she always depicts the indomitable and strong style.

Having said a lot, there are still many that you can speculate on yourself. You can guess the inner heart from the eyes, and you will never guess wrong.

Film Review

Review of "Love on the Spot" 283

— Yan Nan

Yesterday I watched "Love on the Spot" at the Carlton Theatre, and I suddenly thought of "Of Human Bondage" which I saw two months ago. Indeed, this "Love on the Spot" is adapted from a novel, but it has the same effect as "Of Human Bondage", and there are some similarities in the story and skills.

The story is like this: In a hotel, there lives a young man who is a pickpocket with extraordinary skills. After three thefts, the detective suspected him, but could not find any evidence. At that time, another girl and her father also lived in this hotel. The father and daughter are both swindlers wearing gentleman masks. But the girl fell in love with the young man, and she frankly stated that she would change her ways in the future. The young man was also moved, returned all the stolen goods, and the two walked together on the right path.

The actors are very unfamiliar to us. The young man who plays the thief is Rickad Dolman, and he shows all the attitudes of British youth. His natural facial expressions, singing and dancing, are very pleasing. Maybe it can be considered that he has the charm of viewing Fullei? His liveliness and humor make people extremely satisfied. Especially he is extremely suitable for the role in the play. The girl is played by Rosemary Ames, which is generally good. She is very beautiful, but her expressions are a little worse. The songs she sings are very nice. Her father is played by Anbrey Mather, who specializes in making jokes, which can make people laugh.

The old woman who was stolen, Helen Ferrers, occupies an extremely important position in the supporting roles. Her performance vividly describes the general arrogant aristocratic lady, which is very relevant. As for the child John Singer, he is very promising, and in this film, he has shown great acting talent.

There is not too much dialogue. If you can understand every sentence, then you can find countless humorous materials to make you laugh.

As for the director, he can only be regarded as above average. The angle and position of the photography are good. The lighting is also worth watching. From the costumes and scenery, you can tell that it is a British film, with a noble continental color in the beauty. Of course, the attitude of each actor is also related. The editing is all good. As for the big swimming that is used to attract, the girls in the swimming pool, and the filming of the camera, although they copied the old tricks of the stage dance troupe, they still do not lose their novelty, but it is a pity that it is too short and there are too few changes. All four songs are "Jazz Songs", which can be said to be a "good" word.

In all song and dance films, the soundtrack is often supposed to be very good. But the music of this film is very ordinary and does not inspire people's excitement.

The plot is very superficial, but it still has some satirical and teasing meaning. (For example, searching Aixi from the head of a sixty-year-old man)

In short, this film can give you pleasure and make you laugh. Although, it cannot call you to remember it forever.

Big Nose Mockery 284

— Bing

In Hollywood, even children know that when you say Mr. Big Nose, you are referring to Jimmy Durante, whose fame entirely comes from his nose. Since he has such an enviable big nose, many people have created a song to mock him, which roughly means:

The face powder of the girls in Los Angeles can be smelled on the top of Mount Piferlei; in the summer, it can really be used as a sunshade, so that three children can hide underneath to enjoy the cool; but the wind inside is too hot, it is better to go to the beach to enjoy the cool!

Ah! It's hateful why I don't also have such a thing, so I can make big money in Hollywood?

This is a Chinese actress who grew up in Hollywood. Her name is Xia Li Malisha. She was introduced in Si Yingjun's "A Stateless Woman" in this publication on March 6.

Quick News Roundup 285

— Jie

The Tianyi Company's new film "Vitality" is now more than halfway through filming, starring Chen Yumei and Yuan Meiyun. The previous rumor included Hu Shan, but she has long since been replaced.

The Nanyang Company's production "Platinum Dragon" is adapted from a Cantonese opera, so two-thirds of the dialogue is in Cantonese. The rest is a mix of Shanghainese and Mandarin. Apart from the three actors who are from Nanyang Company, the rest of the cast and crew are entirely from Tianyi Company, it is said.

Since Gai Jiaotian stopped performing at the Qitian Stage, he has been actively engaged in the film industry, inviting Peking opera celebrities such as Yuan Yuelou to participate. The originally planned name was "Gai Jiaotian Film Company," but now, adopting a shareholder system, it has been changed to "Qiankun Film Company." However, it is being conducted in secret, so very few people know about it.

Recently, the various studios of the Lianhua Company have been actively producing various short films, mostly of the news and slapstick variety. Five sets have already been filmed and will be released soon. This is likely a good sign for the future of domestic films, it is said.

Ma Xuwibang, famous for his makeup artistry, was once hailed as the "Thousand-Faced Man of the Orient" five years ago. There are rumors that he may join Tianyi Company, but negotiations have not yet been finalized.

The Strange State of Cinemas 286

— Zhao Peng

Cinemas are places of refined entertainment, and going to the cinema is about appreciating the merits of performances on the screen. However, some patrons' purpose is not to watch the performances on the screen, but to admire the faces and clothing of the beautiful women in the theater.

Many women often dress flamboyantly, douse themselves in perfume, and deliberately flaunt their charms in the cinema, hoping to attract the attention of the opposite sex, exchanging glances with men, acting out love stories as if they were on the screen. Has the refined cinema become a public matchmaking agency for romance? The music in many cinemas is also full of tricks, with the music played having nothing to do with the meaning of the film. Most careless patrons are content as long as the music continues uninterrupted. If it stops even for a moment, they will start making a fuss. When the music is playing, they often stomp their feet incessantly, causing headaches.

"Wu Song" to Shoot on Location in Suzhou 287

— Songfu

Gai Jiaotian Film Company's first film, "Wu Song," has been in preparation for a long time. Gai Jiaotian initially wanted to shoot the exterior scenes in Hangzhou. However, because he has other business in Suzhou recently and cannot get away, he has decided to shoot in Suzhou. Filming is expected to be completed in about a month, it is said.

Odds and Ends 288

— Zhou Jingzhi

Zhang Huichong's "Tears of Blood in Rehe," filmed at great risk in the Northeast, has been fully edited. It was screened in Beijing and received a good reception. It is planned to be released at the Beijing Grand Theatre soon, it is said. Star Company's change of style, "Rouge Market," is being rushed to completion and will be released at the Carlton soon.

Amidst the clamor for "National Salvation Through Aviation," the film industry is unwilling to be left behind. Lianhua Company is preparing to conduct a fundraising performance. The script and cast for this performance include major stars such as Jin Yan, Ruan Lingyu, Zheng Junli, and Chen Yanyan. At the same time, all Lianhua's basic staff will be present. It is also said that the tentative title of the play is "Resistance," written by Jin Yan.

Movie Novel "State Fair" (Part 4) 289

— Huijun

"I'm sorry, I thought you had fainted and that's why I held you!" he said, and Maggie's face turned red. "I have never fainted," she retorted.

The boy seemed to be developing an affection for her. "Women are all timid, I bet you're afraid of mice too!" he teased.

"I'm afraid of nothing!" An angry flame flashed in her eyes.

"Another ride?" the boy suggested, as the roller coaster stopped at the station.

"Never again!" she gasped, but seeing his mocking expression, she hesitated, forgetting that the car was about to leave.

Like lightning, the roller coaster sped along the track again, his arm around her again, and she, unable to resist, closed her eyes, leaning powderly against his shoulder.

"Having fun?" he asked. Maggie nodded shyly. As he helped her out of the car and through the tunnel to the ground,

"What's your name?" He told her his name was! No, don't tell me, let me guess. Helen... no! Patty... no! Maggie... that's it! Maggie." She learned that his heart's desire was called Pantuo, and that his profession was a journalist. They talked, laughed, went to drink soda, and went on the Ferris wheel together. Maggie was so happy. Ah, the State Fair is so interesting she's glad she came! She felt that tonight was the most real and lovely night of her life. But now it's over again quickly over! But, looking at Pantuo's earnest, loving attitude, she knew there was still tomorrow!

Tonight, Huien also felt a mysterious freshness. He stood near the large platform, waiting, knowing that this was the place for aerial performances. Suddenly, the drums thumped loudly, and the host announced; "Please watch Ms. Hogan's performance she is the world's number one triple hanging artist!" Before Huien's skeptical eyes, a slender figure, wearing a tight-fitting costume, ran out, bowed, and climbed the ropes. Ah, it was Emily!

His mouth was half-open, barely daring to breathe, watching until the end of the performance. She came down from the ropes, seemingly looking for him among the gathered audience, and then, in his direction, threw a blown kiss. A long sigh came from his lips. Finally, he decided to walk towards the backstage door with the sign "No Admittance." There, he moistened his dry lips, waiting until Emily, in plain clothes, came out happily to greet him.
